pa rnams dar bas/ shes pa skyo bar byung / nged khu dbon gnyis kyis/ mi 'di go chod dam/ 'di sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la sems sam snyam pa rnams la/ gser srang brgya
skor res ma mtha' byas/ jo bo gdan 'dren du btang pa yin na'ang / bstan pa'i bya ba ches pas gdan ma 'drongs des blo ma sad par/ lha chen po des bal yul gyi mtha' 'khob tu/
jo bo spyan 'dren pa'i gser 'tshol du byon pas/ gar log gi rgyal pos/ chos kyi rgyal po paNDi ta gdan 'dren pa'i gser 'tshol ba rig nas/ 'di'i pha mes rnams kyis sngon
yang sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dar bar byas/ 'dis kyang paNDi ta gdan 'dren bstan pa dar bar byed pas zungs la btson khang du chug zer nas mnar/ de bdag gis thos pas/ khu
bo bzlog tu phyin yang / gar log gi rgyal po tshan ches nas ma ldog yang dmag byas na bzlog par snang ste/ de'i bar du 'gro ba mang po'i srog 'chad pa dang / nga rang la
yang bar chad byung na jo bo spyan mi 'drongs par

gda' bas kho rang dang bstun/ kho na re/ 'o na paNDi ta gdan 'dren pa'i 'phro bshol/ nga'i bstan pa la zhugs/ yang na gser rgyal po rang dang mnyam pa khyer la shog de nas
btang gi zer bas/ gser la 'dam nas lus dang mnyam pas bslus kyang ma nyan/ de nas kho bo la/ da ngas dbu tsam cig brnyed pa dang bslur 'ong gis zhus pas/ bzhad cig mdzad
nas/ da des chog nga'i bsam pa la bod 'di chos khrims ma 'chos par shi na mi rung snyam pa yin te/ da na so yang rgas/ 'khor ba thogs med nas chos kyi phyir du lus btang
pa med/ da len chos phyir shi na legs pa yin pas/ sdig rgyal 'di la gser se ba gcig kyang ma ster/ gser thams cad rgya gar du khyer la/ da dung a ti sha gdan ci 'drongs gyis/
paNDi ta chen po'i snyan du yang / ngas khyod dang sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i phyir du lus srog gar log gi rgyal po ngan pa la byin yod pas/ tshe rabs thams cad du bdag
thugs rjes 'dzin pa dang / nga'i bsam pa'i gtso bo khyed bod du byon nas sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dar bar byed pa yin pas/ de kho na bzhin du mdzad par zhu/ skye ba 'di'i
'og rol tu khyed dang nges par mjal bar byin gyis brlabs tu gsol/ zhes nga 'phrin du mdzod cig de ltar lags pas nga blos thong la/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la soms shig
gsungs pa yin pas/ des na khu bo gar log gi rgyal pos med par byas pas gtam de rnams mgon po a ti sha'i snyan du thos/ nged bod mtha' 'khob kyi sems can ma rig pa rnams
kyi snying stobs de 'dra na/ khyed 'gro ba'i skyabs gnas thugs

rje can ji ltar song / zhes zhus shig 'di na gser srang bdun brgya yod pa bla ma'i phyag tu phul/ nged bod pre ta pu ri'i grong khyer lta bu na/ gser se ba re tsam la'ang rtsis
chen po yod la/ da 'dis bdag cag mi nor thams cad rdzogs nas yod kyi/ da lan jo bo bod la ma byon na/ khyed dam pa rnams kyi thugs rje yang de ltar bas pas/ nged kyang
bya ba ci bder spyad par bgyi'o/ /zhes/ khyed 'dul ba 'dzin pas lo rgyus 'di rnams/ jo bo la zhus pa'i tha ma 'byon du ma bzhed na'ang snyan du thebs pa mdzod/ gsungs
nas shums shing gsung byon te/ de'i tshe lha btsun pa mi chen po cig gis de ltar mdzad pas/ lo tsA bas kyang yin min gyi tshig zur tsam yang smra ma nus/ de'i stobs kyis
lus srog dang lam gyi dka' tshegs/ tshe 'di'i bde skyid gang la yang ma chags par/ dpon g.yog bdun gyis gser rnams khyer te/ rgya gar gyi lam du zhugs pa dang lha btsun pas
skyel thung mdzad de/ dge slong khyed kyis nged kyi bya ba byas/ /da lan dka' ba che na'ang phar byon la/ /'bad rtsol chen pos lus dang srog la brdos/ /'khor nas byas
shes bka' drin bzo bar bya/ /zhes gsungs nas/ phyi phyag mdzad nas gshegs/ slar yang jo bo thugs rje chen po la gsol ba 'debs kyi gshegs par zhu gsungs/ de nas bal po rdzong
la byon tsa na mi reng gcig dang 'phrad pas/ khyed yul sa thag ring por don chen po la 'gro bar snang ba 'di skad zer gyin song dang don grub nas 'ong gi dkon mchog gsum
la phyag 'tshal lo/ /kha ba can gyi rgyal khams su/ rgyal ba

thams cad kyi 'byung gnas/ dam pa'i chos 'phel bar gyur cig ces brjod cing song na lam du'ang nye zho mi 'byung zer/ khyed su lags byas pas/ rim gyis shes par 'gyur gyis zer/
de nas bal po'i mtha' 'khob tu sleb pa na/ a tsa ra la gnas g.yar bas snyug khang cig tu bsnyal/ khos gser yod par shes nas/ snyug khang la me spar te bsad nas gser 'khyer
bar 'dod pa na/ lo tsA ba dpon g.yog sa thag ring po la ngal zhing / tshad pas gdungs gnyid kyis myos pa'i sngas mgor/ mi reng dkar po cig snyug khang gi mthongs phye
nas byung ste/ ma nyal ma nyal myur du yar la longs/ /ma phebs da lta longs la lam du zhugs/ /nyal na rin chen srog dang 'bral ba yod/ /nga ni bod khams yongs kyi yi dam
yin/ /zhes gsungs pas/ thugs rje chen po la gsol ba btab nas bros/ nam langs pa dang / bal po'i rgyal phran cig bhi kra ma lar 'gro ba dang 'dzom ste/ de dang 'grogs nas
chu bo ganggA'i 'gram du slebs pa dang / rgyal po dbang che bas sngon du gru la song / der nyi ma phyis pas gser rnams bye ma'i 'og tu sbas te/ phyogs gzhan zhig tu nyal
ba na/ gnyan pa dkar po gcig gru la skya ba chal chal 'debs kyin byung / der lo tsA bas khyed su yin gar gshegs dris pas/ dpon g.yog 'khor bcas bsu ru 'ong ba yin/ /sems
can snying stobs chen pos 'dir 'ong tshe/ /'phags pa gru dang mnyan pa lta bu yis/ /'jigs pa'i dus su su bskyel ma byas na/ /sems can nyon mongs can gyis ji ltar 'grub/
/tshur zhugs

bdun brgya po rnams ma lus par/ /'bol le ka ma la ru sgrol bar bya/ /zhes zer ba dang / gser rnams bton te grur zhugs ma Ni bgrangs pas/ mnyan pa na re/ nged kha ba can gyi
thugs rje chen po de/ /ma Ni 'di ltar byed pa yin zer nas bgrangs byung tsa na/ yid 'dzin gyur pas/ the tshom du gyur te/ khyed su yin nam gsung zhig 'byon par zhu byas
pas/ gnyan pa na re/ tshe dang ldan pa snga 'grogs kyi dus su spobs pa ma myur/ gzhung 'grogs kyi dus su khrel gzhung ma chung / phyi 'grogs kyi dus su phyi thag ma thung
bya ba/ ma nus pa'i dus phan pa dang / dgos dus sleb pa bya ba/ yun du 'grogs pa la dgos pa yin/ rim gyis shes par 'gyur gsungs de ma thag gru sgrol ba dang / da nam phyed
du song / dug sbrul dang / chom rkun gyi 'jigs pa 'ong bas/ do nub bi kra ma la'i sgo spe 'og tu nyol gsungs nas gzhan du song / der sleb pa na/ rgya brtson 'grus seng
ge sgo khang steng na bzhugs pas gsan te/ khyed rnams gang nas 'ong gsungs/ nged rnams mnga' ris stod nas yin zhus pas/ 'o na sgo ba byis pa cig yod de la khyed rang gi
nor rnams chol la der gzims gsungs/ de nas byis pa la gser rnams bcol bas/ blo gtad thub pa grogs kyi mchog bya ba yin/ /khyed rang rnams bag phebs par gzims zer/ nangs par
sgo phye ma thag byis pa gzhon nu cig gis bod kyi skad du/ khyed rnams gang nas byon/ lam la 'jigs pa mi 'dug gam zer bas/ nged mnga' ris nas 'ong / lam 'jam par byung
/

khyod su yin byas pas/ nga yang bod cig yin/ nged rang bod 'di kha mang la gting lhod/ gtam khams chen sbed mi shes/ bya ba gal chen gsang nas sgrub dgos pa yin/ rgya brtson
seng ge bod kyi spyi khang na yod der song zer nas/ kho yud kyis song / de nas srang ring po cig la phyin tsa na drang srong rgan po chu shing gi 'khar ba thogs pa cig
dang 'phrad pas/ de na re/ khyod gang nas 'ong / gang du 'gro/ don ci la 'ongs zer bas/ nged bod mnga' ris nas a ti sha spyan 'dren du 'ongs pa yin/ rgya brtson seng gi khang
pa gang na yod byas pas/ kho 'khar ba la rten nas phyir mig gcu ba cig byas/ da nangs kyi byis pa de bden/ bod kyi mi la ol mdud med pas/ srang nang gi mi 'khyams po
tshun la yin tshul sang nge 'chad pa/ khyod kyis kyang don 'grub tu re ba ang / da lan nga'i rtsar byas pas drag /da jo bo min pa gzhan gyi rtsar khar ma 'don/ rgya brtson
seng la zur tsam zer na'ang rigs/ sgo ngas bstan zer nas kho ga le song ba'i phyi la/ lo tsA bas mgyogs pos ma sleb/ kho bod kyi spyi khang sgor bsgugs 'dug pas/ lo tsA
ba ya mtshan zhing the tshom du gyur pa dang / kho na re/ bya ba chen po bsgrub pa la go lo mgyogs pa yin/ 'dod thag ma nye bar ri bo 'gas kyis 'dzegs/ khang pa 'di yin
zer/ nang du phyin pa na/ lo tsA ba rgya brtson seng rgya dpe tshan cig gzigs kyin 'dug pa la/ phyag rten gser mtshon byed re phul bas/ lo tsA bas khyed rnams don ci la
'ongs gsungs/ de la gong gi lo rgyus rnams zhib par zhus pas/ khong gi zhal nas da a ti sha gdan

'dren du yong skad ye ma zer/ slob gnyer la yong zer ba smros/ 'di na gnas brtan ratna a ka ra dbang che bas/ des tshor du ye mi btub/ da lta rang khong la gser srang phyed
phul la/ der bod nas 'ong paNDi ta ni spyan ma drongs da khyed kyis paNDi ta dang khyad med pa'i slob gnyer gcig thugs la 'dogs pa zhu zhes zhus/ de nas kyang ring ring
dang blo ma phebs par ma byed par/ slob gnyer gyis la sos gdol/ de nas 'o cag thabs mkhas pas jo bo la zhu ba byed pa yin gsungs/ de nas nag tsho lo tsA ba ci gsungs blta
ba'i ched du/ mgon po a ti sha cis kyang gdan ma 'drongs na/ de'i 'og nas gang che ba'i paN chen gcig gdan drangs na zhus pas/ lo tsA ba'i zhal nas/ de 'dra so sgor ma 'don/
de yin na na ning nas paN chen zhig la cig che ba nyi shu tsam gdan drangs na'ang 'drongs te/ 'o skol bod kyi sems can gyi spyod gshis rgyus med dam a ti sha ma gtogs
sus kyang bod kyi sems can mi thul bas/ da dung a ti sha rang gdan ci 'drongs byed dgos gsungs/ gzhan paNDi ta ci 'dra yod zhus pas/ 'di ltar shanti pa/ nA ro pa/ Dombhi
pa/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ a wa dhu ti pa/ byang chub bzang po/ rin chen bzang po/ rin chen rdo rje/ lha'i blo gros/ ngag dbang grags pa/ nag po pa/ dze ta ri dgra las
rnam par rgyal ba/ rol pa'i rdo rje/ sa 'gebs pa'i zhabs/ ye shes gsang ba/ chos kyi bshes gnyen/ tshul khrims dbang po la sogs pa paNDi ta bsam gyis mi khyab pa lnga bcu
rtsa gnyis

tsam yod kyang / thams cad rang sa rang sa na ngo mtshar che mod/ 'o skol bod la mgon po a ti sha min pas phan pa med gsungs/ 'o na a ti sha ston par zhu dang zhus pas/ khyod
rang nangs par dge 'dun gyi kun dga' ra bar dge 'dun stong phrag mang po 'ong gi de'i nang na lhang nge / lham me ba/ sku blta bas chog mi shes pa/ gral gang du bzhugs
kyang mdzes pa zhig yod kyi/ de a ti sha yin pas/ de la nyin mtshan du gsol ba thob gsungs/ de nas rgya brtson seng dpon slob gnyis kyis gnas brtan ratna a ka ra'i drung
du phyin/ phyag byas gser srang phyed phul te rgyas bslabs pa bzhin nag tshos zhus pas/ gnas brtan gyi zhal nas/ shin tu legs/ tshe dang ldan pa 'di ltar yin/ nged 'dir
mi la tsag pa min te/ 'di na a ti sha med na rgya gar sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i 'byung gnas yin pas/ 'di nyams na sems can spyi'i bde skyid nyams 'gro ba yin mod/ de'i rgyu
mtshan/ rgya gar gyi chos srol dang / gtsug lag khang thams cad kyi lde mig a ti sha'i phyag na yod pa yin/ de min na nged kyang bod kyi sems can la sems brtse zhing
/ khyad par du bod kyi chos rgyal de'i mi nor mang po zad pas ngo gnong ste/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la bsam pa yin na brtson 'grus drag pos sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa rab
'byams la slob gnyer gyis ngas kyang phyis su ci 'gro byed/ khyed bod rgya gar ba la 'di ltar sems pa ngo mtshar che/ zhes gsungs/ de nas gnas brtan gyis khrid de dge 'dun
gyi gdugs tshod gral du phyin a ti sha gral gyi dbu la bzhugs

sam snyam pa la/ shanti pa bzhugs 'dug pa/ 'di a ti sha lags sam byas pas/ tshe dang ldan pa 'di ni/ shanti pa zhes pa mkhas grub chen po a ti sha'i yang bla ma de lags mod
zer/ de ltar rje btsun nA ro pa la sogs pa gral gyi dbu la 'dug pa la re re bzhin 'di a ti sha yin nam/ zhes dris pas/ 'di nA ro pa zhes pa ding sang 'gran zla dang bral
ba a ti sha'i yang bla ma yin zer/ gzhan du a ti sha ma mthong pas yid zhum pa na/ dus re zhig bi kra ma la'i rgyal po khri bshams pa'i steng na 'dug pa paNDi ta che chung
gang la'ang lang ba mi byed par snang ba la/ a ti sha sku gzi brjid che zhing zhal 'dzum chags pa/ cam por gshegs pa cig nang du byon pa dang / rgyal po des khri las langs
pas/ paNDi ta dang dge 'dun thams cad kyis ldang ba byas/ gral stod du bzhugs pa mthong bas/ 'di a ti sha yin nam dris pas ci zer/ 'di dpa' bo bzhad pa'i rdo rje zhes
pa gnas nges med du byon pa'i paNDi ta gcig yin zer/ 'di la yon tan ji tsam yod byas pas/ 'di'i yon tan gyi tshod nged kyis mi lon zer nas/ a ti sha yin pa la 'chad ma
nyan/ de nas nag tshos gtsug lag khang gi sgo drung du/ shes rab snying po'i med kyi thad du/ gzugs ha/ tshor ba ha byas pas/ paNDi ta gzhan rnams cang mi gsung ba la/ jo
bo byon zhal 'dzum mdzad de/ tshe dang ldan pa de phal skad yin/ gzugs a/ tshor ba a zer ba yin gsungs/ nangs par de ltar bton pas/ jo bo'i zhal nas/ de yang gyong po cig
yong par snang / spyan ras gzigs kyi gsung yin

gzugs med tshor ba med gyis gsungs pas/ lhag par dad de rjes su 'brangs pa na/ sprang po'i tshogs la zan gnang ba mthong bas/ byis pa cig gi skal ba chad de phyi la brgyug
cing / a ti sha/ bha la ho/ bha ta 'on/ zhes pa thos pas/ a ti sha yin nges snyam nas yus kyis dngangs te phyi la phyin pas/ der bzhugs te/ tshe dang ldan pa bden/ mchi ma
ma 'byin/ khyed bod ngas da dung blos btang ba med kyis/ dkon mchog la gsol ba thob gsungs/ de nas lan gcig rgya'i gzim khang du tshul khrims rgyal bas/ jo bo spyan drangs
nas gser srang bdun brgya maNDal dang bcas pa phul/ jo bo spyan 'dren pa la bod kyi mi nor song ba dang / chos rgyal khu dbon gyis khyed kyi phyogs su dka' ba spyad lugs/
bod na chos log yod tshul la sogs pa lha btsun pas zhu ba bskur ba rnams rgya brtson 'grus seng ges rgyas par snyan du gsol te/ da yang tshe dang ldan pa 'di jo bo spyan
'dren pa la btang bar 'dug pas/ mgon po nged gnyis kyis ji tsam pa'i dka' ba cig spyad kyang / 'dod pa'i don ma grub pa nged bod kyi sems can rnams snying mi rje'am/
lhag par yang gung thang pa 'di rab tu byung nas sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la thos bsam ma gtogs/ mi 'grub pa'i bya ba ma babs/ da lan cis kyang 'byon par mdzad du gsol zhus
pas/ jo bo'i zhal nas/ khyed lo tsA ba rnams shin tu bden/ bod kyi chos rgyal de'i mi nor mang po song bas ngo gnong / kho bo snying rje chung pa min kyang bstan pa'i
bya ba ches/ gtsug lag khang brgya rtsa brgyad kyi lde mig dang chos 'phro

yang mang po yod na yang rgas pas thon par dka' mod/ 'on kyang bod kyi chos rgyal khu dbon dang / lo tsA ba rnams kyi dka' spyad chud ma zos pa zhig bya yis/ re zhig gser rnams
tshags mdzod/ nged 'bod du 'ong skad ma zer/ lo tsA mkhas par slobs gsungs/ de'i nub mo jo bos rje btsun ma sgrol ma la maNDal phul te/ bod du phyin na sangs rgyas kyi
bstan pa la phan nam/ rgyal po byang chub sems dpa'i thugs dgongs rdzogs sam/ lus srog gi bar chad du mi 'gyur ram/ zhes zhus pas/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la phan zhing
/ rgyal po'i thugs dgongs rdzogs/ khyad par u pa si ka gcig la brten nas 'gro ba mang po la phan pas/ the tshom med par bod du bzhud/ ces lung bstan/ de nas jo bo'i zhal
nas rdo rje gdan du ldeng gsungs pas/ der phyin pa na byis pa gzhon nu dar dkar gyi gos gyon pa/ shel gyi mda' gzhu thogs pa zhig byung ste phyag 'tshal zhing da mgon
po bod du byon par zhu/ bod kyi tshe dang ldan pa 'di kun snying rje mod zer te song / jo bo la bod skad smra ba'i byis pa de su yin zhus pas/ nangs par rdo rje gdan gyi

gi byis pa de dang / bu mo sngo ljang ma gcig

kyang ma rgyal lta bur ston/ /rgyal ba'i mdzad pa mthar phyin 'gro ba'i mgon/ /rgyal ba yab sras gnyis la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zer/ byis pa na re/ gang du rgyal ba'i rnam
thar skyong ba na/ /bu mo khyod kyang bdag gi khyim 'ong zhing / /bu dang longs spyod dpal 'byor spel ba dang / /dga' bar 'grogs shing bar chad bsal 'tshal lo/ /he he/
da jo bo yang bod du 'byon ran zer nas khong gnyis gzhan du song / sprul pa zhig yin par shes nas/ jo bo la/ nged bod nas 'phags nas phan thogs kyi sprul pa zam ma chad pa

rin po che 'phrul gyi me

thams cad khyod kyi sras su 'gyur/ /gangs can rgyud der bstan pa dar bar byed/ /der song chos kyi bya ba 'di ltar mdzod/ /rdo rje theg pa nang du dar bar mdzod/ /gzhung lugs

nas/ /'jig rten sgron me bod du spyan drangs te/ /thams cad chos la 'god pa ngo mtshar che/ /bdag gis bskyed pa'i bu 'di rje la 'bul/ /bsam pa bzang po gser dang 'dra
ba 'di/ /chos rgyal bod du chos grwa 'dzugs pa la/ /gser srang sum brgya re zhig 'degs su 'bul/ /slad ma sangs rgyas bstan pa dar ba dang / /a ti sha yang phyogs 'dir yun
ring zhing / /bdag kyang 'phreng bas yun du 'grogs par zhu/ /zhes zhus te/ rgyal po paNDi ta gsum dang bcas pa bal por byon/ de nas a ti sha dpon slob lha btsun pas dbu
bgyis/ bsu ba'i rta pa dgu brgya'i 'khor dang / rnga dang rnga bo che dang / sil sbug dang / dkar dung dang / rag dung la lo paN spyan 'dren gyi rgyud bya bar grags shing
/ de la sogs pa rol mo'i tshogs dang bcas te rgyal po'i pho brang du spyan drangs bsnyen bkur te/ bod 'dir chos zab zab po las kyang / thog mar las rgyu 'bras la rten pa'i
chos kyis skyong bar zhu zhus pas/ jo bo'i zhal nas/ chos kyi gnad go ba'i gtam yin/ nan ltar zab pa las rgyu 'bras kho na yin/ yi dam gyi lha zhal mthong ba bas/ las
rgyu 'bras la yid ches na de nyid mchog tu gyur pa yin te/ gshin rje gshed kyi rnal 'byor pa dang / bi kra ma'i gnas brtan gyi lo rgyus gsungs nas/ de ltar mdzad pas mnga'
ris su paNDi ta

las rgyu 'bras par grags te/ kho bo'i ming tsam gyis kyang bstan pa la phan par byas gsungs nas mnyes/ de'i dus bod dbus gtsang gi mkhas pa phal che ba der tshogs te/ lta ba'i
gnad la sogs pa bstan pa rin po che las brtsams pa'i dri ba mang du zhus pas/ rang rang gi the tshom gyi dra ba chod par mdzad do/ /de nas lo tsa ba nag tshos/ da ni
jo bo bod du lo gcig las mi bzhugs pa'i chad so yod pas/ chos zhu ba rnams zhus shig ces lha btsun pa sogs la bskul bas/ jo bo la lha btsun pas gser srang sum brgya'i me
tog dang bcas te/ bod kyi yul 'dir theg pa chen po'i lam la log par rtog pa'i gang zag dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis ma zin pa dag phan tshun rtsod cing / rang rang gi rtog ges
zab pa dang rgya che ba'i don la spyod pa la rtsod cing / so sor mi mthun pa dag mchis pas/ de dag gi the tshom bsal du gsol/ zhes pa dang / gzhan yang theg pa thun mong
pa'i dri ba gnyis/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i dri ba gnyis/ gsang sngags la dri ba gsum la sogs pa mang du zhus nas/ byams pa dang / klu sgrub nas brgyud pa'i gdams ngag bla
ma nyid kyis thugs nyams su bzhes pa/ tshig nyung la don rgyas pa zhig mdzad par zhu zhus pas mdo sngags gnyis ka'i gnad bsdus nas ston pas/ brjod bya yongs su rdzogs pa
dang / sems 'dul ba'i rim pa gtso bor mdzad pa lag tu blang bde ba dang / shing rta chen po gnyis kyi lugs la mkhas pa'i bla ma gnyis kyi gdams pas brgyan pa lugs gzhan
las khyad par du 'phags pa/

byang chub lam gyi sgron me rtsa 'grel mdzad/ yang lha btsun pas/ rgyud gsang ba 'dus pa/ man ngag ye shes zhabs lugs dang / gtso bo spyan ras gzigs kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs
zhus pas/ gsang 'dus 'jig rten dbang phyug lha bcu dgu'i sgrub thabs mdzad de gnang ngo / /de'i tshe lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos/ rgyal pos spyan drangs lugs/ dka'
spyad du ma'i mthar spyan 'drongs tshul dang / paNDi ta'i yon tan gyi khyad par mtha' yas pa/ sngar nas kyang rang phyogs su byon tshul rnams gsan pas/ dus ding sang nga
las yon tan che ba med dam/ paNDi ta byon kyang zhu rgyu tsam ma mchis/ lhag par yang paNDi ta de 'dul khrims dang mdo sde la rtsal du 'don pa gcig 'dug zer/ de'i rigs la
theg pa chen po gsang sngags kyi lugs 'byung ba shin tu dka' la gang zag bzang po zhig yin par shes/ rmi ltas la sogs pa'ang bzang / cung zad cig bsus nas bsnyen bkur ba
bab snyam du sems pa'i/ de nub rmi lam na mi reng dkar po zhig byung nas/ kho bo sems can gyi don la byas yus che/ 'on kyang rgyal ba spyan 'dren pa la dka' spyad du ma
byas/ da dung mi shes pa yang zhu rgyu mang po mchis/ lo tsA ba thos rtags zhi zhing dul ba bya ba yin/ rgya bod kyi lo paN thams cad kyi yon tan dril kyang paNDi ta'i gzhung
gi yon tan mi rdzogs/ bod 'di kun man ngag gi sna rtses 'dul ba yin/ man ngag thams cad bod kyis mi lon zer nas gtam dri long med par yal nas song / lo tsA ba gnyid

sad pa dang / paNDi ta de snying rje che ba zhig yod par 'dug sna la thugs rje chen po 'ong ba de bzang snyam/ de nas nangs par thag ring po nas bsus te/ sku'i spyod pa la
bltas pas chog mi shes/ rim gyis rang gi khang par spyan drangs nas bsnyen bkur bar bzhed pa la/ paNDi ta dang / khong rang stan mnyam pa tsam bshams/ de nas paNDi ta nang
du byon pa dang / lha khang 'og na theg pa thun mong gi lha bod lugs su bzhengs pa yod pa la phyag la sogs pa saMskr-i ta'i skad kyis yan lag bdun pa mdzad de/ lha re la
bstod pa tshig bzhi pa re mdzad cing 'dug de bzhin du bar khang na theg pa chen po'i lha sku mang po yod pa dang / gsum thog na gsang sngags bla med kyi lha sku mang po
yod pa la'ang yan lag bdun pa phul nas/ lha re re la rang rang gi rgyud dang mthun pa'i bstod pa tshigs su bcad pa tshig bzhi pa re mdzad/ der lo tsA bas saMskr-i ta'i skad
snyan po de thos pas snyan ngag phul du phyin pa 'dug pa dang / sngar ma gzigs pa'i lha ris rnams la'ang bstod pa mdzad pas/ theg pa chen po la'ang de 'dra na/ dang tshugs
nye ba 'khor yin nam snyam pa la brten nas/ rang gi stan la 'brid thebs gsum byas/ mthar stan med pa tsam du nga rgyal skyungs/ de nas bsnyen bkur te lo tsA bas/ rgya
gar gyi lo rgyus mang po dris pas/ sgro bskur med pa tshar ba lan du byung / de nas yon tan gang la mkhas zhus pas/ khyed thun mong pa la zer ram/ thun mong ma yin pa
la zer gsungs/ lo tsA bas thun mong ba la shin tu mkhas/ thun mong ma yin la 'dri ba yin nam gsung bar go nas/ thun mong

ma yin pa la lags mod zhus pas/ kho bo 'di dang 'di la'ang mkhas gsungs nas/ lo tsA bas rna bar ma thos pa'ang mang po bton nas byung / der lo tsA ba'i nga rgyal thams cad
zhi/ de nas paNDi ta'i zhal nas/ 'du bla/ mdo sde/ mngon pa/ gsang sngags la sogs pa du ma las brtsams te/ 'di shes sam 'di shes sam zhes dris pas/ kho bo de la'ang mkhas
zer ba min pa ma byung / paNDi ta de la shin tu mnyes nas khyed lta bu yod pa la kho bo bod du 'ong mi 'tshal ba 'dug pa la zhes pa'ang gsungs/ yang lo tsA ba de dag thams
cad gdan thog gcig tu hril nas nyams su len pa ji ltar byed gsungs pas/ lo tsA ba na re/ theg pa ma 'dres so sor gsal/ /bya ba khyed la ma 'dres par/ /rang sar nyams su
len lags mod/ /zhus pas/ jo bo'i zhal nas/ lo tsA ba ngan par thal/ bod la kho bo dgos par 'dug gsungs nas lan gzhan mi smra bar bzhugs/ de'i nub mo lo tsA bas nam thun
gsum du bgos nas/ gnas gsum du rim gyis theg pa'i mtho dman dang bstun te bsgoms pas/ khong gi spyod pa thams cad paNDi tas mkhyen nas/ nangs par lo tsA ba tsab ta tsob
ta mang pos ci bgyi/ gang zag dam pa rdo rje'i gdan non dgos pa yin gsungs/ der lo tsA bas/ theg pa'i nyams su len lugs zhus pas/ lo tsA ba/ des mi 'ong gsungs/ 'o na khyed
rang ji ltar mdzad lags zhus pas/ ci zer/

gnas gar sdod/ grogs su dang 'grogs/ spyod lam ci byed kyang 'dul khrims la gzhi byas la/ sems can thams cad ma yin pas der bsgom dgos/ ma ltar dag snang sbyongs/ lha skye
med yin pas der sgoms/ 'dril ma shes na snying po mi lon zhes gsungs nas/ 'di skad du/ khrims ni yon tan kun gyi gzhir/ /rang gi ston pas legs par gsungs/ /snying rje chen
po dang 'brel ba'i/ /byang chub sems ni mchog tu bsngags/ /bzang rtog mtshan mas ma bcings pa'i/ /bskyed rdzogs zung 'brel nges 'tshang rgya/ /skyes bu chung dang cher
gyur pa'i/ /bya ba 'di yin 'bring po la'ang / /mi rtag brtson pas bskul ba gces/ /rang dga' spangs nas rgyal ba'i bka'/ /rgyas par 'byed pa mkhas pa yin/ /snying por bsdus
nas nyams len pa'i/ /skyes bu de ni bzang por grags/ /las 'bras khyad du mi gsod pa'i/ /bag yod can de btsun par bzhed/ /kun shes gcig sdug mkhas pa'i skyon/ /lag len mi
byed 'chal ba yin/ /blang dor mi byed btsun po'i gsog /shes par mdzod cig rin chen bzang / /thugs rje chen pos bskul bar zad/ /ces gsungs/ lo tsA bas dam par shes nas/
lha yi lhar gyur paNDi ta/ /rnam dag sku mchog khrims kyis spras/ /don gnyis 'byor pa'i nor gyis phyug /grol nas 'dren par kho bos 'tshal/ /kho bo'i lung rigs sgron me yis/
/sbas pa khyod kyi yon tan mthong / /sngon chad tshig dang 'gal na yang / /da ni khyod bzhin nyams

su len/ /zhes bstod do/ /gzhan yang mdo sngags kyi chos rang rang gi skal ba dang 'tshams par gnang ste/ bod log par lta ba lung rigs kyis tshar bcad/ the tshom za ba spang
blang gi mig phye nas bstan pa ches gsal bar mdzad do/ /de ltar na jo bo chen pos chos kyi rgyal po lha btsun pa sogs kyi thugs dgongs rdzogs par mdzad nas/ bal po'i rgyal
po paNDi ta dang bcas pas gtsug lag khang bzhengs tshar ba'i zhu ba byung ste 'byon du nye ba na/ jo bo chen po dgung lo re gcig bzhes pa'i dus/ bla ma dang yi dam gyis
lung bstan pa'i bshes gnyen ston pa rang lo so dgu bzhes pa/ dang por yang gling gser gyi lha khang du mjal nas byin gyis brlabs pa'i tshul ston pa'i rnam thar gyi skabs
su 'byung la/ de nas bshes gnyen ston pa dang / lha btsun pas/ jo bo rgya gar du 'byon du ma ster/ dbus kyi rgyal khams su bsu ba gnad la dgar ba'i spring yig tshigs su
bcad pa bcu dgu pa btang / bod ston rnams la slob ring la thabs du mas jo bo'i thugs dang bsrings te/ rgya dpe rten gsum la sogs pa'i gzhi thams cad bal por ma bkur/ de'i
dus jo bo'i phyag phyir gung thang pa/ sa'i sa ka u pA si ka e la bha ri la sogs pa dpon slob nyi shus bal por byon nas/ mu stegs bcings pa'i mchod rten nag po bzhi mdzad/
u pA si kas/ bkra shis pa'i mchod rten dkar chen zhes pa che ba gcig bzhengs/ gung thang pas/ jo bo yab sras zhal sprod kyi ras bris che ba gcig u pA si kas/ jo bo'i
sku la lha btsun pa dang /

gung thang pa ldem du byas pa gyang ris la bkod de rab gnas la sogs pa zhag nyi shu rtsa gnyis la tshar bar mdzad do/ /de nas jo bo rgya gar du 'byon par bzhed kyang / u pA
sa ka dang / bod kyi bsod nams kyi mthus/ slar yang mang yul du byon nas/ lha khang keng ru bya ba bzhengs/ de nas lha btsun pas dbus su spyan drangs te las stod du phebs/
bod ston rnams kyang der byon/ gtsang gi sa cha rnams su bod kyi rdo rje gdan dpal sa skya dang / snar thang la sogs pa lung bstan mang du mdzad de/ lo phyed bzhugs/ de
nas bsam yas/ thang po che/ lha sa rnams su lha btsun bo dhi rA dza/ khu ston rngog legs shes rnams kyis rim gyis spyan drangs nas chos mang du gsungs/ gsang phu la sogs
pa lung bstan/ khyad par lha sar ka ba bum pa can gyi nye 'khor nas rgyal rabs ka bkol ma mkha' 'gros lung bstan nas bton/ de nas rngog byang chub 'byung gnas gyis yer
par spyan drangs/ dus der bka' gdams glegs bam gyi zhu lan phal che ba rngog gis zhus nas gnas der mdzad/ de nas dpang ston gyis snye thang du spyan drangs/ lo ngo dgu bzhugs
pa'i lo drug gi bar la 'gyur mang po dang / rgyud sgrub thabs/ man ngag sogs gang la gang 'dul gyi chos gsungs/ rin po che sna lnga'i me tog gi char babs/ lo gsum mam/
ngo bzhir mkha' 'gro'i dbus su rdo rje'i glu rnams gsungs/ de rnams su yang yi dam dpag tu med pa'i zhal gzigs pa sogs rgyas par lam yig tu gsal lo/ /mdor na

gangs ri'i khrod du bstan pa snga dar la mkhan chen zhi ba 'tsho/ slob dpon padma sambha ba/ slob dpon ka ma shi la rnams bka' drin ches shin tu che la/ bstan pa phyi dar la/
lta spyod log par smra ba 'ga' zhig shing rta chen po'i gzhung rnams la nyams len gyi gnad med pa'i bshad chos su bsam zhing / nyams len snying po'i don ston pa'i man
ngag zur du yod par 'dod pas/ bshad pa dang sgrub pa'i chos don tha dad du 'dzin pa dang / sdom pa gsum 'gal bar bsams nas tshul khrims kyi bslab pa khyad du gsod pa dang
/ lam phyogs re bas thar pa thob par 'dod pa rnams 'gog pa la/ dpal ldan a ti sha nyid kha ba can pa thams cad la bka' drin che ba yin te/ rgyal ba'i gsung rab thams cad
kyi gnad bsdus pa/ shing rta chen po klu sgrub dang / thogs med gnyis kyi lam srol/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i sar 'gro ba'i skye bo mchog gi chos lugs/ skyes bu gsum
gyi nyams su blang ba'i rim pa ma tshang ba med par bsdus pa byang chub lam gyi sgron me'i sgo nas skal ba dang ldan pa rnams rim gyis sangs rgyas kyi sar khrid pa'i lam
ma nor ba gsal bar mdzad pas bka' drin che ba yin no/ /de yang spyir rgyal ba'i lung gi bstan pa thams cad sde snod gsum du 'du bas/ rtogs pa'i bstan pa yang bslab pa gsum
du 'du la/ tshul khrims kyi bslab pa ni/ ting nge 'dzin gyi bslab pa sogs yon tan thams cad kyi rten du gsungs shing / ting nge 'dzin dang shes rab kyi bslab pa ni/ byang
chub mchog

tu sems bskyed nas/ pha rol tu phyin pa drug sogs la gtso bor slob pa byang chub sems dpa'i lam dngos yin zhing / rdo rje theg pa nyams su len pa rnams kyis kyang dbang bskur
rnam dag thob nas dam tshig dang sdom pa bsrung ba/ bskyed rdzogs nyams su len pa rnams thabs kyi cha nas khyad che yang / 'dul lugs kyi dbang du byas na bslab pa gsum
du ma 'dus pa med pas/ des na jo bo chen po 'dis bstan pa thams cad 'gal med du gsal bar mdzad do/ /de lta bu'i bla ma yon tan rgya mtsho lta bu mnga' ba de'i rnam thar/
sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yul du gyur pa/ so so skye bo blo dman pa dag gi yul ma yin zhing / yi ge nyung ngu dag gis kyang rtogs par dka' la/ mthong
tshod tsam zhig bris na'ang mang pas/ 'dir ni zur tsam zhig brjod pa ste/ rnam thar rgyas pa don du gnyer na bla ma dang yi dam gyi lhas lung bstan pa dngos grub kyi 'od
zer dang / lam yig dam pa chos kyi 'byung gnas chung ba dang / chos kyi 'byung gnas che ba la gsang skor du grags pa rnams ston pas mdzad pa dang / de rnams dang phyogs
mthun pa lo tsA bas bstod pa brgyad cu pa dang / thun mong ma yin pa rnams bka' gdams glegs bam du skyes rabs nyi shu rtsa gnyis gsungs pa/ jo bo yab sras gnyis ka'i rnam
thar shugs la rgyas par 'byung ba rnams su shes par bya'o/ /de ltar skal ba dang ldan pa rnams la mdo sngags kyi gzhung gdams ngag ma lus pa bstan nas/ bstan pa'i srol
nub pa rnams gsar du btsugs/ srol

cung zad yod pa rnams 'phel bar mdzad/ log par rtog pa'i dri mas sbags pa rnams legs par bsal te/ bstan pa rin po che dar zhing rgyas par mdzad nas dgung lo don gsum shing
pho rta'i dbyug gu zla ba'i tshes nyi shu la dga' ldan du gshegs pa lam yig tu gsungs kyang / ston pa'i gsung gi gral tshes bco brgyad la byon par bzhed de/ dga' ldan du
rje btsun byams pa'i drung du lha'i bu nam mkha' dri ma med pa zhes bya bar gyur te/ bka' gdams pa'i bla ma dam pa rnams kyi gsung las/ bskal bzang 'di la rje btsun byams
pa'i rjes su/ rgyal ba seng ge 'byon par gsungs pa de jo bo rje yin par bzhed do/ /lnga pa de'i rjes su slob pa'i bshes gnyen byon tshul la gnyis/ rgya gar du byon tshul
dang / bod du byon tshul lo/ /dang po ni/ rgya gar/ kha che/ u rgyan/ gser gling / li yul/ bal po rnams su dngos slob paNDi ta dang / grub thob du ma dang / de dag gi yang
nying slob bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig byon la/ bi kra ma shi lar yang slob ma paNDi ta ratna kirti/ ta thA ga ta rakShi ta/ su ma ti kirti/ bai ro tsa na rakShi/ bA lo
ka na kA shI la sogs pa sum cu tsam yod kyang / thun mong ma yin pa'i slob ma lnga ni/ paNDi ta chen po bi to pa/ dharmA a ka ra ma ti/ dbu ma seng / bshes gnyen gsang ba/
sa'i snying po rnams ni jo bo dang rtogs pa byin rlabs mi mnyam yang / mkhyen pa mnyam pa tsam du grags so/ /gnyis pa bod du byon tshul ni/ gangs ri'i khrod 'dir rab tu
byung ba dang skye bo phal che

bas chos thob cing bka' drin gyis khyab pa las/ de rnams kyi nang nas chos brgyud 'dzin pa la slob ma grags che ba byon tshul dang / slob ma mchog byon tshul lo/ /dang po ni/
mnga' ris skor gsum nas lha byang chub 'od dang / pho brang zhi ba 'od/ lo chen rin bzang / rgya brtson seng / nag tsho lo tsA ba/ lo chung legs shes/ mang yul lo tsA
ba grags 'byor shes rab/ 'bro lo tsA ba shes rab 'od/ lo tsA ba dge blo/ lo tsA ba shAkya blo gros/ go mi bsgom chen/ 'dul 'dzin gzus rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ gnas brtan gser
bzo rnams byon pa las/ lha btsun pas jo bo chen po'i chos mang du mkhyen/ 'jig rten dbang phyug gi zhal gzigs/ mngon shes lnga thob bo/ /lo chen rin chen bzang po ni/ rigs
kha che'i g.yu ri g.yu sgra bya ba/ yab gzhon nu dbang phyug yum cog ro kun bzang shes rab brtan ma/ lcam sring bzhi yod pa'i gcen shes rab dbang phyug gi gcung rin chen
dbang phyug tu sku skye ba bzhes/ dgung lo bcu gsum la mkhan po legs pa bzang po las rab tu byung ste/ mtshan rin chen bzang por gsol/ de'i mod la 'dul ba rgya cher 'grel
thugs su chud/ de nas rgyal po'i bkas kha cher byon/ lo tsA mkhas par bslabs/ paNDi ta ka ra rnam gsum sogs rgya gar gyi paN grub du ma la gtugs/ theg pa mtha' dag gi
chos la sbyangs/ bstan pa la bya ba cher mdzad/ a ti sha dang pu rangs su mjal te/ gu ge khri thang pas mdzad pa'i lo chen gyi rnam thar las/ dgung lo brgyad cu rtsa bdun
la mjal bar gsungs/

ji ltar mjal ba'i tshul sogs ni gong du bshad pa ltar yin la/ gzhan yang yo ga gsang 'dus/ bde mchog sogs kyi dbang dang rgyud kyi bshad pa/ man ngag sogs theg pa gong 'og
gi chos mtha' dag gis thugs tshim par mdzad/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs gnang bas rtogs pa khyad par can 'khrungs pas lhag par dad de/ lha rten dang dpe ma gtogs
pa gang yod phul/ jo bos dbus su lo tsA la 'gro dgos gsungs pas/ nga rgas pas mi nus zhus/ 'o na sgrub pa bgyis gsungs pas mnyes te/ lo tsA ba chen po la paNDi ta'i bla ma
drug cu yod kyang / jo bo nyid ma gtogs pa gzhan rnams kyis sgrub pa la ma chud/ de nas lo tsA bas sgo gsum rim du byas pa la/ dam bca' ba'i yi ge gsum bris te sgrub pa
mdzad pas/ gsang 'dus dang bde mchog gi zhal gzigs/ dgung lo dgu bcu rtsa brgyad la dgun zla tha chung gi tshes bcu bdun skar ma rta pa yod pa'i nyin mkha' spyod du gshegs
par gu ge khri thang pas gsungs so/ /rgya brtson seng gtsang stag tshal du 'khrungs/ rten dge bsnyen zer te phyis rab tu byung ba mdzad/ rgya gar du jo bo la chos mang
du gsan/ 'jam dbyangs kyi sprul par chos kyi 'byung gnas su bshad cing bal por sku gshegs/ lo tsA ba nag tsho ni/ yul gung thang / gdung nag tsho/ mtshan tshul khrims rgyal
ba/ 'dul ba 'dzin par grags/ rgya brtson seng la mngon pa mkhas par bslabs/ dgung lo nyer bdun la rgya gar du jo bo chen po spyan 'dren

du byon/ lo bcu dgu'i bar tshul bzhin du bsten/ thun mong gi yon tan rnams rdzogs par mdzad/ nag tsho snye thang nas mnga' ris su 'byon khar/ jo bos bslab bya mang du mdzad
de/ dam tshig gsum bkod kyi sku phyag tu bzung nas byin rlabs mdzad/ 'dul ba mdo rtsa dang / gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgya dpe dang / 'gro chos su thun mong ma yin pa'i spyan
ras gzigs kyi sgrub skor sogs sbas chos nyi shu gnang ste lung bstan mang du mdzad/ jo bo rang gi sku mthe bong tsam seng ldeng la bris te ga'ur bcug nas gung thang pa'i
dpung pa la btags/ mnyes mnyes rgya cher mdzad/ jo bo la gung thang pas kyang lan gsol te phyi bzhag rnams 'brom la bzhag rnal 'byor pas kyang nag tsho la bslab bya ji ltar
mdzad pa'i tshul rnams/ snye thang du mdzad pa'i zhu lan dang / rnal 'byor pa'i bstod yig tu grags par gsal lo/ /de nas mnga' ris su byon nas lung bstan pa bzhin sgrub
pa mdzad pas/ 'jam dpal rdo rje/ sgrol ma/ yi ge drug pa rnams zhal gzigs/ mngon shes kyang mnga' la/ de las slob brgyud phyag sor ba sogs byon tshul 'og tu 'chad do/ /lo
chung legs shes ni 'khrungs yul mnga' ri pu hrang pa/ bal por thang bi ha ra bya ba rgyal pos bzhengs pa'i gtsug lag khang du rngog rin chen rgyal mtshan gyis zhus sna
byas te mjal/ rdo rje 'byung ba/ gtsug dgu/ khams gsum rnam rgyal gyi dkyil chog bstod 'grel dang bzhi'i rgya dpe/ gsang 'dus kyi chos skor zhu ba'i rten du phul nas/ jo
bo dang / lo tsA bas

bsgyur/ de nas yo ga rnams gsungs te bod du jo bo'i yo ga'i 'khor 'dus pa dang po lo chung legs shes yin gsungs/ lo tsA ba dge blo ni/ lo chen gyi slob ma rig pa can gyi khye'u
lnga'i nang nas/ gnyis kha cher tshad pas grongs/ gsum ni smra lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros/ mang wer gyi lo tsA ba byang chub rtse mo/ ljang lo tsA ba rin chen gzhon
nu dang gsum las/ 'di nyid dang po ste/ lo chen la mkhas par sbyangs/ jo bo chen po'i drung du chos mang du zhus yun ring du bsten/ lam sgron sogs 'gyur mang du mdzad do/
/go mi sgom chen ni/ jo bo la lo chen gyi rnal 'byor rgyud kyi skor gsan pa'i dus su sbyong rgyud dang / gtsug dgu'i dbang dang / rgyud kyi bshad pa sogs gsan te da lta
yang go mi nas brgyud pa kun rig sogs bsnur lugs su grags pa rnams so/ gzus rdo rje rgyal gyis dang por klu mes can du byon te mdo rtsa 'grel pa dang bcas pa sogs 'dul ba'i
gzhung rnams la mkhas par sbyangs/ de nas jo bo'i drung du theg pa che chung gi chos mang du gsan te/ ngas bslabs pa'i chos thams cad kyang lam du song gsungs/ 'di la
bu chen bzhi ste/ stod du zhang zhung pa rgyal ba'i shes rab/ 'dzim pu gzhon tshul/ dbus su 'brom seng dkar/ bstod pa ye shes bla ma/ de rnams kyi slob ma rgya 'dul 'dzin
yin la/ 'dis dgung lo brgyad cu rtsa lnga bzhugs/ grwa ba 'dul ba'i bshad nyan pher ba stong phrag lhag pa sogs byung ste/ bod du 'dul ba'i bshad grwa rnams dang / 'dul
'dzin gser ri'i phreng ba lta bu byon pa rnams

phal cher 'di las mched cing / a ti sha nas brgyud pa'i chos skor la nyams len mdzad pas slob brgyud du gyur pa yin no/ /gzhan yang glo bo'i yul nas ston pa yang rab sogs dang
/ gtsang stod nas grags ston che chung gnyis/ legs 'brel che chung gnyis byon/ gtsang smad nas 'gar mgos yol gsum zhes grags che bas/ de dag gi lo rgyus cung zad bshad
na/ rong pa 'gar dge ba gsal gyis jo bo la mdo sngags kyi chos mang du zhus/ khyad par lU hi pa'i dbang bka'/ lha sbas kyi 'grel pa la brten pa'i bshad bka'/ chos tshan
dgu la sogs pa'i rdzogs rim yongs su rdzogs par gsan nas/ des lha rje bstod pa/ steng pa zla gsal sogs la brgyud do/ /rje 'gos ni/ rus 'gos/ yab yum rus gcig pas khug pa/
lhas phug tu 'khrungs pas lhas btsas te/ gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer dang 'grogs te rgya gar du byon/ spyir paNDi ta bdun cu/ mkha' 'gro'i bla ma gnyis la chos gsan/ de'i tshe
paNDi ta mnyam po la'ang / 'dus pa la kha zin che bar snang bas/ thog mar gsang 'dus la slob gnyer mdzad de/ 'dus pa la mkhas pa'i paNDi ta bcu tsam bsten pa'i nang nas/
yul bhaM ga la'i mkhas pa chen po dI paM ka ra zhes rgya gar du 'dus pa gsan pa'i dpon slob yin la/ jo bo'i gsang 'dus 'phags skor thams cad mnga' zhing / bod du yang
chos mang du gsan te rtsa ba'i slob ma yin/ spyir sngags thams cad/ khyad par du gsang ba 'dus pa la mkhas par grags/ 'di la slob

ma rgyud kyi ka ba tshugs pa bzhi/ man ngag gi gdung theg pa brgyad/ las tshogs dang 'phrin las la mkhas pa lcam dang gral ma ltar dpag tu med pa byon no/ /yol chos dbang ni/
sku mched gsum ste/ yol drang srong / yol thog 'bebs dang gsum ka jo bo'i dngos slob tu gtogs pa yin yang / 'dir dang po ste/ jo bo gtsang nyang tsho gnas su phebs dus/
jo bo'i zhal nas/ da nangs tho rangs nam mkha' la hriHdkar po sgra dang bcas pa cig byung / bcu gcig zhal gyi sku li ma 'di la phog de las 'od 'phros bod thams cad 'od
kyis khyab nas 'od de ban chung gzhon nu zhig la phog pas/ de'i sgyu lus 'od gsal du shar ba rmis gsungs/ nyi ma rtse shar la yol chos dbang btsun chung lo bcu drug lon pa
gcig gis dar dang gser phul/ bdag la thugs rje chen po'i gdam ngag zhig zhu zer bas/ jo bo dgyes nas bcu gcig zhal gyi sku de yang gnang / spyan ras gzigs dang / rta mgrin
sogs kyi chos skor rnams snga phyir rdzogs par gnang / thugs rje chen po zhi khro mang du zhal gzigs te dngos grub brnyes so/ /gzhan yang stod lung gnam gyi rdzing kha
ba/ mal shes rab sems pas jo bo la yun ring du bsten te/ bsgoms pas smin mtshams nas 'od zer byung / de'i rjes sems bcug nas bsgoms pas zhing khams mang po mthong ba byung
ste/ jo bo la lam du 'gyur ram zhus pas/ zhi gnas kyi cha mthun yin/ bla ma mtshan nyid dang ldan pas zin na lam du 'gyur gsungs/ yang lan cig snye thang na/ jo bo'i
gzim chung du khong

rtogs pa 'bul ba la/ khu ston gyis lkog nyan byas pas/ sa thob pa tsam du mngon te/ khong phyir byung ba'i rjes/ khu ston gyis jo bo la/ de su lags/ rtogs pa ji tsam du 'dug
zhus pas/ mal shes rab sems dpa' bya ba theg pa chen po'i sbyor lam dro la nye bar 'dug gsungs/ de gar song zhus pas/ kho rkang mgyogs kyi dngos grub thob pas rlung shod
ngar gyi la la slebs song / rang sgreng la 'gro bar 'dug gsungs/ 'dis stod lung tsha thog gi dgon pa btab ste/ spyan snga'i rab byung mdzad pa'i mkhan po yin no/ /dbus
nas khu rngog 'brom gsum grags che bas de rnams kyi lo rgyus 'og tu 'chad la/ gzhan yang rngog byang chub 'byung gnas/ rlan ye shes shes rab/ zhang sna nam rdo rje dbang
phyug gsum la/ theg chen gdung rgyud rten mdzad gsum du grags/ ka ba ston pa shAkya dbang phyug rag shi ston pa tshul khrims gzhon nu/ rma ston pa shAkya byang chub/ dar
ston pa byang chub dpal/ sba ston pa g.yu rung rin chen/ gar mi ston pa yon tan g.yu rung / rgyus ston pa chos kyi rgyal po/ bang ston chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ 'dang 'jang
ston pa/ zhang sna chung ston pa/ lhab mi ston pa shes rab 'od zer te dbus kyi ston chen bcu gcig go /zhang btsun yer pa ba ye shes 'bar/ sa phug pa zhu sgom/ mkha' ru ba
chen po grags pa snga ma ste sgrub pa rtse gcig tu mdzad pa gsum mo/ /gzhan yang rngog sgom yon tan rgyal po/ sgom pa dad pa bla ma/ rnal 'byor pa g.yung drung rgyal mtshan/
sum pa mthu chen/ sgro arYa byang chub/ khu sengge

rgyal mtshan rnams byon cing / zhang btsun yer ba pa ye shes 'bar ni/ rje btsun byams pa la chos gsan par gsungs shing / po to pa'i gnas kyi slob dpon yin la/ phyis kyi zhang
yer 'bar ba rten skya bo bla ma zhang gi bla ma dang mi cig la/ de rnams jo bo chen po'i thun mong ma yin pa'i slob ma yin no/ /gzhan yang mar pa lo tsA la dbang rin chen
phreng ba gnang / khyung po rnal 'byor la sems bskyed/ byams chos/ bde mchog gsang 'dus/ gshed bskor dang bcas pa gnang / mar pa do ba dang / pu hrang lo chung la bde
mchog gi bskor rnams gnang / ba ri lo tsA la sgra'i skor rnams gnang ste/ mdor na gangs ri'i khrod 'dir skyes mchog kun la bka' drin gyis khyab par mdzad do/ /khams nas
rnal 'byor pa chen po dpal ldan dgon pa ba/ rnal 'byor pa shes rab rdo rje/ phya dar ston pa dang bzhi la khams pa sku mched bzhi zhes grags pa de rnams kyi lo rgyus cung
zad brjod na/ rnal 'byor pa chen po 'khrungs yul mdo smad tsong kha yos bu lo ba/ gdung rus lung / mtshan byang chub ran/ lo sum cu rtsa gnyis la dbus su byon/ jo bo dang
thog mar mang yul bzor gnas su mjal/ lo dgu bsten/ dpal ldan dgon pa ba/ mdo khams stod kyi ldan ma sga pa'i sgrol ma lha khang pa/ gdung rus 'dzeng / 'brug lo pa/ mtshan
dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ mdo khams nas dang po kaM po ri pa bya ba'i grub thob gcig la gtad nas byon/ mnga' ris na paNDi ta byon 'dug bya ba gsan pas/ jo bo dang nya
mtsho gnas

rnying du mjal/ rnal 'byor pa dang gnyis la jo bos thun mong gi chos bzhis rgyud snod rung du mdzad nas/ lha 'di dang las 'brel 'dug gsungs te/ dam tshig gsum bkod kyi sgrub
thabs gnang nas bsgrubs pas/ bzlas pa stong phrag brgyad brgyad song nas zhal gzigs/ jo bo lo dgu bsten/ rnal 'byor pa shes rab rdo rjes jo bo lo lnga bsten cing / phyis
rngog legs shes dang lhan du bzhugs te gsang phur sku gshegs so/ /phya dar ston pas kyang jo bo lo lnga bsten te snye thang du bod ston rnams kyis phar phyin gsung ba zhus
pas/ thog mar paNDi ta'i bshad lugs dang / de nas jo bo nyid kyi bzhed pa/ ston pa bzhi'i sgo nas khrid tshul gsungs pas/ phya dar ston pas zin bris su btab pas shin
tu legs pa cig byung / phar phyin khams lugs mar grags te/ khong phar phyin la rtsal thon par gsungs/ gnyis pa chos brgyud 'dzin pa'i slob ma mchog byon tshul la gsum/ bshes
gnyen ston pa byon tshul/ dge bshes gsang phu ba byon tshul/ nag tsho'i rjes slob byon tshul lo/ /dang po ni/ de rnams kyi nang nas jo bo chen po'i chos kyi brgyud 'dzin
pa'i mchog 'brom ston pa rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas yin te/ 'khrungs yul byang rtsa dgye mo phyogs su mdzad/ gdung rus 'brom gyi nang tshan brag gsum/ yab yab bsher sku bzher/
ltag sku bzher/ yum khu rdo 'od bza' gnyis kyis sras su shing pho 'brug la 'khrungs/ gzhur zhang po'i sar g.yung chos mgon la klog bslabs/ slob gnyer mdzad kyin yod
pa'i dus/ rgyal

gyi zhang chen po la dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa blangs/ de nas dgung lo bcu bdun bzhes pa la/ se btsun dbang phyug gzhon nu khams nas yar byon/ rgya gar du 'byon par bzhed de/
bal yul bar byon/ lo gcig na slar log pa dang mjal khrid par zhus pas/ sang red shog gsungs bas/ tshong pa dang 'grogs te byon/ khams su lo hril po bcu dgu se btsun la bsten/
mdo sngags kyi chos mang du gsan mkhas par gyur te dge bsnyen chos 'phel du grags/ snying rje pad dkar du/ byang phyogs su bstan pa la dad pa lhar skye zhing / rab byung
chos bzhin mi spyod pa log par ltung / der dge bsnyen chos 'phel zhes pa rdzu 'phrul dang ldan pa 'byung / zhes pa dang / sangs rgyas phal po cher yang / byang phyogs
su dge bsnyen chos 'phel bya ba 'byung zhes 'brom ston pa nyid lung bstan pa yin no/ /de nas 'brom gyi dgongs pa la/ dal 'byor mi lus thob par dka' ba skyed pa'i dus 'dir
chos rnal ma gcig byed na 'di tsam gyi chog gam mi chog rgya gar mkhas pa gcig la dri ba la bar du lo tsA ba mi dgos pa byed dgongs te paNDi ta sgra'i tsher ma bya ba
la bi warta la sogs pa bslabs/ kha cig smr-irti nydzA na dang gcig par 'dod/ de nas lo tsA mkhas par bslabs/ de nas se btsun gyi zhal nas pha dang phrad par song gsungs te/
dgung lo so brgyad 'gro ba la yar byon/ byang 'phrang kha sogs chu khar phebs/ 'phrang kha ber chung gis ra sgreng gi dgon pa phul/ mnga' ris su lha bla mas paNDi ta spyangs
te phebs

pa sngar nas gsan kyang / de'i tshe ring por mi thogs par rgya gar du 'byon par 'dug zer bas/ mtshan thos pa tsam gyis dad pa lhag par skyes te yar byon/ jo bo dpon slob pu
hrang na bzhugs pa la/ sgrol ma'i zhal nas/ da ni zhag gsum dros dang bzhi bod kyi u pA sa ka 'byon pas byin gyis rlobs shig gsungs/ jo bos kyang de'i sta gon mdzad/ u pA
nye ba/ a sa ka gnas pa ste mtshams sbyar bas/ u pA sa ka nye bar gnas pa'am/ dge bsnyen la 'jug la/ pa'i ring cha chad pa dang / se ka ces pa ma dag ste/ u pa se ka dge
bsnyen ma la 'jug go /de nas rta'i lo rang lo so dgu la jo bo dang mjal/ byin gyis brlabs/ dbang skur/ 'jam dpal rdo rje'i sku yang gnang / khyod bla ma rnams dang / sgrol
mas lung bstan pa'i slob ma yin pas nga'i rtsar sdod/ nga'i bka' brgyud 'di la gsol ba thob dang byin rlabs yod kyis/ byin rlabs 'byung gi gsungs/ de'i tshe jo bo nyid
kyang rgya gar du log par bzhed/ lo tsA ba yang sngar gyi chad yod pas phar bskyal bar bzhed pa la/ ston pas kyang bzhugs par zhu ma nus/ 'on kyang thabs la mkhas pas dbus
na rgyal blon gyi bzhengs pa'i gtsug lag khang yod tshul dang / dge 'dun gyi sde mang du bzhugs pa rnams jo bo phebs par mos tshul dang / bod ston rnams la yang chad
yod pa bzhin 'phrin yig btang ba sogs gong du bshad pa ltar dka' ma du mas bod du spyan drangs te ston pas lo ngo bcu gsum tshul bzhin du bsten cing / bshes gnyen ston pa
la bla ma lnga yod pa ni/ dang por

klog bslab pa'i slob dpon/ gzhu'i kun dga' ra ba'i g.yung chos mgon/ rgyal gyi zhang chen po/ se btsun dbang phyug gzhon nu/ paNDita sgra'i tsher ma can/ jo bo ni 'gran gyi
do med yin la/ spyir jo bo'i chos thams cad thugs la mnga' ba yin te/ mi 'chug bsdams pa las kyang / jo bo'i zhal nas/ gzhung bzang khyod ni tshangs spyod sdom pas phyug
/smon 'jug sems skyed lag len snying rjes mdzad/ /dbang bzhi yongs rdzogs gsang ba phyir mi sgrog /sdom gsum khyod kyi rgyud la rdzogs par gnas/ /de dag kun gyi lam rim
lag len rnams/ /rim pa bzhin du nyams khrid bskyangs pa las/ /kun la thogs med khyod kyi blo la rdzogs/ /gzhan yang bslab bsdus spyod 'jug la sogs pa/ /don yod go ste sems
la phan pa'i chos/ /brgya dang bcu gsum khyod kyis dag par bslabs/ /gsang ba gzhan la bstan par dka' ba yang / /sbas pa'i chos rnams khyod kyis lon par mdzad/ /khyon ni
zhu mkhas kho bo snod la rtog /lha rnams kun la bag chags bzhag pa'i phyir/ /sgrub thabs stong phrag nyi shu rtsa bzhi'i khrid/ /kho bo phyogs 'dir bos pa'i dgos pa dang
/ /sdom gsum don du gnyer bar 'dod pa la/ /so so'i lag len rim par dkrol ba lags/ /zhes sogs mang du gsungs pa sogs kyis shes so/ /khyad par du rgyal bas lung bstan pa shing
rta chen po gnyis kyi gdams pa'i bcud/ rgyal ba'i bka' bstan bcos thams cad 'gal med du nyams su len pa'i lam ma nor

ba'i gdams ngag khyad par can dpal ldan a ti sha la mnga' ba de gtso bor 'brom ston pas thob par mdzad cing / bshes gnyen ston pa'i rjes 'jug sku mched gsum la sogs pa rnams
la yang bka' gdams pa zhes mtshan du grags la/ ston pas mdzad pa'i lha chos bdun ldan chung ba las/ ngo mtshar bka' ni sde snod gsum po ste/ /gdams pa skyes bu gsum gyis
phyug pa yin/ /bka' gdams rin chen gser gyi phreng ba la/ /'gro ba gang gis bgrangs kyang don yod 'gyur/ /zhes pa nas/ bdag gi bla ma 'gran gyi do med 'di/ /tshul khrims
gos can lta ba'i rnal 'byor pa/ /ye shes lus can mtshan dang dpe byad ldan/ /log pa'i chos las nges par 'das pa yin/ /e ma ya mtshan bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i/ /bde bar gshegs
pa rgyal ba gnyis pa 'di'i/ /brgyud par bcas pa'i rjes su 'brang du byung / /de yis kho bo bod du lus blangs kyang / /bsod nams mi chung shin tu skal ba bzang / /zhes
pa'i bar gsungs so/ de ltar 'brom ston jo bo dang mjal ba'i dus dang / bsten pa'i lo grangs la mi mthun pa mang yang 'di las gzhan du 'dod pa ma dag par mngon no/ /jo
bo dga' ldan du gshegs nas/ ka ba shAkya dbang phyug sogs bod ston rnams kyis jo bo'i 'das mchod chen po snye thang du btang / ston pas snye thang du lo gcig bzhugs/ jo bo'i
gdung dang rten gsum sogs spyan drangs te/ shing mo lug gi lo la ra sgreng du byon/ dgon pa'i sa spyad gzigs pas shin tu legs par dgongs te/ brag seng ge'i zhol du mnal
lam brtags pas/

dbu rtse'i sa na gser gyi mchod rten 'dug pa'i 'od zer las/ dbu rtse dga' 'ji ra ser lhag ge ba mang po byung nas bod yul thams cad 'od kyis gang bar byas te tshur 'dus shug
pa'i gseb thams cad gang ba dang / gzhan yang 'ching dkar ba mar gyi phung po dang / pha 'ong thang rin po che'i phung por song ba la sogs pa'i bltas khyad par can mang
po rmis te/ nang par sum pa mthu can dang / rnal 'byor pa/ dgon pa ba gsum gyis bltas bzang ngam zhus pas/ bzang gsungs nas/ dgon pa 'debs par thag bcad/ sa 'dul la brgyad
stong pa 'grel pa dang bcas pa gsungs/ me pho spre'u lo la dgon pa gong dang / gzim khang rnams mdzad/ me mo bya'i lo sa ga zla ba'i tshes gnyis la sa chog mdzad/ dpal
gsang ba 'dus pa lha bcu dgu'i thig btabs te/ ka gnyis ma'i rmang bting / gur dkar phebs/ jo bo'i gdung dang / dngul gdugs can/ 'jam dpal rdo rje las sogs pa bzhugs/ bzo
bo bi ri rnal 'byor bya bas ka gnyis ma rgya phibs/ khyams stod ka ba bcu gnyis rnams bya lo rang la grub par mdzad/ rten gsar bzhengs pa rnams kyi rab gnas sogs rnal 'byor
pa gong 'og gis grogs mdzad de phun sum tshogs par grub nas/ jo bo'i gdung bzhugs pa'i khyung mgo grub nas/ 'di man chad la byed pa po gcig 'ong gis gsungs nas/ 'dzim
rdo yon tan 'bar la/ khyod 'jig rten gyi shes che bas gyis/ kho bos tshe 'di'i rnam rtog yongs blo cig bgyi gsungs te/ 'jig rten mkhyen pa rnyed dang ma rnyed dang / /zhes
sogs gsungs shing / 'jig rten

chos brgyad mgo snyoms mdzad do/ /de dus rnal 'byor pa phyag khri mchog jo bo lo lnga bsten pa de ra sgreng na bzhugs pa la kho bo mtshams shig byed pa yin gsungs nas/ 'jig
rten gyi rnam par rtog pa la mtshams po che mdzad de shug sib na gang dgar bzhugs nas rtse gcig tu sgrub pa mdzad/ dgung lo zhe gnyis 'gro ba'i dus bshes gnyen ston pas
'khor cig la bdud rtsi'i ka pA la gang bkur te/ phyag khri mchog la gtad pa gsol nas mkha' spyod du gshegs so/ /de ltar bshes gnyen ston pa thugs zab la skyel che ba mkhyen
pa rgya mtsho lta bu mnga' ba des/ mdo rgyud du ma nas lung bstan pa'i ra sgreng de/ bod kyi sde pa gang gi yang phyogs su ma chad pa/ bi kra ma shI la'i gnas chung /
jo bo'i gdan sa/ rnal 'byor gong 'og rnams kyi sgrub gnas/ bod kyi spyi mchod khyad par can 'di byung ba yin no/ /de yang sngon gyi yi ge las/ chos kyi rgyal po srong btsan
sgam po byang du mi rgod 'dul ba la byon dus/ ra sgreng du phebs te dbu skra gtor nas/ 'dir spos shing rgyas par gyur pa'i tshe/ gnas 'dir nga'i sprul pa 'byung / zhes
gsungs pa/ bshes gnyen ston pa yin par bzhed do/ /de lta bu'i ra sgreng der sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa/ a ti sha'i chos srol dri ma med pa rnams btsugs te/ spyir las dang
skal ldan gyi slob ma brgyad cu tsam smin par mdzad cing / khyad par du sku mched rin po che gsum jo bo nyid kyi snye thang du lung bstan te/ 'brom rje thub pa'i bstan pa
lnga stong gnas/ /'on kyang bod du chos spyod ji ltar dar/ /bdag

gis bstan pa skyong skyed byas pa yin/ /da ni legs par gzhi bzhengs tshar ba yin/ /chos 'di legs par skyongs shig rgyal ba 'brom/ /mtha' rgya byang nas skyed cig snying stobs
can/ /pho rus rnam thar zungs shig khrol gzhung can/ /pha gcig bu gcig yin no snying la soms/ /shes dang / bdag gis bstan pa 'di ni khyod la gtad/ /lo skor gcig gi bar
du byang phyogs su/ /chos kyi char pa phobs la gzhan don mdzod/ /de nas khyod kyi yon tan ma lus pa/ /gang zag gcig gis blang bar mi nus kyis/ /las can brgyad cur bgos la
mtha' rgya skyod/ /gtso bo sprul pa'i sku mched gsum po la/ /gzhung dang man ngag thun mong gsum byin la/ /lhag chad med par rang gi gdan sa gtod/ /gnas kyi gdan sar a
mes chen po bskos/ /de nas zhen cing chags pa ma byed par/ /dga' ldan gnas su bdag gi drung du shog /ces bshes gnyen ston pa bstan pa'i bdag por byin gyis brlabs shing /
chos kyi gdan sa sku mched gsum dang gnas kyi gdan sa rnal 'byor pa dang bcas pa lung bstan cing / las can brgyad cu'i nang nas grags che ba gong du bshad pa'i khams pa sku
mched bzhi dang / gzhan yang khams nas rnal 'byor pa byams pa'i blo gros/ yongs rdzogs rnal 'byor pa/ lho brag nas rnal 'byor pa phyag khri mchog btsun pa dge skyong sogs
dang bi ri rnal 'byor pa/ stong rtsan nam go rgyu ra gzhon nu 'od zer/ lhab mi shes rab g.yung drung / sgom pa rin chen bla ma/ gtsang pa jo pad/ ka ba rgya dkar/

mar ba jo legs/ bran ka jo btsun/ sum sgom dbang phyug 'od zer/ rnal 'byor pa g.yung drung rgyal mtshan ste 'di rnams jo bo dang ston pa thun mong pa'i slob ma/ yi dam lha
zhal gzigs pa/ skyes bu chen po'i lam la bzhugs pa sha stag go /sras kyi thu bo ni sku mched gsum po nyid yin la/ kha cig khams lung pa dang sku mched bzhir yang 'dod de/
'dis yung nga'i khams lung du dgon pa btab/ 'gro don mdzad cing lo go bzhi bzhugs so/ /gzhan yang zhang ye shes rgyal mtshan/ brag rgyab pa gnyan ston shAkya 'byung / mnga'
ris pa 'dul 'dzin rug pa'i zhang chen po/ rnam thar gtsang ba'i ka skyog pa chen po/ 'dzin sgom yon tan 'bar/ sgro byang chub tshul khrims/ a mi thar pa rgyal mtshan/
a mi sman la sogs pa de rnams bshes gnyen ston pa'i slob ma thun mong ma yin par grags che ba rnams yin no/ /de ltar slob ma rnams smin par mdzad de/ lo dgur bstan pa'i
mnga' bdag mdzad nas drug cu re gcig pa 'brug lo la ra sgreng nas/ rje btsun byams pa'i drung na jo bo rje nyid lha'i bu nam mkha' dri ma med pa zhes bya bar bzhugs pa'i
drung du gshegs/ bka' gdams kyi gsungs rab dag las/ ston pa ni lha'i bu rgyal ba rgyal mtsho/ ka ba shAkya dbang phyug ni lha'i bu shAkya dri med/ rngog legs shes ni lha'i
bu shes rab sgron ma/ lo tsA ba nag tsho ni lha'i bu tshul khrims ldan zhes bya bar 'gyur bar gsungs so/ /de'i srol 'dzin byon tshul la gsum/ ra sgreng du byon tshul/ sku
mched gsum byon tshul/ de las 'phel ba'i slob brgyud byon tshul lo/ /dang po ni/ rnal 'byor

pa chen pos ston pa yang lo dgu bsten/ ra sgreng gi gdan sa lo bcu gnyis mdzad pa'i ring / dgon pa gong nas phyir byon/ da lta dbu rtse ka ba bcu drug ma'i sa der gzim chung
mdzad/ de dus zhang phreng kha zer chung gi sras dgra bcom/ de'i sras ber brgyud dar ma ye shes kyis ka gnyis ma'i khyams rmad/ khyams chung / nag tshang gsum mdzad de
rab gnas rnal 'byor pa chen pos mdzad/ grwa sa mang du btsugs/ gdul bya du ma smin par mdzad de dge 'dun sam brgya tsam 'dus/ drug cu rtsa gnyis pa 'brug lo rgyal zla'i tshes
brgyad la ra sgreng nas gshegs/ dpe la lar/ rta lo ba yos la gshegs pas bdun cu tham pa bzhugs zer ba yang snang ngo / /de nas dpal ldan dgon pa ba gdan sar bskos/ ston
pa yang lo dgu bsten pa rnal 'byor pa dang 'dra/ ra sgreng gi gdan sa lo bcu mdzad/ dgon pa gong du bzhugs nas/ sne'u zur ba la sogs pa'i slob ma mang du smin par mdzad
de drug cu rtsa bdun pa khyi lo'i mngon par byang chub pa'i nya la ra sgreng du gshegs/ dgon pa ba la slob ma mang du byon pa'i mchog bu chen bcu ni/ klung shod rug pa'i
zhang ka ma ba shes rab 'od/ kha rag sgom chung / rog chor bu ba smra ba'i seng ge mtha' bzhi sgom pa/ 'phan yul rgyal du snyan sna mo ba dang / 'bri go te lung pa tshul
khrims skyabs gnyis/ dar yul du chu sgom gzhon nu snying po dang / tshul sgom ye shes rgyal mtshan gnyis/ 'phan yul gnya' ra sman 'dzar/ 'gar 'dul 'dzin/ spras mthong
pa sar sne'u zur ba rnams so/ /de rnams

kyi nang nas chos rgyud 'dzin pa'i mchog sne'u zur ba yin te/ 'di'i lo rgyus cung zad 'og tu 'chad do/ /de rnams rnal 'byor ba dang thun mong ba'i slob ma yin kyang / dgon
pa ba'i bu chen du yi ge rnying ma rnams su bgrang pa bzhin 'dir yang bkod pa yin no/ /kha rag sgom chung ni/ gtsang du sku 'khrungs/ lam po gnas su mkhan po mar sgom las
rab tu byung ste/ mtshan dbang phyug blo gros su btags/ dang po sba sgom bsod nams ye shes bya ba jo bo'i slob ma cig la chos gsan/ de nas ra sgreng du byon lo drug bzhugs
nas/ rnal 'byor pa dang / dgon pa ba gnyis la chos mang du gsan/ sgom chung pa'i thugs dgongs la/ da ni rang gis kyang chig skya thub ste 'ong snyam ste/ nyung ma'i sa
bon phul gang khyer nas spras kyi sne'u ke ru ru byon/ dbyar lo thug gsol/ dgun nyung thug la phye bun re btab nas gsol gyin lo bcu gcig sgrub pa rtse gcig tu mdzad/ de
nas kha rag tu byon nas sgrub pa mdzad pas/ kha rag sgom chung ngu grags/ kha cig mtho chos dang / aM yig bdun cu rnams spras brag rgyab tu mdzad zer te/ rnam thar na kha
rag shar du mdzad gsungs so/ /'dis rnal 'byor pa gong 'og gi gsung la rten nas lam rim don tshan bcu gnyis su bsdus pa mdzad de/ kha rag bskor gsum du grags pa'i gcig yin
no/ /bdun cu rtsa lnga la gtsang gi phug nag po bya bar gshegs khar/ lho pa la skyes pa'i yul spongs/ nye du dang thag bsrings/ bshes gnyen rtag tu bsten/ hrul po'i gos
gyon/ dman pa'i sa zung / ngan pa'i zas zo/ lo tshod chu bzhin du

'thungs la sgrub pa gyis gsungs pa'i gdams ngag gnang ste/ rus pa lhag ral rol tsho bsdus la/ byang ra sgreng na dpal ldan dgon pa ba'i sku 'bum yod pa/ de'i grib ma dang ser
bu phog sar skyol cig gsungs te/ de ltar byas so/ /de nas ra sgreng du dpal ldan dgon pa'i rjes su/ po to bas gdan sa lo gsum mam/ gcig mdzad kyang zer te/ zhang chos
rgyal la sogs pa khams pa ma rung pa 'ga' zhig gis bzhugs dbang ma byung pa dang / po to ba rang gi mnal lam du yang / zhing sa ma dul ba sogs byung bas/ der ma bzhugs par
sku mched gsum po dka' thub kyi sgo nas ri sul rnams su drang srong gi spyod tshul gyis gnas nges med du thugs dam dang / gzhan phan gong 'phel mdzad pas/ ra sgreng du
gdan sa la bar stong lo sum cu tsam dang / chos tshul la yang dar rgud cher byung / de nas sku mched gsum gshegs nas lo gcig gnyis na/ mtha' bzhi sgom pa bya ba/ ston pa
la yang thug cing / sku mched gsum gyi slob ma yin pa/ yid dam gyi lha mang po zhal gzigs cing / gzhan don 'phrin las la dbang 'byor pa des bla ma'i gdan sa nyams pa'i gtam
gsan pas/ ra sgreng du byon gnas tshul rnams gzigs te/ shar pa ba zho'i khang pa gnas na bzhugs pa dang / bya yul ba chen po/ glang ri thang pa/ ka ma pa/ lor sding po
ba rnams kyi drung du byon nas/ khyed rnams bla ma'i gdan sa la phyir mig lta na dus la bab nas 'dug gsungs te bskul bas/ de rnams kyis grogs mdzad 'bul ba chen po byung
ste/

ra sgreng du grwa tshang yang mang du btsugs/ bud med dang / ra lugs rnams phud/ chos khrims shin tu dam pa dang / dge 'dun mang po yang bzhugs par mdzad de chos srol cher
btsugs/ tshogs dpon bshes gnyen mtha' bzhis lo shas su mdzad do/ /khyad par shar ba pas/ ka gnyis ma'i nub tu dbu rtse ka dgu ma gcig dang por bzhengs pa/ phyis dpon gyad
pa dang / zer gu chos grags gnyis kyis mgo byas bzang 'dus bcu drug bya bas bdag rkyen byas nas/ ka chen bcu drug yod pa lho sgor bstan/ nyis thog gser 'bru/ gser bya gnyis
dang bcas pa bzhengs/ de'i khyams sman sgang phyug po bya bas byas so/ /po to ba bzhud nas/ lo mang po'i bar du mtha' bzhi la sogs pa sgres pa res gral dbu tsam ma gtogs/
gdan sar ming btags pa dang / 'chad nyan sogs cher med la skabs zhig tu rngog blo ldan shes rab la phul bas/ gsang phu dang sbrel te lo kha yar du chos bar zla ba gcig
gnyis tsam bzhugs pa yang mdzad do/ /de nas ka gnyis ma bzhengs nas lo dgu bcu rtsa gsum lon pa sa pho 'brug gi lo la ka ba nyi shu rtsa bzhi ma bzhengs pa'i sbyin bdag
brang kha ber chung gi brgyud pa se'o gzhon tshul zhes pa/ spyir ra sgreng gi skor du zhabs tog cher mdzad/ khyad par dbu rtse ka ba nyi shu rtsa bzhi/ ka gnyis ma'i shar
phyogs su bzhengs par 'dod pa la/ rin chen sgang du sangs rgyas dbon ston la sa spyad zhus pas/ shar nub nas rdo gnyis khyer shog gsungs te/ de la gzigs pas/ shar phyogs
su klu'i

rgyal po'i pho brang la gnod par 'dug pas/ nub phyogs su gyis gsungs pas/ bshes gnyen zhang 'od 'jo bas ra sgreng du lo bcu gnyis bzhugs pa'i bcu pa'i thog tu sa chog mdzad/
rmang btings/ de nas lo gnyis lcags pho rta'i lo bdun tu rtsa gsum pa bya zla'i tshes bco lnga la gshegs/ 'phan yul jog po 'chad khar byon pa'i bshes gnyen nam mkha' 'bum
gyi bla ma de yin no/ /de nas gzhon tshul gyi ka ba nyi shu rtsa bzhi/ nyi thog lho sgor bstan/ spen bad gser 'bras mdzes pa byas/ de'i khyams smad rtsong kha shaka 'byung
gis bzhengs/ de rnams kyi rab gnas pa sangs rgyas dbon ston gyis mdzad do/ /zhang 'od 'jo ba gshegs khar dgon pa dang gdan sa/ dgon 'od 'jo ba la gtad kyang / ra sgreng
pa gzhan rnams kyis ma phul ba/ sgang thang dkar bas thang dkar dang / ra sgreng sbrel nas lo nyi shu rtsa dgu gdan sa mdzad/ chu mo bya la gshegs/ der rjes sngar gyi
'brel pas zhang 'od 'jo ba'i slob ma dgon 'od 'jo ba yang zer/ zhogs pa chen por grags pa des gdan sa lo bcu drug mdzad/ de nas sgang thang dkar ba'i rje dang gnyis su gyes
pas/ dgon gong 'og gnyis su grags pa byung ngo / gnyis pa sku mched rin po che gsum byon tshul ni/ de ltar bshes gnyen ston pas ra sgreng du bka' gdams kyi chos srol
rnam par dag pa btsugs te bzhugs pa'i dus su 'phags pa sku mched gsum gyi byon tshul bzhin du bsten te yon tan rnams rdzogs par mdzad do/ /de yang bshes gnyen phu chung ba
ni/

rgyal gyi ra'i phu chung du lcags mo lugs la 'khrungs/ rus zur tshang / yab yum 'byor pa chung yang gser zho do bsnams nas/ rgyal lha khang du zhang chen po la rab tu byung
ste/ mtshan gzhon nu rgyal mtshan du btags/ khu ston la phar phyin 'grel pa don gsal tshar bco lnga dang / 'dul mngon la sogs pa mang du gsan te thos pa cher mdzad/ sne
thang du jo bo la chos kyi 'brel pa zhus pas/ mi rtag pa rang 'khrungs su byung ste gang la yang zhen chags med pa'i blo skyes gsungs/ de nas ra sgreng du byon pas/ sku mched
gzhan gnyis kyang byon te rten 'brel dang / pha rol tu phyin pa'i gdams ngag bslab phyogs/ spyod phyogs kyi skor rnams zhus/ lo bdun bsten/ khong rang la chos zhus mang
du byung yang / sha zug bzang po rang bza' ba'i dus yin/ gzhan la ster ba'i dus min gsungs nas sgrub pa gtso bor mdzad pas/ bdag las gzhan gces pa'i byang chub kyi sems
dang / chos thams cad bdag med par rtogs pa'i shes rab khyad par can 'khrungs/ yi dam mang po'i zhal gzigs/ nyams len byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa'i bka' gtso bor babs/ de
nas sku mched gsum 'bral med du sgrub pa mdzad kyin bzhugs/ phyis yung nga'i phu chung du bzhugs nas kyang sgrub pa gtso bor mdzad de/ brag gi dkyil na gser bre yod pa mngon
par mkhyen pa'i dgongs nas phyag 'khar gyis reg pas rang bye ste bton pa'i rjes dang / gzim khang gi nub na brag la phyag mdzub btsugs sar sgrub chu dang / zhabs rjes
dang / dbu zhwa'i rjes

yin zer ba yang da lta bar du yod par grags/ 'di la slob ma grags che ba/ sha pho sgang pa dang / 'ban tshul khrims rgyal ba zhes pa sku lus ma spangs par mkha' spyod du gshegs
pa dang / zhogs su 'khrungs pa sding pa shes rab rgya mtsho dang / zhogs phu'i karma brag pa rgyun du bzang spyod la zhal 'don mdzad pa la/ chu len dus bde ba can gyi
zhing der rab tu 'gro /zhes pa'i skabs su mkha' spyod du gshegs pa sogs/ sgrub pa snying por mdzad pa nyi shu tsam byon no/ /spyir sku mched gsum grwa pa la res su chad
pa med pas/ chos kyi 'brel pa la khyad par med do/ /de nas po to ba gshegs pa'i gdung cha lngar bgos te/ cha gcig dang / thugs bzhugs pa'i dngul gyi mchod rten khru bzhi
pa cig byas pa/ phu chung pas gsan pas/ dngul las byas na nga'i grogs po'i gdung ma 'ongs pa na mi ngan gyi grog mor phung ngo 'ongs dogs 'dug ste/ da byas stings rab gnas
nga la babs pas/ dbyar rgyal gyi do bo dgon par 'gro ba'i zhor la bya gsungs nas tshul khar rab gnas mdzad/ khyi lo'i ston yung nga'i phu chung du byon/ bdun cu rtsa drug
bzhes pa rgyal zla'i nyi shu gnyis la gshegs/ la lar po do dgon par gshegs zer ba yang 'dug go /bshes gnyen po to ba ni/ 'khrungs yul spras bra 'o thang / gdung rus gnyos/
yab sku bshen srid la dbang phyug yum me mo bya ba'i sras su me mo yos la 'khrungs/ byis pa'i dus su yab kyi mchod gnas ma sgom bya ba la sgom bslab par zhus pas/ khong
gi zhal nas/ thos pa en gcig

ma byas pa'i sgom mchan khung bas phu thag thung gsungs/ byis pa'i dus nas byang chub kyi sems skyes thob tu mnga' bar sha ra ba'i bstod pa nas gsungs/ de nas yer par rngog
byang chub 'byung gnas dang / rlan tshul khrims byang chub la mkhan slob zhus nas rab tu byung / mtshan rin chen gsal du btags/ jo bo chen po la yang de'i dus yer pa mjal/
dge bshes ston pa byang du 'bul ba'i gser sgrub pa la bzhud 'dug pas/ nag tshos lo tsA mdzad/ sgom rim tshar gcig gsan/ de nas khu ston gyi drung du byon mtshan nyid kyi
chos mang du gsan/ yer pa'i zhang btsun la gnas kyi slob dpon zhus/ de nas ra sgreng du bshes gnyen ston pa'i drung du dbyar de gdams ngag gcig zhus nas khams su 'byon
dgongs pa la/ sku mched gsum lhan gcig tu thog mar lam rim dang / spyod 'jug gsan nas/ bdag ni grol ba don gnyer la/ /snyed dang bkur stis 'ching mi nus/ /zhes pa'i skabs
kyi man ngag gsungs pa'i thad du thugs sna 'gyur te/ tshe 'di'i rnam rtog skyur nas bshes gnyen bsten pa yin gsungs/ ston pa lo bdun bsten nas yon tan thams cad rdzogs
par thob/ thugs rab che bas shin tu mnyes/ ston pa gshegs khar/ sku mched gsum gyi thugs la 'jigs sar skyel mas bor ba 'dra ba cig yong par 'dug na/ da su la brten snyam
ste spyan chab byung bas/ mngon shes kyis mkhyen nas/ ngas khyed gsum brten pa su yang ma mthong bas/ da phyin gsum yan/ lnga man dpung steng chos la dge ba'i bshes gnyen
mdo sde la

gyis/ sems bzang por gyis dang khyad par can cig dang / 'phrad de yong gis gsungs/ mdun na jo legs yod pas sems bzang po bya ba byang chub kyi sems la zer ba ma lags sam/ zhus
pas/ yin mod gsungs pas de snga nas ma go rgyus med pa la/ des gsal btab pa 'dra ba cig byung nas/ de'i thabs lkog tu man ngag tu yang gsungs/ tshogs su lung dang sbyar
nas kyang gsungs/ tha na bka' skyon tshun chod kyis kyang de'i thabs gsungs nas yod pas lo gnyis tsam du mya ngan bsangs pa 'dra ba cig byung / phyis sems bzang po byed
pa la/ khong rang dgos par song bas mya ngan la sangs dus ma byung gsungs/ ra sgreng nas byon te sku mched gsum/ dang po klung shod na mgor bzhugs/ des nas gnas nges med
du sgrub pa mdzad/ thugs gting zab pas yon tan 'di yod cher mi gsung yang / byang chub kyi thugs rang 'khrungs kyi tshul du mnga'/ yi dam lha dpag tu med pa'i zhal gzigs/
mngon par shes pa rgya chen po dang ldan pa'i tshul bsam gyis mi khyab bo/ /gzhan phan mdzad pa'i thog mar lam sgron/ yon tan mtha' yas par bstod pa/ bslab btus sogs gsungs
pas grangs sum brgya tsam byung / de nas rim gyis 'phel te/ grwa pa nyis stong tsam 'dus/ de thams cad kyang tshe 'di blos thong pa sha stag yod par grags/ ram sdings
ma bsrung na bzhugs dus cha rkyen med pas gos cung zad gnang ba la/ 'di ye mi gnang bar zhu/ bdag gi blo chud zos nas/ zad dus dge bshes kyis gnang ste 'ong snyam nas
brnab sems skye zhus pas

khyed ma 'dzoms snyam nas yid chad mi dgos/ nga gnas brtan bcu drug gi gcig yin pas nga dang mjal bas bsod nams che gsungs/ phyis gnas brtan yan lag 'byung gi sprul par zhal
gyis bzhes/ zang zing gi dngos po bre gang yang 'dzin chags mi mdzad/ phyis po tor bzhugs nas gzim chung ka gnyis ma dpe khang du grags pa sogs la brten nas bzhugs/ gzhan
phan mchog tu gyur te dgung lo don dgu bzhes pa bya lo la po tor yi dam mang po zhal gzigs/ shar phyogs kyi nam mkha' la lhas rol mo dang bcas te spyan drangs pa snang
ba las dag pa rnams kyis mthong / de na phyag thal mo sbyar te sems can rnams kyi skyabs dang mgon du gyur cig gsungs te gshegs/ gdung bzhu bas thugs ljags dang / ring bsrel
kha dog sna lnga mang du byon/ de nas sras chen brgyad kyi ka ba re btsugs pa'i dbu rtse ka brgyad ma dang / zhang ston shar ba pas sngar gyi chos ra'i sa la khyams
ka ba nyi shu rtsa lnga yod pa bzhengs so/ /sngon gyi gtam brgyud la po to'i sgo la su 'dzul rgyal/ sdings ma'i chu la su 'thung rgyal zer ba la kha cig po to'i sgo steng
du/ sdings ma ba'i gzims sa mdzad pas zer kyang / po to ba chos gsungs ba'i sgo nang du su tshud rgyal zer ba'i don yin zhes bka' gdams pa'i bla ma gong ma rnams gsung bar
grags/ rgyas par don du gnyer na rnam thar che chung gnyis la sogs par blta'o/ /'di la slob ma'i mchog bka' babs brgyad pa sogs pa bka' gdams gzhung pa'i srol 'dzin byon
tshul 'og tu 'chad do/ /grub pa'i dbang phyug chen po spyan snga ni/ 'khrungs yul nyan

gyi snang ra sgang / gdung rus dbas/ yab shAkya rdo rje/ yum li mo ye shes sgron gyi sras su lcags mo bya la 'khrungs/ mtshan stag tshab 'bar du btags/ byis pa'i dus su yum
gyi pang du khyer nas/ grong 'dul bya ba la phung po lnga'i rab byed gsan pas phung po 'di lngar 'byed tshod kyis mthar stong pa nyid du 'dug snyam du rang bzhin med pa'i
don thugs su chud/ dgung lo bcu gnyis la gong mo snang pa bya ba/ rang bzhin gyi rnal 'byor ma cig byon rdzogs rim zab pa cig gnang nas 'di sgoms gsungs te mi snang bar
gyur/ phyis de'i steng du sleb pa dpal ldan dgon pa bas gnang ba de min pa ma byung gsungs/ lo bco brgyad la tod lung tsha thog dgon par mal shes rab sems dpa' la rab tu
byung / mtshan tshul khrims 'bar du btags/ der yum gyi rmi lam du dung dkar gcig bus pa 'dzam bu gling byin gyis thos pa cig byung bas/ nga'i bu de rab tu byung nas grags
pa yang che ba cig 'ong bar 'dug gsungs/ slob gnyer mdzad dus tsha thog dgon par 'byon pa'i zhor la jo bo snye thang na mo cher bzhugs pa dang mjal te sems bskyed gsungs
pa gsan de'i dus spyi bor phyag bzhag saMskr-i ta'i skad du bkra shis kyi tshigs bcad mang po mdzad/ gser gling pa'i bum pa padma'i mchu can gnang / nga'i chos brgyud 'dzin
pa cig 'ong gsungs/ de nas lan tsha rab dang / rug par sde snod kyis gsan sbyong mang du mdzad/ rgya gar rdo rje gdan chos kyi 'byung khungs yin pas der 'byon dgongs
te/ lo tsA dang rgya gar gyi yig sna mang du bslabs/

de'i tshe sum rug bar byon nas/ 'di rnams phal cher dgra 'dres rtser ba dang / lto don du gnyer ba sha stag yin/ chos bya bsam nas rab tu byung ba ni khyod dang / zhang btsun
gnyis yin/ snying nas chos byed na ra sgreng du dengs zer nas yum gyis khrid nas/ dgung lo nyer drug la 'brom ston pa dang mjal/ spyan snga'i zhal nas/ nga'i ma rang bzhin
gyi rnal 'byor ma yin pas 'dir bskyal ba yin gsungs/ rgya gar du 'gro ba'i chos 'dra zhus pas/ ston pa'i zhal nas/ khyod rdo rje gdan du ma 'gro ngas rjes su 'dzin pa
yin/ tshes grangs 'di la lam rim gyi dbu 'dzugs gsungs te byon/ nyi ma shar ba dang 'dzoms pas rten 'brel bzang gsungs te/ lam rim gyis khrid pas ji lta ba bzhin thugs
la 'khrungs/ sku mched gzhan gnyis dang lhan cig gzhung gi bshad pa gsan/ spyan snga'i zhal nas/ zin nges pa re la'ang lan gsum gsum ston pa'i spyan sngar bskyar nas shog
bu dmar po la bris yod gsungs/ nub cig mnal lam du rdo rje gdan du byon pa rmis te/ jo bo shes rab dbang phyug bya ba rdo rje gdan la lan gsum skor ba cig dang / lo rgyus
rnams zhu thub byas pas cig par byung / rgya gar du mi thon pa la lta bar 'dug pas de'i dam bca' ma grub pa'i sdig sbyong du/ ngas tsha tsha bsags na ri de'u tsam 'ong
ba btab gsungs/ ston pa lo bdun tshul bzhin du bsten/ gzims g.yog kyang mdzad/ rgyun du spyan sngar bzhugs pas mtshan yang de ltar du grags/ yon tan thams cad rdzogs par
mdzad/ de dus ston pas theg pa chen po gsang sngags la

'o skol pha spad gnyis tsam yin gsungs pa'i yongs rdzogs rnal 'byor pas zhus sna mdzad de gsang sngags kyi chos mang po sku mched gzhan gnyis la thugs rgyus med par lkog chos
su snang bas yongs rdzogs rnam 'byor pa de nga la drin che gsungs/ ston pa gshegs nas zang zing gi dgos skal med de/ chos kyi dgos skal nged gsum gyis thob gsungs/ de
nas jo bo'i dngos slob grags che ba rnams la bsten pa'i dam bca' mdzad de/ rnal 'byor pa/ dgon pa ba/ shes rab rdo rje/ phyag dang ston pa sogs dang / gsang phur rngog legs
shes la yang zla ba bco brgyad bsten/ ra sgreng du zla ba re la nas bre lnga la brten te sgrub pa mdzad dus/ yi dam gyi lhas/ rigs kyi bu dal 'byor gyi mi lus thob pa
dran nam gsungs nas/ mnal sangs te nyin mtshan g.yel med du thugs dam mdzad pas/ rnal 'byor pa'i zhal nas/ bu khams bag re bsang gsungs pas/ dal 'byor rnyed par dka' ba 'di
bsam na/ skad cig kyang g.yel ma nus gsungs/ bskyed rim la brtan pa thob par rang lus mi g.yo ba'i skur gzigs/ mi g.yo ba'i bsnyen pa dung phyur dgu song / spyan ras gzigs
padma gar dbang dang / 'jam dpal brtan pa'i 'khor lo la sogs pa zhal gzigs/ pha 'ong thang du grub chen klu'i byang chub dang mjal/ chos zhu dgongs pa na mi snang par
gyur/ rang dad gus chung pa yin nam dgongs nas/ bdag byin rlabs kyi sgor bzhugs nas gsol ba btab pas/ dngos su byon nas byin gyis brlabs/ chos

bzhi tshan bzhi la sogs pa gsungs pa ni/ gnyid dang rmi lam gyi dpes/ snang ba 'di 'khrul par shes pa'i rnal 'byor/ chab dang chab brol gyi dpes/ snang stong dbyer med du shes
pa'i rnal 'byor/ bu ram gyi mi gzugs kyi dpes/ snang grags kyi chos thams cad ro gcig tu shes pa'i rnal 'byor spyod pa pha rol tu phyin pa drug la bslab gsungs/ thams
cad sems su rtogs pas chos thams cad la skur pa mi gdab sems sangs rgyas su rtogs kyang dge ba'i bshes gnyen mi spangs/ rang la 'khor ba dang ngan song gi dogs pa med kyang
sdig pa mi dge ba phra mo tsam yang spangs/ rang dang sems can tha dad med par rtogs kyang sems can thams cad la snying rje chen po mi spang gsungs/ ting nge 'dzin sems
la zhogs/ yang dag don la ltos/ byams dang snying rje bsgom/ lha sku 'ja' tshon lta bur sbyongs gsungs/ a skye ba med pa/ rlung mtshan ma med pa/ sems rang bzhin med pa/
re shig lus la brten pa yin zhes sogs mang du gsungs so/ /de nas sku mched gsum so sor byon nas/ rlung shod phyor ba sogs gnas nges med du gzhan don rgya cher mdzad/ dgung
lo drug cu la nyan du phebs/ ra sgreng btab nas lo ngo nyi shu rtsa lnga 'gro ba'i lcags mo bya lo la/ jo bo yab sras kyi lung bstan pa/ lo'i gtsug lag khang gsang ba
'dus pa'i thig btab nas rmang bting / dbu rtse khyams stod dang bcas pa dang / 'gran gyi do med lnga la sogs pa bzhengs nas de'i dus glang ri thang pa/ nyan gyi tshan par
dpon slob stong tsam dang / shar ba pa

slob ma mang po bcas te chos gsan cing / mkhar las kyi grogs mdzad pas dgon pa myur du grub/ dbu rtse'i rgyab tu sgrub chu dang / bkris mched lnga'i bla ye'i rab gnas la na
ga bho dhi dngos su spyan drangs tshul sogs kyi snyan grags kyang 'byung ngo / /lor lo brgyad bzhugs/ dge 'dun bdun brgya tsam 'dus/ lo nas snyug grum dgon par 'byon pa'i
lam du/ pha bong dkar leb bya ba'i steng nas bya yul gyi rgyab ri gzigs pas/ ri de rgyal ba'i gtsug tor 'dra/ /yan lag brgyad ldan chu bo 'bab/ /de yi shar lho phyogs mtshams
na/ /tshe dang ldan pa'i dgon gnas yod/ /ri bya yul pha gi'i thad du gtsug lags khang bzhengs nas sems can la phan pa rgya chen po gyis/ zhes lung bstan/ der zhabs
rjes kyang byon/ de nas snyug grum du lo gsum bzhugs bla ma dang yi dam mang po zhal gzigs/ nga ni tshogs yongs su rdzogs pa'i gang zag yin/ nga'i rdo rje'i gdan 'di yin
gsungs so/ /gtsang pa rin po che'i zhal nas/ bar dor mchog gi dngos grub brnyes pa'i gsungs yin gsungs so/ /dgung lo don gcig bzhes pa/ lug lo'i smin drug zla ba'i nyer
gnyis snyug grum du gshegs/ 'di la slob ma'i mchog bsgom bzhi/ 'gran gyi do med gsum la sogs pa bka' gdams gdam ngag pa'i srol 'dzin byon tshul 'og tu 'chad do/ /de yang
sku mched gsum po 'di khong rang gsum gyi gsung ltar na gnas brtan chen po bcu drug gi rnam 'phrul du byed/ rigs gsum mgon po'i sprul par byed pa ni/ lam yig las/

bal yul gyi 'phags pa shing kun la nam gyi gung mi ma yin rnams skor ba byin pa'i khrod du rdo rje phag mo'i grub pa thob pa gcig gis skor ba byas pas gling bu'i skad 'dra
ba'i glu las/ sngon dang sngon gyis dus tsa na/ /thugs dgongs bla na med pa de/ /jo bo a ti sha la yod/ /rtogs pa bla na med pa de/ /jo bo a ti sha la yod/ /da lta ma rig
'khrul par 'khyams/ /zer ba dang / yang / a ti sha yi gdung tshob pa/ /'phags pa sku mched gsum po yin/ /cig tsam lho brag mtshams na yod/ /'phags pa 'jam dpal gnyis su
med/ /cig tsam bal po'i yul na yod/ /'phags pa wa ti gnyis su med/ /cig tsam mang yul grong na yod/ /'phags pa pu gang gnyis su med/ /zer ba gsan pas de'i don ni brten de
rnams rigs gsum mgon po dngos dang khyad med pas/ de rnams gyi sprul pa yin par byed/ ces bla ma gong ma rnams kyi gsung las 'byung ba dang / yang bka' gdams glegs bam gyi
rgyal bu chags pa med pa'i skyes rabs las/ bla la chags pa med pa'i zhal nas/ sras kyi snying po chags pa med/ /bdag gi rab 'byin mgon po gyur/ /de bzhin khye 'u stong
phrag dag /lnga rdo snyigs ma ma rung tshe/ /khyed kyis srid 'dzin 'gro ba skyong / /mtha' 'khob yul gyi dbus su byed/ /rin chen phreng ba bstan pa'i dpal/ /nor bu rtsegs
pa bzhin du skyong / /sa bcu'i mgon po 'jam pa'i dpal/ /bstan pa rin chen gsal bar byed/ /sa bcu'i dbang phyug spyan ras gzigs/ /ston pa'i rgyal

mtshan 'dzin par byed/ /sa bcu'i dbang phyug rdo rje 'dzin/ /tshul khrims me lce rab 'bar te/ /'chal pa'i bud shing bsreg par byed/ /ces gsungs pas kyang rigs gsum mgon pa'i
sprul par grub pa yin no/ /de ltar bshes gnyen ston pa la/ las can gyis slob ma brgyad cu tsam/ mtsho la padmas brgyan pa ltar byon pa las/ chos kyi brgyud pa 'dzin pa'i
mchog 'phags pa sku mched gsum yin no/ /gsum pa de las 'phel ba'i slob brgyud byon tshul la gnyis/ po to ba nas brgyud pa/ bka' gdams gzhung pa'i slob ma rnams byon tshul/
rje spyan snga nas brgyud pa bka' gdams gdam ngag pa'i slob ma rnams byon tshul lo/ /dang po ni/ po to ba la spyir slob ma mang du byon kyang / grags che ba mtha' chen
brgyad/ dbus kyi nyi zla zung gcig ces pa ltar na/ gtsang du ram snang gnyis/ mnyal du gling gnyos gnyis/ dol du 'be rog gnyis/ khams su bya phag gnyis dang / dbus su glang
shar gnyis rnams yin la/ bka' babs brgyad du byed na/ bya phag gnyis mi 'dren par/ byams snying rje byang chub kyi sems bdag gzhan brje nus pa'i bka'/ glang ri thang
pa rdo rje seng ge la babs/ bka' 'gyur ro cog la gzhung bshad 'chad pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes la mnga' bsnyes pa 'dra ba yod pa'i bka'/ shar ra ba yon tan grags la
babs/ gsung rab thams cad skyes bu gsum gyi gdams ngag tu dril nas/ sman pa mkhas pas nad brtags te nad thog tu sman btang ba 'dra ba yod pa'i bka'/ snang gre'u

lhas pa ye shes rgyal mtshan la babs/ stong nyid kyi blta bas dngos po dang mtshan mar 'dzin pa thams cad 'jig nus pa yod pa'i bka'/ ram sdings ma ba 'byung gnas rdo rje la
babs/ rtsod pa paNDi ta'i rgol ba yang bzlog nus pa yod pa'i bka'/ dol pa shes rab rgya mtsho la babs/ bla ma la sangs rgyas dngos kyi mos gus rgyun chad med pa'i bka'/
gnyal pa chos 'bar la babs/ dang tshugs mchog zung cig la 'gran nus pa yod pa'i bka'/ grab pa yon tan 'od la babs/ rgyun du dkon mchog gi drung du mchod pa khra lam me ba
'bul ba yod pa'i bka'/ dge bshes brag dkar ba la babs so/ /de yang glang ri thang pa ni/ 'khrungs yul 'phan yul gnya' gong gser ma gshong / yab jo bo dar ma mdo bzang gi
sras su rta lo la 'khrungs/ rus zhugs tshangs/ khong rang gi zhang bo bshes gnyen grog mo mkhar pa la rab tu byung / mtshan rdo rje sengger btags/ rgyal ba 'od dpag tu med
pa'i sprul par byed la/ sngon lo tsA ba ka ba dpal brtsegs su sprul nas bstan pa cher gsal bar mdzad cing / 'dir gdul bya blo dman pa rnams kyi ngor/ dang po shin tu bkren
pa'i tshul mdzad de/ lo na spyan snga ba la chos gsan dus/ yos par ba res gdan non mdzad kyin bzhugs/ de nas bsod snyoms mdzad pa'i bsnyen pa gang byung spyir dge 'dun
dang / khyad par po to ba dpon slob la drangs pas/ sku bsod skyes pa ltar mdzad de/ grwa pa nyis stong tsam 'tshogs pa'i rgyags khong rang gis gnang / gnas nges med du
bshad sgrub zung 'brel

du mdzad/ gtso bor po to ba la yun ring du bsten/ phu chung ba dang / khams lung ba chen po sogs la yang chos gsan/ po to ba gshegs nas/ thang grong ltag tu gtor ma mdzad dus/
gtor sder bya rog gis khyer te glang thang gi shar ri de'u de'i khar bzhag pas/ dpon shAkya bya bas zhabs tog byas te der lo gsum sgrub pa mdzad/ zhol du sgrub chu yang
byung / nyin mtshan dbyer med du byang chub sems kyi ting nge 'dzin sgom pa'i mdangs la/ klu mo spun gsum gyis glang thang gi gnas phul/ dge 'dun gyi sde 'dzugs par zhus/
phyis ri de'i steng nas yar 'phur te/ thugs dam gyi phreng ba skyur sar khron pa brus/ dbu zhwa skyur sar bla brang byas te dgon pa btab/ slob ma mang du 'dus/ bka' gdams
gzhung drug lam sgron sogs la 'chad nyan mdzad cing / bdag gzhan brje ba'i byang chub kyi sems kho na gtso bor mdzad de/ gsung las kyang / kho bos rlung tha mal du gtong
ma myong gsungs/ zhal bzhugs rin glang thang gi lcags ri'i nang du srog chags rnams cig la cig mi 'tsho bar grags/ dgung lo bdun cu pa yos lo sa ga zla ba'i nyer gsum
la dpe'i chu lung du gshegs/ rgya lcags ri gong kha ba ni/ khams su glang ri thang pa'i snyan pa thos pas/ dbus su chos la 'byon pa'i 'dun pa yod pas/ glang ri thang pas
