mkhyen nas der byon/ bgegs bskrad/ gtor mas byin gyis brlabs pas mi'i lus su gyur/ srin mo cig gi gnod pas pho bo drug 'das/ khong rang yang sngags kyi bcings te/ khyi'i
lus su bsgyur kyang / glang ri thang pa la mjal bar mgron po'i phyi la yong /

srin mo mnan du sleb pa na/ glang ri thang pas mkhyen nas der byon/ bgegs bskrad/ gtor mas byin gyis brlabs pas mi'i lus su gyur/ stong nyid snying rje thugs su chud de slob
ma'i mchog tu gyur/ jo bo'i slob ma bshes gnyen bal po bas btab pa'i lcags ri gong khar bzhugs pas rgya lcags ri bar grags/ gzhan yang slob ma che ba dge bshes lcags zhing
ba/ khyung po rnal 'byor/ rA lo tsA ba/ gnyan chen po/ zhang zhung pa/ mdo sde pa sogs byon la/ zhang sha ra ba chen po ni/ pa tshab rom po'i rgyud du khyi lo la yum
phyugs skyong ba'i dus rdo leb steng du 'khrungs te/ de la zhabs rjes kyang byon/ dgung lo bco brgyad la rlung shod phyor bar bros te rab tu byung / mtshan yon tan grags
su btags/ de nas spyan snga phyor phur sku 'tshams mdzad pa'i sar mjal/ zla ba bzhi mtshams khrod du bzhugs te chos gsan/ da nga'i grogs po'i rtsar rgyugs gsungs pas/ stag
lung du po to ba'i spyan sngar byon/ grwa pa lo dgu nang mi lo dgu ste bco brgyad bsten/ zhar la phu chung pa dang / spyan snga la 'dod chos rdzogs par gsan/ po to ba gshegs
nas/ yon tan gyi rjes su 'brang ba'i 'khor rnams dang lhan cig thog mar rlung shod du byon te tshogs bsdus/ de nas gnas nges med du 'chad nyan mdzad pas/ grwa pa nyis
stong brgyad brgya tsam 'dus/ de rnams phal cher chos don du gnyer ba sha stag go /de yang bshes gnyen ston pa/ rnal 'byor ba/ dgon pa ba/ sku mched gsum pa/ sne'u zur
pa/

sha ra ba rnams la bka' gdams zhal brgyad du grags so/ /ram sdings ma ba 'byung gnas rdo rje ni/ khong la rnam thar che chung gsum 'byung ba'i skye ba bcu drug pa'i rnam thar
du bdag nyid ting nge 'dzin la mnyam par bzhag tsa na/ bskal pa stong gi skye ba dran te/ yab yum/ bla ma dang / chos gang la bzhugs pa/ rus dang rigs dang / gnas dang
sa phyogs thams cad kyang dran/ dus rgyun du sa le ba ni/ skye ba bcu drug dran no zhes gsungs la/ gtsang du ram sdings ma ba yi chos sde btab/ gzhi bdag gi mdzo mo dkar
mo cig phul ba sa la thim pas/ chu mig khyad par can zhig byung ste/ rgya gar gyi mda' chu khron pa skyes dang khyad med sus 'thungs kyang rgyal gsungs/ lho brag sdings
ma ba de'o/ /dol pa shes rab rgya mtsho ni/ jo bo dol du phebs dus yul 'di nas byang chub sems dpa' rtags mtshan can zhig 'byung / zhes lung bstan te/ phag lo la 'khrungs/
zhogs ya gad kyi gtsug lag khang bzhengs/ be'u bum sngon po'i rtsa tshig sogs mdzad/ dol pa dmar gzhung du grags te/ 'khor nyis stong tsam 'dus/ bdun cu rtsa gsum pa phag
lo rgyal zla'i tshes bcu gsum la gshegs/ slob ma che ba bde gshegs phag mo grub pa sogs byon kyang / chos brgyud 'dzin pa'i mchog lha don stong pa dang / de'i slob ma
'bri sgang pa sogs yin no/ /lha don steng pas be'u bum sngon po'i rtsa tshig 'grel pa mdzad do/ /grab pa yon tan 'od ni/ 'phan yul grab tu 'khrungs/ bzhugs gnas

grab phu'i pho brang sdings te/ khong rang gzhon dus nas thos pa che bas/ dang po po to ba la chos kyi tshod ltar byon kyang / phyis mi phyed pa'i dad pa skyes te/ lkog chos
lo bcu drug gsan/ po to ba'i gsung bgros bsgrigs pa/ dpe chos rtsa 'grel mdzad do/ /dge bshes brag dkar ba ni/ spre'u lo la 'khrungs/ 'khor bzhi brgya tsam 'dus/ dpe chos
gsan pa'i ched du grab pa'i slob ma mdzad/ brgyad cu thams pa yos lo'i dgun zla tha chung gi nyer gnyis la gshegs/ de'i slob ma slob dpon byang chub snang ba pa/ de'i
slob ma grub thob gces sgom/ de'i slob ma skyer sgang pa la sogs pa byon no/ bka' babs rnams kyi nang nas zhang ston sha ra ba po to ba'i chos srol 'dzin pa'i mchog ste/
'di la slob ma'i mchog bka' babs lngar grags pa ni/ byang chub thugs kyi bka' babs bya 'chad kha ba/ byin rlabs kyi bka' babs gtul ston blo gros grags/ gzhung bshad kyi bka'
babs dam pa stabs kha ba/ rnam thar gyi bka' babs nyi ma'i 'dul 'dzin/ longs spyod kyi bka' babs rnal 'byor shes rdor ro/ /dang po bya 'chad kha ba ni/ 'khrungs yul lo
ro/ gdung rus ja/ yab 'phags pa skyabs/ yum bsod nams skyid kyi sras su sbrul lo la 'khrungs/ slob dpon dwags po gtsang 'dul la rab byung zhus/ mtshan ye shes rdo rjer
btags/ gnyal du ngor rje btsan po'i chos 'khor la byon pas/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ rngog lo tsA ba sogs sde snod 'dzin pa mang po/ grub mtha'i rnam dbye 'byed pa

gzigs pas/ chos 'tshol ba la mos te byon/ g.ye chung gi sgre dgon pa na spyan snga'i slob ma sgre pa chen po bzhugs pa dang mjal/ bsnyen rdzogs kyi mkhan po zhus pas ma gnang
/ khyad par glang ri thang pa'i slob ma lcags zhing pa la blo sbyong tshig brgyad ma gsan pas dad nas/ po to ba'i slob ma dol pa dang / sgre ba jo gdan tsha rong pa dang
/ dgas po gtsang 'dul mjal du byon pa la/ mkhas slob zhus nas bsnyen rdzogs mdzad de/ sha mi la 'dul ba gsan/ de nas yar lung du byon te bshes gnyen mang po bsten/ khyad
par glang ri thang pa'i slob ma lcags zhing pa la blo sbyong tshig brgyad ma gsan pas dad nas/ po to ba'i slob ma dol pa dang / lung snang pa gnyis lo bzhi bsten/ dol
pa la be'u bum sngon po yang gsan/ de nas dgung lo sum cu la glang ri thang pa la gtad nas byon kyang ma mjal bar/ sha ra ba zho'i khang par gnas na bzhugs pa dang mjal/
dang por tshogs chos gsan/ de nas blo sbyong rtsad chod de nyams khrid du lo dgu bskyangs pas/ bdag gces 'dzin gyi 'phri ba chod pa cig byung gsungs/ ston chos la bya yul
du byon/ sprul sku bya yul ba la gdams ngag gi skor rnams rdzogs par gsan/ 'phan yul du byon nas kyang sha ra ba yun ring du bsten/ de nas gnas nges med du thugs dam gyi
gtso bo blo sbyong la mdzad cing bka' dog pa la/ phyis 'gres bu sgom chen sdings su nyer gnas la khyod kyi slob ma 'di rnams la mar khu'i skyogs 'dren gyis ming ston byed
gsungs nas/ don bdun gyi sa bcad mdzad de tshogs chos su gsungs/ de nas mal gror byon/ 'chad kha rnying ma btab/ lo

bcu gcig tu chos gsungs pas slob ma stong tsam 'dus/ de nas mtha' phur zla ba brgyad bzhugs/ khyad par gyi sras se spyil bu ba/ ran tshan rab kyi rnal 'byor byang seng / rang
po bo dhi sa twa/ dgas po nyang sogs dang / yab sras gnyis ka'i slob ma rnal 'byor byang seng gis gro sa dgon pa btab/ gzhan yang lho pa thams cad mkhyen pa sogs mang
du byon/ bdun cu rtsa lnga pa lug lo zla ba bcu gcig pa'i tshes lnga la mtha' phur gshegs/ gdung bzhu bas thugs ljags sogs byon/ gser gyi mo tog gi char babs par grags te/
rgyas par blo sbyong gi byung tshul dang / rnam thar che chung du blta'o/ /de'i khyad par gyi sras se spyil bu ba ni/ 'khrungs yul lho stod der ma sgang / gdung rus se/
dgung snying glang lo pa/ rab byung dang bsnyen rdzogs gnyis ka'i mkhan po cha bas mdzad/ mtshan chos kyi rgyal mtshan du btags/ bya 'chad kha ba dang mjal/ yun ring du
bsten cing / yon tan bum pa gang byo'i tshul du mdzad/ sngar bya 'chad kyi lung bstan pa bzhin 'chad kha gsar ma btab/ 'chad kha pa chen po'i nang rten du sku lder rin po
che dang / phyi rten gyi mchod rten la sogs pa bzhengs nas klung shod du byon/ spyil bu'i dgon pa btab ste rnam g.yeng spangs nas/ stod du mkhar gong la ga smad du nyung
zhing snang du mtshams tho brgyabs nas/ lo bdun du mtshams mi 'da' mdzad/ de nas brag dkar gnas brtan sogs kyis spyan drangs nas 'chad khar dgun chos la byon/ gdul bya du
ma smin par mdzad nas drug cu rtsa dgu pa bya lo'i

dbyar zla ra ba'i tshes bcu gsum la spyil bur gshegs/ 'di la slob ma'i mchog lha chen po/ gya yangs pa thang pa/ nyan lha ldings pa sogs mang du byon pa las/ lha chen po ni/
yab jo bo rnal 'byor/ yum sna nam za'i sras su stag lo la pho brang khang dmar du 'khrungs/ dgung lo bco lnga la rgya dur gyi mkhan po klub dkar dang / gtsang pa khyung
po la mkhan slob zhus/ bya par rab tu byung ste/ mtshan byang chub rin chen du btags/ de nas bya 'chad kha ba'i sku 'dra gzigs pas dad pa'i rkyen byas te dge bshes se dang
mjal/ chos mang du zhus/ nyi shu rtsa bzhi la rgya sar sgang nas mkhan po rlan spyan drangs te bsnyen par rdzogs/ gzhan yang kha che paN chen la sogs pa mang du bsten/
se spyil bu ba gshegs nas/ 'chad kha spyil bu'i gdan sa mdzad/ bka' 'gyur gyi lung bzhugs pas/ lha lung gi dbang phyug tu grags/ sangs rgyas sman bla sogs yi dam mang po'i
zhal gzigs pa rnam thar du gsal/ 'brug lo bdun cu rtsa lnga la 'chad khar gshegs/ lha 'gro mgon ni/ yab jo 'bag gi sras su rta lo la 'khrungs/ lo bcu drug pa la 'chad
khar khu bo'i drung du dge bsnyen zhus/ de nas skyur mo lung du sba ti la rab tu byung ste/ mtshan dbang phyug 'od du btags/ de nas po tor dge bshes gnas brtan la mkhan po
zhus te bsnyen par rdzogs/ lha chen po gshegs nas gdan sa mdzad/ mi g.yo ba'i grub pa brnyes pas stag sham can du yang grags/ gdul bya mang po smin par mdzad nas bdun cu
rtsa bzhi pa

lug lo zla ba dgu pa'i nyer gcig la spyil bur gshegs/ lha brag kha ba ni/ jo bo shAkya bkra shis kyi sras su khyi lo la 'khrungs/ lha 'gro mgon dang mjal te rab tu byung /
mtshan ye shes blo gros su btags/ sbas pa ston gzhon sogs la chos rnams rdzogs par gsan/ 'chad kha spyil bu'i gdan sa mdzad/ sum cu rtsa bdun la gshegs/ de nas jo 'phel gyi
sras lha dbang phyug ye shes/ 'brug lo pa/ zur khang pa snga bar grags pas gdan sa mdzad de drug cu la gshegs/ de nas grags pa rin chen gyi sras lha blo gros 'od bya lo
pa/ gdan sa lo bzhi bcu mdzad de/ lha rin chen seng ge mkhan chen sengge rgyal mtshan sogs smin par mdzad/ drug cu rtsa bzhi la gshegs/ mkhan chen sengge rgyal mtshan pa'i
sku che ba'i yon tan rnams/ jo bo brtan sgom dpal gyis byas pa'i rnam thar du gsal la/ de la slob ma rje btsun ye mgon pa/ byang sems ra sgreng pa shAkya bsod nams sogs
mang du byon no/ /rgya yangs pa thang pa ni/ gdung rus rgya/ mtshan nyi ma dbang phyug spang pa'i dgon pa btab/ dgung lo lnga bcu bzhugs/ de nas gdan sa yang mang du nyan
lha sdings pas nyan gyi lha sdings btab/ blo sbyong gi bla ma brgyud par ram pa lha sdings pa zhes 'byung la/ stod lung mdar ram pa lha sdings zhes pa'i dgon pa yod pas/
'di dang bla ma gcig mi gcig brtag par bya'o/ /ram pa lha sdings pa nas/ sangs rgyas dbon/ slob dpon yon tan dpal/ mkhan chen bde pa dpal/ mkhan chen bka' bzhi ba/ rin
po che

bsod grags pa/ rgyal sras thogs med pa ste/ de rnams kyi rnam thar chos rje mtshal min pa bsod nams bzang pos mdzad par gsal lo/ /byin rlabs kyi bka' babs gtum ston blo gros
grags ni/ gdung rus gtum/ 'khrungs pa lcags mkhar ste/ sha ra ba sogs bka' gdams kyi bla ma mang du bsten/ de nas snar gyi mda'i thang la lo ra yod par spyil bu mdzad de/
chu mo bya'i lo la gzhi btsugs snar thang gi dgon pa btab ste/ lo bcu bzhi bzhugs/ grwa pa stong tsam 'dus pa'i grags che pa rdo ston rdo rje grags/ bdud rtsi grags zhag
btsun rdo rje 'od/ sga ston shes rab grags rnams las rdo rton rdo rje grags la nyid kyi dgon pa 'di bzung la 'gro don skyongs gsungs nas/ khong rang byang rta sde'i chos
lung du thugs dam la bzhugs te/ chos lung sku gshegs su grags/ rdo ston gyi gdan sa lo nyi shu mdzad/ de nas zhang btsun rdo rje 'od kyis gdan sa lo brgyad mdzad/ dpal
ldan gro mo che ba ni/ gdung rus gro/ 'khrungs yul chu sgo ba/ mtshan bdud rtsi'i grags/ yi dam mang po dang gnas brtan bcu drug zhal gzigs/ snar thang gi dbu rtse rnying
ma bzhengs/ gdan sa lo sum cu so dgu mdzad/ de nas zhang ston chos kyi bla mas gdan sa lo bcu mdzad de/ de nas sangs rgyas sgom pas gdan sa lo bcu mdzad de/ tshogs chos
chen mor grags pa dang / lam sgron TIkka sogs mdzad cing / dben gnas byang chen btab/ gnyal zhig gi slob ma grags pa sengge spyan

drangs te mtshan nyid kyi bshad grwa btsugs/ de nas 'chim nam mkha' grags pa zhes bya ba/ gdung rus 'chim/ nyang stod smon gro'i shu kha'u bya bar sku 'khrungs/ gnas brtan
bcu drug gi gcig tu grags/ mkhyen rab dang 'phrin las che bas rtsom chos mang du mdzad cing / gdan sa lo sum cu rtsa drug mdzad/ chos rgyal 'phags pa'i bla ma yang mdzad
nas/ chos 'khor chen po cig gi gral dbu la spyan 'dren zhus/ de nas skye ston par grags pas gdan sa lo bco lnga mdzad de/ snar thang gi gtsug lag khang che ba dang lcags
ri sogs mdzad/ de nas chos rje nyi ma ba/ mkhan chen 'dul ba 'dzin pa/ 'chim blo bzang grags pa sogs dpal snar thang du bka' gdams pa'i bshes gnyen bzang la mang ba rim par
byon pa yin no/ /gzhung bshad kyi bka' babs dam pa stabs kha bas/ stabs kha grwa pa'i sgang / 'dod 'jo chos kyi sgang / khra phu longs spyod kyi sgang ste dgon pa gsum
btab/ grwa pa brgyad brgya tsam 'dus/ grags che ba'i zhang bzhi ni/ zhang ston 'dod 'jo ba dar ma g.yung drung / zhang ston khang mo che ba/ zhang ston sho ma ra ba/ zhang
ston gtso thang pa chen po'o/ /thugs kyi sras bzhi ni/ sgang thang dkar ba rdo rje rin chen/ gu ra ba tshul khrims rdo rje/ stabs kha'i rnal 'byor pa nam mkha' rin chen/
khra phu ba 'dul ba 'dzin pa'o/ /'dod 'jo zhang ston dar ma g.yung drung la gtad/ de nas rong ston kha po ches bskyangs so/ /khra phu 'dul 'dzin pas bskyangs te/ de las

'phel ba'i zhang ston dar/ grab phu ba chen po/ de'i slob ma btsan dgon pa ba sogs byon te rgyas par ma spros so/ /gnyis pa rje spyan snga nas brgyud pa bka' gdams gdam ngag
pa rnams byon tshul ni/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug spyan snga la slob ma'i mchog sgom bzhi/ 'gran gyi do med gsum dang / gzhan yang mkhar phu ba/ rol po rdo rje/ g.yo nas
sgre pa chen po/ zhang ston dpal brtsegs/ rgya rtse sgro ba/ 'phan yul gyi sgro lag pa chen po/ zhang ka ma ba chen po shes rab 'od/ ku ma ra shAkya/ sku srung ston pa/
'dul 'dzin la gur ston pa/ 'chang bu ba chen po/ dgag dbye shes rin sogs ming chen nyi shu rtsa lnga tsam byon pa'i dgag dbye shes rin gyi nyan cher sgyes kyis mchod khang
bzhengs/ spyir grwa pa bdun brgya tsam 'tshogs pa'i sgom bzhi ni/ zar pa zag sgom rdo rje ye shes kyis mal gro zar gyi mchod khang bzhengs/ rug pa ston sgom gyis klung
shod rug pa'i mchod khang bzhengs/ mang ra sgom pa brtson 'grus 'bar gyis thang skya'i dgon pa btab/ dbu rtse gsar ma bzhengs/ ral pa seng sgom gyis rlung shod ngor gyi
mchod khang bzhengs/ 'gran gyi do med gsum ni/ ston lung pa chen po/ bya yul ba chen po/ snyug grum pa chen po'o/ snyug grum pas klung shod mdar snyug grum dgon pa btab/
stod lung pa chen po ni/ 'khrungs yul stod lung gser phug dgung snying spre'u lo pa/ rab tu byung pa khyung po jo bsod la mdzad/ mtshan rin

chen snying por btags/ gtsang phyogs la gzhon nu nas mtshan nyid kyi slob gnyer la byon nas/ bla ma seng ge sgra gcan 'dzin bzang po dang / paNDi ta 'bum phrag gsum pa sogs
mkhas pa mang po la mdo sngags kyi gsan sbyong rgya cher mdzad/ rtsod pa yang bzang / de nas stod lung thag mar/ dbus gtsang gi ston chen thams cad 'tshogs nas chos kyi
bgros gleng 'ba' zhig mdzad pas/ khong gis kyang grwa skor la byon/ rtsod pa mdzad pas/ klo kya gtso rgan bya bas nyan nas/ khong na re bod dbus gtsang gi ston chen 'di tsam
cig nyin re bzhin 'tshogs nas/ mar 'khor ba yong lugs/ yar thar pa sgrub lugs kyi chos tshig bzhi pa cig med par/ klad pa gas gas ba glang dkar zal la 'chi ba 'di byung
re che zer ba gsan pas/ khos kyang de tsam cig go 'dug na/ da rgya gar du chos 'tshol ba la 'gro dgongs nas byon pa dang / mkha' ru ba'i grwa ba dge slong snam sbyar phrag
par bzhag pa tshul khrims kyi dri bro ba cig dang mjal te/ tshe 'di yun thung shes bya'i rnam pa mang / /tshe yi tshad kyang ji tsam mi shes pas/ /ngang pa mtsho la
'o ma len pa ltar/ /rang gi 'dod pa dang du blang bar bgyi/ /zhes gsungs/ de sus mdzad byas pas/ jo bo'i gsung yin zer/ gang nas byon byas pas/ mkha' ru dgon pa nas 'ong
zer bas/ mkha' rur byon/ skyabs 'gro'i chos skor gsungs pa gsan/ de nas mkha' ru bas lung bstan nas/ ra sgreng du rnal 'byor pa chen po'i spyan sngar byon/ lta ba'i dri ba
mang po mdzad pas/

ston pa sngon du thabs goms pas rgyu smin dgos pa yin gsungs nas thog mar skyabs 'gro dang / byams snying rje nas rim gyis khrid de chos mang du gsan no/ /de nas spyan snga
sku mtshams la bzhugs pas/ rnal 'byor pas mjal sna mdzad de chos gsan/ rtsa ba'i bla ma zhus/ de nas rnal 'byor pa lo dgu/ dgon pa ba lo lnga bsten/ spyan snga lo bdun 'bral
med du bsten te bka' gdams kyi chos thams cad rdzogs par gsan/ gser srang brgyad brgya 'bul bar dam bcas te/ phyed phyag tu phyin pa la spyan snga gshegs pas/ bzhi brgya'i
tshab tu dgung lo don gnyis la/ lam pa'i gtsug lag khang gi rmang btings te rdzogs par grub/ sku gsung thugs kyi rten snga phyi dpag tu med pa bzhengs pa'i grags che
ba la/ rab gnas kyi dus su spyan snga pa la chos gsungs pa'i/ 'jam dpal dpa' bo'i sku la sogs pa/ rgyud sbyangs ma bdun dang / rnal 'byor pas rab gnas mdzad pa/ po to'i
gsung 'byon/ mkha' ru'i ljang skyes/ btsan 'gro'i chu khol zhes/ rten rtags thon gsum du grags pa sogs rten mang du bzhengs/ spyan dang mngon par shes pa mnga'/ yi dam
mang pos zhal gzigs/ bden gnyis kyi rtogs pa thugs la 'khrungs/ 'gro don rgya cher mdzad de/ slob ma rtogs ldan sdings po ba snub chos 'bar/ dge bshes lha bzo/ khyung khams
po che/ klog skya/ dge bshes zar pa/ bya 'dul 'dzin/ dge bshes gnas brtan la sogs pa rtogs pa dang / gzhan phan

la mnga' brnyes pa mang du byon no/ /de nas stod lung pa/ dge bshes lha bzo la gdan pas gtod dgongs pa la/ lha bzos mngon shes kyi rig nas/ gram rta chad skad par bzhugs pas/
glen pa lha bzo de byung na bslab bya 'dra bya rgyu yod pa yin te ma byung / da dge bshes klog skya dang / zar pa gnyis kyi 'di dang mal gro zar gnyis spyi la skyong gsungs/
der yod pa rnams kyi rjes su rten bzhengs sogs ji ltar byed zhus pas/ spur 'di g.ya' phu ru'i rtse la skyol/ rten ma bzhengs gsungs/ 'o na sprul sku bya yul ba rten
bzhengs pa 'dug na ji ltar byed zhus pas/ nga khong la drin che ba yin/ lo bdun 'gro ba nas bskyangs/ bla ma spyan snga rnal 'byor lta bu la sprad/ khong rang ji ltar dgongs
pa mdzad du chug gsungs/ de nas sku gshegs khar/ ngas don khyad par can grub pa yin/ zhes lan gsum gsungs/ drung na yod pas/ yi dam gyi lha zhal gzigs pa yin nam zhus
pas/ yi dam kyi lha zer nas mig hu re/ rna ba co re ba yod pa yin/ chos thams cad don dam par skye ba med cing / kun rdzob tu rmi lam sgyu ma lta bur rtogs gsungs te/
brgyad cu rtsa lnga pa spre'u lo mngon par byang chub pa'i zla ba'i tshes brgyad la lam pa dgon par gshegs/ sang lha bzo dpon slob kyis kyang phebs/ nya ga mo pas mdangs
ma gir bzhugs pas ma byung zhus pas/ tshe dang ldan pa/ mi theg pa'i khur chen po cig bkur bar 'dug pas bsdad pa yin/ bla ma dang 'dang mjal/ bzod gsol kyang tshar gsungs/

der klog skya'i zhal nas/ nga rgas pas ya gir mi thon/ khyod kyi zar skyongs gsungs/ zar pa'i zhal nas/ nga yang bla ma'i gdan sa dga' ste/ ngas zar bskyangs shig gsungs/ de
nas bya yul ba chen pos kyang phebs/ sngar gyi zhal bkod rnams snyan du gsol pas/ gzhi 'di la zan kyi dgos pa'i dgongs pa yin yong gsungs te/ chas rkyen thams cad dang
/ sol ba tshun chad dbu stod nas drangs te gdung khang chen po bzhengs so/ /sprul pa'i sku bya yul ba ni/ mdo ting 'dzin gyi rgyal po las/ phyi ma'i tshe na ting nge 'dzin
pa dag /lnga brgya las ni mi nyung de 'byung ste/ /mdo sde mchog 'di rgya cher bzung ba la/ /de dag sngon du 'dren pa gzhon nu yin/ /zhes lung bstan te/ 'khrungs yul stod
lung go ga lung gi grong mkha' rog gdung rus gnyos/ yab g.yung drung 'bar/ yum stod lung pa'i lcam sring ljang za lcam bu ste/ yos lo la 'khrungs/ dgung lo bdun la ston
lung pa chen po dang mjal/ lo bcu gnyis la stod lung tsha thog dgon par/ rnal 'byor pa'i slob ma sgom pa byang grags dang / spyan snga'i slob ma sgom pa ye shes rgyal mtshan
gnyis la mkhan slob zhus dge tshul mdzad/ mtshan gzhon nu 'od du btags/ de nas stod lung pa/ mal gro zar du 'byon pa'i phyag phyir byon/ lo bcu zhabs tog tshul bzhin
du mdzad/ thugs 'dzin yangs pas bslab spyod gzhung che chung rnams tshegs med par thugs su chud par mdzad/ de nas spyan snga cho ba na bzhugs pa

na/ stod lung pa dpon slob gnyis kyis mjal du byon pas mngon shes kyis gzigs nas stod lung pa la/ jo bo ston pa re skyed 'khor 'di lta bu yod pa/ shes yang yang gsungs pas/
bla ma mnyes par dgongs te phul/ lo bcu gsum zhabs tog tshul bzhin du mdzad pas/ spyan snga mnyes pa'i gsung mang po dang / byin rlabs zhugs te/ nang ma gcig la sde snod
gsum dang / rgyud sde bzhi'i tshig don thugs la 'khrungs/ spyan snga la dpon slob nA ga bo dhi dang mjal ba bden nam zhus pas/ btsun chung 'di 'dir bcug pa'i chos mi 'dra
ba gsungs/ phyi gshegs khar ngas slob dpon nA ga bo dhi dang dngos su mjal/ chos mang du zhus/ rtsa ba'i bla mar byed pa yin/ khyod rang yang gsol ba thob dang rjes su
'dzin par 'dug gsungs/ mdor na spyan snga'i yon tan bum pa gang byo'i tshul du mnga' zhing / spyan snga snyug grum du gshegs nas sku gdung bzhu ba'i dus/ thugs nam mkha'
la 'od dang bcas ste sprul sku chen po'i pang par babs pa/ phyis bya yul gyi gdung khang du bzhugs so/ /snyug grum du sku mtshams lo dgu mdzad/ de nas tshogs bsdus te/ thog
mar bul gyi ra ba dkar por dgon pa btab/ dge 'dun lnga brgya tsam 'dus/ de'i tshe rje btsun ma sgrol ma la sogs pa yi dam mang po zhal gzigs/ nA ga bo dhi la dngos su
chos gsan/ de nas gdul bya bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / dgon pa 'bul ba yang mang du byung ba la/ bla ma dang sgrol mas lung bstan pa'i gnas bya

yul du dgon pa 'debs dgongs kyang / yon bdag rnams the tshom bsal ba'i phyir/ bshes gnyen mtha' bzhi spyan drangs te/ dgon pa thams cad nas rdo re blangs pa la sa spyad mdzad
pas/ se g.ya' ba'i g.yung drung gi phul ba bya yul nas blangs pa'i rdo la sa'i spyad bzang bar lung bstan pas/ gzhan rnams kyang ma dga' ba med par mdzad de/ lo dgon pa
btab nas lo ngo nyi shu rtsa gnyis pa chu pho rta'i lo la gtsug lag khang gi rmang btings nas lo bcu gsum rta lo'i nang tshun la dgon pa rdzogs par grub/ de'i tshe spyan
snga ba mnal lam du byon nas/ snam sbyar gser mdog can bskon pa rmis pas/ bla mas snang ba byung gsungs nas/ mkhan po bya 'dul 'dzin/ las slob mang ra sgom pa/ gsang ston
rgya shes rab 'bar gyis mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/ bya yul du dge 'dun nyis stong lnga brgya tsam 'dus/ de dus bya yul/ klung shod/ mal gro gsum du dus gcig la gral dbu
mdzad pa dang / mdo smad du ngang tshang ba'i gtsug lag khang gi rab gnas dang / dwags por sha ba gling pa'i mchod rten gyi rab gnas zhus pas/ dus tshod tshes grangs 'di
la mchod pa rgya chen po bshoms/ gsol ba thob/ ngas gzims chung 'di'i steng nas rab gnas byed pa yin gsungs te/ kun gyis mthong bar gtsug lag khang dang / mchod rten steng
du phyag nas babs pas/ de nas sprul skur grags/ mi ma yin mang po la chos gsungs pa dang / bskyed rdzogs kyi

rtogs pa mnga' ba/ mngon shes mang du gsungs pa sogs don du gnyer na rnam thar che chung dang / gtsug lag khang bzhengs tshul rgyas par rten bshad kyi yi ger gsal lo/ /de ltar
slob ma mang du smin grol la bkod/ 'gro don rgya cher mdzad de dgung lo drug cu rtsa bzhi pa rta lo la bya yul du gshegs/ de nas gzhi byes kyi grwa pa mang pas/ sku gdung
bzhugs pa dang bzhu ba la ma 'chams pas/ sku stod rdo rgyus kyis pang khebs kyis dril nas/ sku smad bzhu phul bas spur dud kyis gang khyab tu ring bsrel 'byung ba dang
/ dung g.yas 'khyil/ sgrol dkar/ rnam rgyal mchod rten rnams byon no/ /sprul sku chen po la slob ma nyis stong re 'dus pa'i nang nas ting nge 'dzin skyes pa lnga brgya/
dge bshes jag rtse 'chang ba brgya dang bcu/ de'i nang nas grags che ba/ phyi'i chen po brgyad/ nang gi che po brgyad/ thugs kyi sras bzhi dang / rje sgam po par grags
pa dwags po lha rje sogs pa byon pa'i/ phyi'i chen po brgyad ni/ mdo smon nas ngang tshang pa chen po/ grags mar chen po/ dwags por sha pa gling pa chen po/ lhor lha rgya
ri ba dang / dge g.yel ba chen po/ stod lung du rnam par ba dang / nya ga mo pa chen po/ dkon mchog 'od zer/ gtsang du mus sman pa chen po dang brgyad do/ /nang gi chen
po brgyad la/ khrom zher chen po 'brug lo pa/ mtshan rin chen 'od/ skam skam dang / brag par sogs dgon pa mang du btab/ don gcig bar bzhugs so/ /snyug grum

pa chen po ni/ snga phyi gnyis byung pa'i phyi ma yin no/ /mal gror bul pa chen po ni/ rus klog skya/ dgung steng yos/ mtshan dbang phyug rin chen/ bya yul ba chen po dang
thog mar 'brom du mjal/ rgyal steng gi dgon pa btab/ don grub bzhugs so/ /sku 'jol pa chen po'am/ ba ngar ba chen por grags pas/ ba ngar gyi mchod khang bzhengs/ 'phan yul
du rta pa zhang sgom chen pos rta phu'i dgon pa btab/ 'brom du bkra shis sgang pa chen pos smon grong gi dgon pa btab/ rgya mig mang pa chen po dang brgyad do/ thugs kyi
sras bzhi'am lnga ni/ rgya par sgang nas/ rgya chen pos rgya par sgang gi mchod khang gsar rnying gnyis bzhengs/ 'phan yul char rje nas snub mchod nas/ dgon mkha' ru ba
la gsum byon pa'i bar pa dang / gtsang pa rin po che dang bzhi/ sras lngar byed na/ sgyer sgom chen po gcig yin la/ dpe kha cig tu/ nang gi chen por bgrang pa yang snang
bas/ mi 'dra ba cung zad 'dug kyang rnam thar gtso bor byas so/ /dwags po lha rje ni snying rje pad dkar du/ dge slong 'tsho byed ces bya ba theg chen pa 'byung / zhes lung
bstan te/ 'khrungs yul mnyal bdo gnyer gnyi ba/ dbu rtso rgya la 'bar gyi sras su sa mo lugs la 'khrungs/ dgung lo nyer lnga la dwags por mar yul blo ldan dang / shar
pa gling pa la rab byung bsnyen rdzogs zhus/ mtshan blo gros grags par btags/ bka' rgyud gser phreng du/ skya ming dar ma grags dang / chos mtshan bsod nams rin chen zer/
de nas

bya yul ba/ sha pa gling pa/ dge bshes sgre ba/ snyug grum pa/ rgya lcags ri gong kha ba dang lnga la bka' gdams gsan/ de nas sgrub pa bya dgongs nas khong rang gi yab mes
kyi brtsigs pa'i gser kha bya ba'i gtsug lag khang yod sar brang khang brtsigs/ pha zhing la yon bdag byas te sgrub pa byed pa'i dus/ nyin cig lcags ri'i lho phyogs su skyo
sangs la byon pa na/ sprang po gsum las/ rje btsun mi la'i snyan pa gsan pas/ dad pa'i rkyen byas te/ pha zhing gser zho bzhi dang cha zho gang la btsongs nas/ dge bshes
rgya lcags ri ba dang / bya yul pa/ snyug grum la rnams la phyi phyag mdzad pas/ bya yul ba'i zhal nas/ khyed rnal 'byor pa khyi thul can gyi spyan sngar ma 'gro cis kyang
'gro na nged kyi rtags rnam thar ma dor ba shog cig lar ser kha la phan na khyi tshil yang sman yin/ zangs nged kyi brdungs nas zangs skad mi yis 'don pa cig 'ong bar
'dug ste/ thabs med gsungs/ snyug grum pa'i zhal nas/ khyod kyi nga rgas khar ma bor ba shog cig gsungs/ de nas mi la dang mjal gdams ngag gi thugs tshim par mdzad/ 'phrin
las mtha' yas shing / dgas lha sgam por dgung lo brgyad cu bar du bzhugs shing / rnam thar rgyas pa bka' brgyud gser phreng sogs su gsal lo/ /'di dag bka' gdams kyi brgyud
pa dngos su mi 'dzin kyang / bka' phyag zung 'brel bas grags pas slob ma'i khongs su gtogs pa yin no/ /de nas lo bya yul gyi gdan pa rim par byon

pa'i tshul ni/ spyan snga rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug sku gshegs nas/ lor gnas brtan gyi bu gzhon nu smon lam gyis gdan sa lo dgu de nas rtogs ldan sdings po ba snub chos 'bar
gyis gdan sa lo gsum/ de nas gnas brtan smon lam blo gros kyis zla ba bco brgyad byas/ yang sdings po bas lo drug dril bas lo dgu mdzad/ bdun cu rtsa brgyad lor gshegs/
de nas gtsang pa rin po che byon nas gdan sa mdzad do/ /bya yul du sprul sku chen po gshegs nas/ dge bshes rgya spre'u lo pas gdan sa lo lnga mdzad/ drug cu rtsa bzhi pa
rta'i zla ba'i nyer brgyad la bya yul du gshegs/ de nas snub mchod gnas khyi lo pa gzhon nu rgyal mtshan gyis lo nyi shu rtsa bzhi mdzad/ brgyad cu rtsa drug pa mngon par
byang chub pa'i zla ba'i tshes brgyad la bya yul du gshegs/ de nas lo brgyad gdan sa ba med pa'i rjes la/ lor gtsang pa rin po che'i rjes su rin po che glang lung pa bzhugs
pa/ mal gro 'dar ston mo'i gral dbu nas bya yul du gdan drangs/ de nas bya yul gyi gdan sa sbrel ba'i srol byung ngo / /gtsang pa rin po che ni 'khrungs yul gtsang
gi rngubs yul rol/ gdung rus snub/ yab snub a la la/ yum ral chags bzang lcam gyi sras su 'brug lo la 'khrungs/ mtshan nam mkha' rdo rjer btags/ dpe kha cig tu rdo rje rgyal
mtshan zhes pa yang snang / rten tshangs spyod kyi dge bsnyen mdzad/ gzhon nu'i dus nas chos thams cad rmi lam sgyu ma'i nyams dang / mkha' 'gro mang po zhal gzigs/ de
nas gnyan lo

tsA ba rgya gar nas byon pa dang mjal te/ mdo sngags kyi thos pa rgya cher dang / khyad par sngags la mkhas par sbyangs/ bod kyi mkhas pa mang po la ni ngas thug da rgya gar
du 'gro dgongs te/ ding rir dam pa mjal bar byon pas/ chos mi gsung par brda chos bzhi mdzad pa'i cig rdo dkar po shar phyogs su 'phangs song pa/ dam pa kun dga' la dris
pas khyod kyi yongs 'dzin shar na yod zer ba'i brda yin zer bas/ lha sar jo bo mjal ba dang / yer par sgrub pa la byon pas/ bya yul ba chen po 'brom smon grong du chos
bar la byon pa'i chos nyan pa mang po dang 'phrad de/ sprul sku bya yul ba la chos nyan du 'gro zer/ de la yon tan ci yod byas pas/ gzhan ni ma shes/ bla mas byin gyis brlabs
pa cig yin par 'dug zer/ khong gis kyang tshod blta ba'i phyir/ chos ra'i mthar bzhugs pas/ sems la phan pa mang du byung ste/ mjal bas mi phyed pa'i dad pa 'khrungs/
phyag phyir bya yul du byon nas lo bcu bzhi bsten/ bka' gdams kyi chos thams cad rdzogs par gsan/ yi dam mang po zhal gzigs/ chos nyid kyi bden pa mngon sum du gzigs/ phyis
lor byon pa la mkha' 'gro ma dung phreng can mang pos bsu ba mdzad de/ rdo rje gdan gyi chos skyong dang gcig par snang gsungs/ dgung lo re gcig la dga' ldan du byon
pa'i mnal lam byung pas/ sgrol ma dkar mo'i sgrub pa mdzad/ lo'i gdan sar lo bco lnga bzhugs te/ brgyad cu rtsa lnga pa zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes brgyad la lor

gshegs/ 'di la slob ma dge bshes 'gar la sogs pa bu bzhi dang / tshe blos thongs pa bcu bzhi la sogs pa byon te 'dir ma spros so/ /de'i slob ma rin po che glang lung pa/ 'khrungs
yul stod lung tshur bu/ yab rdo rje grags kyi sras su yos lo la 'khrungs/ lo bcu dgu la/ pa tshab lo tsA ba las rab tu byung ste/ mtshan brtson 'grus gzhon nur btags/
zur chos pa gcig la 'dul ba mkhas par bslab/ nya ga mo ba la lo bdun lam rim khrid tshar gcig bskyangs pas/ ji ltar 'dod pa bzhin blo bkol du btub pa byung gsungs/ nyer
bdun la snon gyi gyad par bya 'dul 'dzin/ cha pa chos seng / btsun pa chos mchog gsum la bsnyen par rdzogs/ de nas lor gtsang pa rin po che lo lnga bsten/ chos mang du
gsan/ dad gus tshad med pa 'khrungs pas rtogs pa bzang po mang du 'khrungs la/ sngon du lo'i gdan sa lo bcu gnyis dang / de nas lo bya yul sbrel nas lo drug ste bco brgyad
mdzad/ bdun cu rtsa lnga pa la bya yul du gshegs/ glang lung pa'i dus su chos rje 'jig rten mgon po bya yul du byon te/ khrom sher dang gnyis la bka' gdams kyi chos gsan
pa'i dus su/ de gnyis kyi slob ma skyo rin po che la nged dben gnas byon pa'i sa cig dgos gsungs pas/ gzho'i phu na 'bri phyugs 'jog pa'i se nags yod pa phul/ dgon pa
btab te 'phrin las rgyas pa'i tshul gzhan du gsal lo/ /glang lung pa'i rjes su se rnal

'byor pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan 'khrungs yul gzhung / yab se shes rdor kyi sras su 'khrungs/ glang lung pa'i phyag phyir yun ring bzhugs/ bla mchod pa lo 'ga' dang / lo bya
yul gyi gdan sa lo dgu mdzad nas/ grog gi dbye phu dgon pa btab pa'o/ /sangs rgyas sgom pa ni/ 'khrungs yul gzhung / yab 'be spyan ras gzigs kyi sras su 'brug lo la 'khrungs/
lo bcu bzhi la 'dul ba 'dzin pa sbal ti'i sar rab tu byung / mtshan rdo rje gzhon nur btags/ de nas lo bco brgyad la glang lung pa stod lung du byon pa dang mjal/ lo
bcu bzhi bsten/ rtogs pa khyad par can 'khrungs/ de nas la mo lha khang du lo drug sku mtshams mdzad/ so brgyad la ra mo cher mkhan po sbal ti la bsnyen rdzogs zhus/ 'dul
ba mkhas par bslabs/ lor byon nas zhe bzhi la lo bya yul gyi gdan sar byon/ glang lo bar bdun cu bzhugs/ zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes bzhi la lor gshegs/ de nas gtsang pa jo
sras kyi lo dgu mdzad/ lo'i dbu rtse gsar ma bzhengs/ zem rin po che ni/ yul ha ma mdo'i de'u gong bya ba/ phag lo la yab pa yag rtse mo'i bur 'khrungs/ lo bcu bdun la lor
sangs rgyas sgom pa'i spyan sngar byon pas/ sngon la gro sar song gsungs nas rnal 'byor byang seng la rab byung zhus/ mtshan grags pa seng ger btags/ 'dul ba dang / jo
bo nas brgyud pa'i chos mang du gsan/ lo lnga bzhugs/ yar lam rin chen sgang du sangs rgyas dbon la chos zhus/ de nas ha ma mdor lo bzhi sgrub

pa mdzad pas sangs rgyas padma gar dbang zhal mjal/ de nas bya yul du sangs rgyas sgom pa la tshogs chos/ lkog chos thams cad rdzogs par mdzad/ thugs dam bum pa dbu thog tu
bzhag pas ting nge 'dzin khyad par can 'khrungs/ ra sgreng du byon dus jo bo 'jam dpal rdo rjes chos gsungs/ lo bya yul gyi gdan sa lo bco brgyad mdzad/ drug cu rtsa drug
pa 'brug lo zla ba gnyis pa'i nyi shu la glang lung du gshegs/ 'di la slob ma'i mchog bzang po drug tu grags pa'i/ ri mer ba chen pos lho ri mer gyi dgon pa btab/ 'od gsal
sgang pa ni/ 'khrungs yul 'on bra ma thang / don steng pa la rab byung zhus/ gro sar rnal 'byor byang seng la 'dul ba sogs bslabs/ phar 'byon par chas pa la/ sna ra sman
rtsar zem phebs pa dang mjal bas mi phyed pa'i dad pa skyes/ lo dgu bsten/ 'dis zhogs kyi 'od gsal dgon pa btab bo/ smad kyi byang chub sems dpa' zla ba rgyal mtshan/
'dis dum bu ri'i dgon pa btab/ gzhan yang dwags po spyi ther 'bri sgang pa/ chos rgyal khams lung pa rnams byon/ khams lung pa'i 'khrungs yul nyan ka ka ba/ gdung rus dbas/
yab rnal 'byor mgon po'i sras su 'brug lo la 'khrungs/ byis pa nas zem rin po che lor phar 'byon mar 'byon mdzad pa dang mjal res kyis sems phrogs pa bzhin byung / lo
bcu gnyis la zem bya yul du bzhugs pa la rab byung zhus/ mtshan rin chen seng ger btags/ de nas phyag phyir lo bdun bzhugs/ tshogs chos rnams rdzogs par gsan/

zem kyi zhal nas/ khyod nga'i yon tan 'di rnams rtsad chod/ bsnyen rdzogs gyis gsungs pas/ zem lam dgon du phebs pa la skyor mo lung gi mkhan po zhig po bya ba mjal du byung
dus bsnyen rdzogs dang / 'dul ba yang gsan/ de nas zem la lkog chos rnams zhus/ ma 'ongs pa na 'di ltar gyis ka lung bstan mang po mdzad/ zem gshegs nas/ ri yer pa gdan
sar spyan drangs kyang / khyed rang gi pha gi na 'os pa cig chos skyong gi bdag tu bzung 'dug gsungs nas lung bstan mdzad de ma byon/ khong yu nga'i khams lung du bros te
de nas spyan drangs pas/ mtshan yang de ltar grags/ nyi shu rtsa lnga la gdan sar bskos nyi shu rtsa bdun mdzad/ lo'i mched khang gi khyams smad/ gling bskyed pa/ gser
thog sogs bzhengs pas bka' drin che zhing / lnga bcu nga gnyis pa rta lo zla ba gnyis pa'i nyer lnga la ka phug tu gshegs/ yar lung jo bo'i chos 'byung du 'di'i dus su bka'
gdams kyi bshes gnyen grags che ba thus chen brgyad du grags pa byung zhes bshad do/ sangs rgyas jo bo ni 'khrungs yul rgya sar sgang / yab lha'i brgyud pa jo bo bsod
nams mgon gyi sras su sbrul lo la 'khrungs/ gzhon nu nas sangs rgyas sgom pa shar phyogs dang ba'i 'od kyi 'jig rten na bzhugs zer ba'i dbyangs 'then pa gsan pas mtshan thos
pa tsam gyis dad gus skyes/ bcu gnyis la zem glang lung du bzhugs pa la rab byung zhus/ mtshan dbang phyug gzhon nur btags/ nyi shu rtsa gnyis la zem la mkhan po zhus
te bsnyen par

rdzogs bka' gdams kyi chos la sogs pa gsan sbyong mdzad/ lnga bcu rtsa gnyis la lam dgon gyi gdan sar byon lo dgu mdzad/ drug bcu la lo bya yul gyi gdan sar byon pa'i dus mngon
shes mang du gsungs bya yul gtsug lag khang dang / gling gi zhig gsos sogs mdzad de bka' drin lhag par che zhing / bla ma yi dam chos skyong mang po zhal gzigs/ gdan
sa lo bco brgyad mdzad/ bdun cu don bdun bya lo dbyug gu zla ba'i tshes bcu bar du bzhugs/ sangs rgyas ston pa ni/ 'khrungs yul lho brag gru shum sgo/ yab sum pa bkra shis
kyi sras su byi ba lo la 'khrungs/ bcu bzhi la khams lung pa'i drung du rab byung zhus/ mtshan tshul khrims seng ger btags/ nyi shu la mkhan po dge g.yo ba la bsnyen par
rdzogs/ 'dul ba mkhas par mkhyen/ de nas lo bya yul gyi chos skyong rnams kyi bsu ba byas pa'i snang ba byung ba dang dus mtshungs par/ sangs rgyas jo bos shog gsungs
te bya yul steng khang du bskos/ jo bo chen po zhal gzigs/ de nas gdan sar byon te lo bcu drug mdzad/ lo bya yul du chos khrims shin tu dam pa dang / bka' gdams kyi srol
bzang po btsugs/ glang lo bar drug cu rtsa gnyis bzhugs/ sangs rgyas sgom pa gsar ma 'khrungs yul lo ro thu shul/ yab sum pa brgyad stong dpal gyi sras su 'brug lo la 'khrungs/
gzhon nu'i dus mtsho sna pa la dge tshul zhus/ mtshan tshul khrims shes rab tu btags/ de nas bya yul du byon nas sangs rgyas jo bo dang ston pa la

bsnyen rdzogs zhus/ bka' gdams kyi chos rdzogs par gsan/ khyad par du sangs rgyas ston pa la sngags kyi rdzogs rim gsan pas/ 'od gsal kyi rtogs pa 'khrungs/ de nas lam dgon
gyi gdan sa lo gsum mdzad dus thugs skyo ba cung zad skyes te sham po gangs la bzhugs pa/ lo bya yul gyi gdan sar spyan drangs nas lo bcu gsum mdzad/ nga dgu pa stag lo
bya yul du gshegs/ sangs rgyas dbon po gzhon nu smon lam dgas por spre'u lo la 'khrungs/ dwags po spyi ther gyi dbon por grags/ rgyal steng gi gdan sa lo mang rab dang /
de nas gdan sa gong lo gsum mdzad/ bdun cu rtsa gnyis pa lug lo zla ba gnyis pa'i tshes brgyad la lor gshegs/ rin po che bcu bzhi pa rlung sho sho nag thang bya bar/ yab
seng ge'i sras su yos la 'khrungs/ gdung rus rtsi/ lo bco lnga la lug rur sangs rgyas jo bo la rab tu byung / mtshan tshul khrims mgon por btags/ lo bzhi bsten/ tshogs chos
rdzogs par gsan/ bcu dgu la brag tshab tu bsnyen rdzogs mdzad/ de nas skyor mo lung dang / thang sag du 'dul ba dang dbu ma mkhas par sbyangs/ sangs rgyas ston pa lo bcu
gsum bsten/ lkog chos rdzogs par gsan/ yi dam zhal gzigs pa/ mngon shes mnga' ba sogs rnam thar du gsal/ 'khor rnams la nged yan chad du bka' brgyud 'di la dam tshig dang
lta spyod la lhad dang zegs med/ byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa ma nyams/ nyams rtog rgyun chad med pa yin pas/ khyed zhabs rtog byed pa don

dang ldan pa yin gsungs/ bya yul gyi mkhan po lo gsum/ lam dgon gyi gdan sa lo brgyad/ gdan sa che ba lo nyi shu rtsa gnyis mdzad de/ bdun cu rtsa gcig pa glang lo zla ba dgu
pa'i tshes bcu bzhi la lor gshegs/ stod lung pa rin chen snying po'i sprul par grags so/ /rin po che gnam gang pa 'khrungs yul 'ol kha/ gdung rus byen/ yab chos skyong
bsam me'i sras su khyi lo la 'khrungs/ lo bcu gcig la rgyas steng du sangs rgyas dbon po la rab tu byung / mtshan gzhon nu ye shes su btags/ mkhan chen cha ru ba la 'dul
ba/ spyod 'jug gdams ngag skor mang du gsan/ bcu dgu la rin po che tshul khrims mgon po la bsnyen rdzogs zhus/ nged kyi gzims g.yog bgyis/ zin bris thob gsungs pas de ltar
mdzad de/ tshogs lkog gi chos rdzogs par gsan pas/ thugs rab la mnyes te blo gros rnams dag ces gsungs/ lo nyer drug la rgyas stengs su bskos bco lnga mdzad/ de nas rin
po che bcu bzhi pas/ thub pa'i gser sku/ dbu zhwa/ stan rim sogs gnang nas byin gyis brlabs/ bzhi bcu la gdan sar byon lo so bzhi mdzad/ don gsum pa khyi lo zla ba gnyis
pa'i gnam gang bar du bzhugs/ rin po che tshes bcu pa 'khrungs yul 'ol kha gdung rus ljang / yab dpon dkar gyi sras su 'brug lo la 'khrungs/ lo bcu bzhi la rin po che bcu
bzhi pa rab byung zhus/ mtshan chos kyi rdo rjer btags/ nyer gcig la bya yul du rin po che de nyid kyi drung du bsnyen rdzogs

mdzad de/ dal dang 'byor pa brnyed dka' bas/ /'di dag ji lta bzhin du sgrubs/ /gsungs pa'i skabs su thugs la nges shes skyes te/ tshul khrims mig 'bras bzhin du srungs gsungs/
bcu bzhi pa lo dgu bsten/ bka' gdams kyi chos rdzogs par gsan/ gsang sngags kyang mnos te/ 'dul mngon/ spyod 'jug sogs mkhas par sbyangs/ byes kyi mkhan po lo gsum/ rgyas
stengs spyan pas sbrel ba lo nyi shu rtsa brgyad/ gdan sa gong lo brgyad mdzad/ bde mchog sogs zhal gzigs pa/ mgon po lho nub pa bran bzhin du 'khol ba sogs rnam thar
du gsal/ bdun cu rtsa gsum pa dgun zla tha chung gi tshes bcu bar du bzhugs/ rin po che bco brgyad pa dgung snying yos/ zhogs su 'khrungs/ rin po che gnam gang pa la rab
byung bsnyen rdzogs zhus/ mtshan blo gros rin chen du btags/ 'od gsal gyi gdan sa lo bdun/ gdan sa gong lo brgyad mdzad de/ bzhi bcu rtsa drug pa byi ba lo dpyid zla ra
ba'i tshes bco brgyad bar du bzhugs/ rin po che rin chen rgyal mtshan/ yab lhas pa dpon rdor gyi sras su gro bzhir byi ba lo la 'khrungs/ rab byung dang bsnyen rdzogs rin
po che gnam gang pa la zhus/ mgon po gri gug zhal gzigs/ bla ma bco lnga bsten/ gdan sa lo nyi shu rtsa gsum mdzad/ lnga bcu rtsa dgu pa khyi lo zla ba dang po'i tshes
bco lnga bar bzhugs/ yongs 'dzin chen po tshul khrims dar gyi zhal snga nas/ yab dpon bsam 'grub dang / yum sog mo rdo rje sgron gyi sras su shing pho stag la lcas bar

'khrungs/ dgung lo bcu gsum la gugs rdzong du slob dpon tshul rgyal ba la rab tu byung / mtshan tshul khrims dar du btags/ nyi shu rtsa lnga la rin po che chos kyi rdo rje'i
drung du bsnyen rdzogs/ skyor mo lung du slob dpon bsam gtan don grub dang / gro sar mar ston dbu ma pa sogs la 'dul ba'i sde snod mtha' dag la mkhas par sbyangs/ mkhan
chen sangs rgyas dpal ba dang / chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa sogs las/ sher phyogs byams chos mtha' dag thugs su chud par mdzad/ thang sag tu zla grags gsar ma dang / slob
dpon tshul dpal ba la dbu ma'i gzhung che chung mtha' dag gsan/ rin po che rin chen rgyal mtshan sogs bla ma lnga'i drung du bka' gdams kyi chos skor rnams dang / chos
rje kun bkras pa sogs la sa lugs kyi chos skor dang / zha lu grags pa rgyal mtshan pa la bu lugs kyi chos bskor dang / gdan sa thel du chos rje bsod nams rgyal mtshan pa
la phyag rgya ba'i chos bskor dang / rtogs ldan sngo nyal ma dang / drung rin rgyal ba la dus 'khor rgyud 'grel sogs la mkhas par mdzad/ mdor na mkhas grub kyi bla ma sum
cu tsam bsten te/ bde bar gshegs pa'i gsung rab mtha' dag gi tshig don la mnga' brnyes par mdzad de/ mkhas pa'i grags pas phyogs kun khyab/ 'chad nyan sogs gzhan phan rgya
cher mdzad de/ slob ma'i mchog chos rje dge ba rgyal mtshan/ zad pa blo rgyam/ zad pa padma bzang po/ chos rje blo brtan pa/ khams su lha 'bri

ston pa sogs mang du byon/ sher phyogs gsungs ba'i tshe me tog gi char 'bab pa/ yi dam dang chos skyong zhal gzigs pa sogs rgyas par rnam thar du gsal la/ lor byes pa mkhan
po lo lnga/ gzim 'og lo gsum/ gdan sa gong lo bcu bdun mdzad/ bdun cu don lnga pa 'brug lo zla ba bcu gcig pa'i nyer drug bar du bzhugs/ rje bsod nams lha'i dbang po ni/
byams mgon gnyis pa rin po che tshul khrims dar las bsnyen rdzogs mdzad de/ bka' gdams kyi chos bskor phal cher gsan/ rong ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ byang ra sgreng pa sems
dpa' chen po shAkya bsod nams/ ra sgreng pa rin chen grags pa/ chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan pa/ dwags po 'jam dbyangs bkra shis rnam rgyal/ dus zhabs don grub kun dga'/
bka' 'gyur ba shAkya rgyal mtshan sogs yongs 'dzin mang du bsten nas mdo sngags rab 'byams kyi dbang lung khrid man ngag sogs kyi gsan pa dpyis phyin par mdzad cing
/ dpal lo dgon pa'i spyan snga lo mang du mdzad/ dgung lo don drug gi bar du spyir bstan pa dang / khyad par bka' gdams kyi bstan pa ches cher gsal bar mdzad cing bzhugs
so/ /spyan snga ngag dbang chos kyi grags pa ni/ yab stong dpon 'phags pa dpal dang / yum spyod yul mtsho gnyis kyi sras su lcags mo glang gi lo sku bltams/ bsod nams lha'i
dbang po las rab tu byung / mtshan ngag dbang chos grags rgyal mtshan dpal bzang por btags/ 'jam

dbyangs kun dga' chos bzang las bsnyen par rdzogs/ mkhan po de nyid dang / chos rje blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rje mkhyen rab rin chen mchog grub/ snyug la paN chen ngag dbang
grags pa/ sngags 'chang rin chen rnam rgyal/ mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa/ rje byams pa chos kyi nyi ma/ bdag chen ngag gi dbang phyug sogs bla
ma mang du bsten nas mdo sngags rig gnas kyi bsdus pa'i chos tshul rgya mtsho lta bu'i pha mthar gson/ thugs dam la gcig tu gzhol bas nyams dang rtogs pa'i dbang phyug
tu gyur/ snyigs dus kyi bstan pa'i gsal byed chen po sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen yab sras sku mched sogs kyi bka' gdams kyi chos bum pa gang
byor gsan pa'i bla mar bsten/ lo bya yul sogs bka' gdams kyi dgon gnas rnams kyi gdan sa sku tshe ril por mdzad/ spyi dang bye brag gi bstan pa yar ngo'i zla ba ltar
rgyas par mdzad de/ dgung lo brgyad cu rtsa dgu pa sbrul lo smin drug zla ba'i nyer lnga'i nyin bde bar gshegs so/ /de lta bu'i skyes chen dam pa de nyid kyi sku'i rnam par
sprul pa bdag gi bla ma spyan snga rin po che byams pa kun dga'i mtshan can 'di nyid ni/ lug lo bkra shis pa'i dge mtshan dang bcas nas sku 'khrungs/ mkhas grub kyi bla
ma du ma las gsan pa rgya mtsho'i pha rol du gson te/ lung dang rtogs pa'i yon tan bsam gyi mi khyab pa'i mnga' bdag tu gyur/ lo dang bya yul sogs bka'

gdams kyi dgon grwa chen po rnams kyi gdan sa mdzad bzhin par da lta dgung lo lnga bcu rtsa gnyis kyi steng na bzhugs pa 'di nyid ste/ yongs 'dzin dam pa 'di nyid kyi rnam
par thar pa rgyas pa ni logs su 'chad par sha chags pas 'dir ma spros so/ /bdag cag gi yongs 'dzin dam pa 'jam mgon grub pa'i dbang phyug bsod nams dbang po dang / yab rje
sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa'i mtshan can/ khyab bdag 'khor lo'i mgon po rje btsun mus pa chen po sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen
pa ngag dbang chos grags rnams kyi ngo mtshar ba'i mdzad pa'i cha shas mtha' dag ni sngar nas logs su bshad cing / 'chad par gyur pa'i rnams thar kyi yi ge byas pa dag las
khongs su tshud par bya zhing / 'dir skabs su babs pa dge pa'i bshes gnyen bka' gdams pa rnams nas brgyud pa'i chos tshul rnams bdag gi bla ma so sos gsan pa dang / rang
nyid kyis ji ltar thos pa'i tshul mdo tsam brjod na/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang pos ni spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags dang / yab sngags 'chang chen po gnyis las bka'
gdams pa'i chos rnams rdzogs par gsan zhing / sngags 'chang grags pa'i mtshan can gyis rang gi yab sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen gyi drung
du rgyas par gsan la/ rje btsun mus pa chen po dang mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags gnyis kyi/ lo nas spyan snga rin po che'i ngag dbang chos grags kyi

dngos slob paN chen nam mkha' dbang phyug dang / 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya mtsho sogs kyi drung du bka' gdams thig le bcu drug gi dbang khrid/ gzhung drug gi lung / chos
chung brgya rtsa/ lha bzhi'i khrid/ rin spung bskor gsum/ bka' gdams glegs bam yongs rdzogs/ blo sbyong gi skor sogs mtha' chod par gsan zhing / de ltar 'jam pa'i dbyangs
sku mched dang / rgyal ba mus pa chen po sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ spyan snga kun dga' don grub/ mkhan chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs ngag dbang chos grags/ gzhan yang brgyud ldan
gyi bla ma yid ches can du ma'i drung du sa skya pa sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po bdag gis dge ba'i bshes gnyen bka'
gdams pa nas brgyud pa'i chos skor rnams dwang 'dod yid ches kyi dad pa bla na med pa'i sgo nas 'bad rtsol chen pos rdzogs par mnos shing / lhag par sngon jo bo chen po
dpal ldan a ti shas 'brom ston pa la thugs kyi sras gcig pu lta bur mdzad pa ltar dus gsum sgrib med du gzigs pa'i rje btsun mus pa chen po de nyid kyis kho bo cag la thugs
rje'i spyan ras kyi bu gcig pa ltar 'tsho bar mdzad pa'i skal ba mchog kyang thob pa lags/ gong du smos pa'i stod lung pa'i slob ma la grags che ba sdings bu ba/ klog
skya/ dge bshes zar pa/ dge bshes lha bzo ba/ khyung khams/ bya 'dul 'dzin dang drug las/ stod lung pa'i dgongs pa lon pa phyi ma gsum

yin te/ lha bzos mngon shes lnga thob/ stod lung pa 'khor lo bde mchog dang gnyis su med par gzigs gsungs/ khyung khams kyi sgyu lus kyi rtogs pa brnyes/ stod lung pa'i zhal
nas/ khyod kyi gdul bya gtsang du yod pas der song / dgon pa thob/ slob ma bsdus la bden gnyis shod/ nga'i bden gnyis 'di ma dor cig gsungs pas/ khyung khams gtsang la
'byon khar/ bden gnyis dang khyung khams gtsang la bzhud/ bden nam mi bden/ pha bong 'phen g.yag la dris gsungs nas phyag mkhar brdabs pas tshal par gas/ de nas nyang ro
tha mtshal du byon nas sdings bu dgon pa'i rmang btings/ bden gnyis chos tshan bcu gnyis su bsdus pa gsungs/ gzhan phan bskyangs pas slob ma mang du 'phel lo/ bya 'dul 'dzin
ni 'khrungs yul gtsang rong g.yung gi nang gi snya pa/ yab bya rgyal ba la sras gnyis yod pa'i gcung po/ lcags mo lug la 'khrungs/ gzhon nu'i dus rong mnar mda' tsha
dmar gyi gtsug lag khang du 'bre shes rab 'bar/ chos gzhi la byon pa dang mjal du byon pas/ phar phyin gsungs pa'i lam shes kyi skabs su sleb chos gsan pas/ lha'i me tog
gi char 'bab pa mthong / dad pa skye pas/ yab la zhus pas/ rab tu byung / mtshan brtson 'grus 'bar du btags/ 'bre'i zhal nas/ rab tu byung bas 'dul ba bslab dgos pas thog
par 'dul ba slobs gsungs pas/ ldan du sog tshul khrims bla ma/ de nas rgya 'dul 'dzin dang /

rma tsho la 'dul ba gsan cing mkhas par gyur/ de nas rgya tsha zhang ye la dbu tshad dang / dkar lo tsA ba la yo ga bslabs/ 'go nas bshad nyan mdzad pa'i skabs su dpe cha rnams
khams pa'i grwa pas brkus pas/ thugs skyo ba skyes te stod lung pa'i drung du bka' gdams zhu ru byon pas/ yon tan che ba'i nga rgyal gyis dang por phyag ma byas pa sogs
spyod pa 'ga' zhig la rten nas/ stod lung pa'i bka' bkyon drag tu mdzad de bskrad/ der log nas byon/ stod lung zam khar bslebs pa na 'gyod pa skyes te/ chos zhur 'ong
pa la de ltar byed pa nga ma bden snyam du dgongs pa dang / stod lung pa'i zhal nas nye gnas la/ da kho 'gyod pa skyes nas 'dug gi mar gdan drongs la shog gsungs/ gdan drangs
bkur bsti byas/ der bka' gdams kyi gdams ngag thams cad yongs su rdzogs par gsan nas thugs dam gyi gtso bo mdzad do/ /de nas zul phur bshad grwa btsugs te tshogs lo
dgu'i bar du bskyangs/ mdo rtsa'i TIkka che chung dang 'dul pa spyi'i rnam gzhag mdzad/ de'i tshe bsam yas dpe dkar gyi bar chad rtsom pa'i phyir btsun par sprul nas zhabs
tog lo mang du byas kyang / 'dul ba dang 'gal ba'i mdzad pa na bza'i spu phyir bstan te gyon pa tsam ma gtogs skyon ma brnyed pas dpe dkar yang dad par grags so/ /de ltar
bka' gdams kyi man ngag la nyams len mdzad/ bu chen 'dul ba la mkhas shing 'gro don phun sum tshogs pa bdun cu rtsa drug

byung pa'i nang nas/ dbus kyi bu chen gsum ni/ ka pa dar seng / rnal 'byor byang seng / rje mo chos seng dang gsum/ gtsang nas gtsang ngu rin skyabs/ rtsis pa gzhon nu seng
ge sogs byon/ de ltar bstan pa'i bya ba rgya cher mdzad/ dgung lo bdun cu don drug bzhes pa la zul phur sku gshegs/ gdung bzhu bas thugs ljags ring bsrel sogs mang du byon
no/ /de nas sgyer sgom chen po nas brgyud pa cung zad bshad na/ dang po yar lung 'phyong rgyas kyi bang so padma can bya ba/ yon bdag nyi ma mgon gyi sras/ sgyer shes
rab skyabs zer ba dbu ru snon mda'i rog snar yul 'chugs/ btsun mo tshal stod nas klu lcam bya ba khab tu bzhes/ sras gsum byung ba/ khre la stag bu mo stag khre la dar ro/
che ba khre la stag rab tu byung ste/ sgom pa shes rab grags zer/ chung ba khre la dar dgung lo bcu gnyis la snon phu gnyer du/ sprul sku bya yul bas mkhan po mdzad/ zhang
snying phug pas slob dpon mdzad nas rab tu byung ste/ mtshan gzhon nu grags su btags/ dgung lo bcu bdun la sne'u zur du byon lo dgu bzhugs/ sne'u zur pa gshegs nas bya
yul pa chen po lo lnga bsten/ bka' gdams kyi chos skor rdzogs par zhus/ slob ma brgyad brgya tsam byon pa'i nang nas grags che ba/ sba bya zur dang gsum/ dge bshes g.yor
ston/ skyis ston/ lho brag ston pa/ dmar ston/ khams ston/ ston pa 'od zer bla ma/ smon lam bzang po/ ston pa

gzhon legs sogs byon/ sangs rgyas dbon ston ni 'gran gyi do med yin no/ /me mo bya la ra sgreng btab nas lo drug cu re gnyis song nas/ sa mo phag la rin chen sgang gi gtsug
lag khang rnying ma bzhengs/ bla ma'i gdan sa la sgo bton gsungs nas bya yul phyogs su bstan/ jo bo mi g.yo ba/ dam tshig gsum bkod/ jo bo 'jam dpal rdo rje'i zhal gzigs/
sne'u zur pa dang / bya yul ba'i gsungs bgros sgang bsos nas/ lam rim po ti bzhi ma dang / gnyis ma bya ba sangs rgyas dbon ston sogs la gnang bas/ sangs rgyas dbon ston
gyis zin bris su btab/ gdan sar lo lnga bcu bzhugs/ gya gnyis la gshegs/ sangs rgyas dbon ston ni/ sgyer sgom chen po'i spun zla sgyer bu mo stag zhes pa dang / yum sha
mo rdog ge'am/ sha mo 'do le zhes pa la sras gsum byung ba'i che ba yon bdag ya po zhes pa dge 'dun dang dkon mchog la dad pa cig byung / bar pa sangs rgyas dbon ston/ chung
ba slob dpon ston pa/ khong gis chos skyong gri gug zhal gzigs/ sangs rgyas dbon sprul sku bya yul ba'i sku skyer byed pas/ sgyer bsgom gyi zhal nas/ ngas bla ma'i gsung
gcig la brten nas btsun chung 'di la byams par byas pa yin gsung / sangs rgyas dbon dgung lo bcu bdun la dge bshes 'ban thang pas mkhan po/ dwags po bang rim pa 'de'u
bsgom gyis slob dpon mdzad de rab tu byung / mtshan gzhon nu 'byung gnas su btags/ lo bcu dgu la skyi smad

du byon/ dge bshes nyang ran dang / dge bshes kha ches mkhan slob mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/ 'phan yul mdar ka ba dar seng la 'dul ba dang / gzhan yang sde snod mang du gsan/
/de nas lo bco brgyad kyi ring la sgyer bsgom rang bsten nas gsung rab mtha' dag dang / lung man ngag rdzogs par gsan/ yi dam chos skyong dpag tu med pa zhal gzigs/ rgya
ma'i dbu rtse gsar ma bzhengs pa dang / rin chen sgang gi gling rgya bskyed pa/ phyogs kyi gtsug lag khang dang / rten gsum mang po'i rab tu gnas pa sogs 'gro don rgya
che zhing / sangs rgyas skal ldan shing rta zhes par 'gyur bar zhal gyis bzhes/ spyan ras gzigs kyi sprul par yang grags/ rgyas par don du gnyer na/ khu dpon gyi rnam thar
thun mong ba che ba gcig dang / mchod khang bzhengs tshul bkra shis leb brgyad ma bya ba lho pa dbu ma pa zer ba'i slob ma cig gi byas pa dang / ri bo maNDal rtser byon
pa'i rnam thar rnams su gsal lo/ /slob ma rtogs ldan bzang mo ba/ nags spo ba/ zung chu spo pa/ nag mo sang yon dang mo bzhir grags pa rnams so/ gdan sar lo bzhi bcu bzhugs
te bdun cu don gnyis pa smal po zla ba'i tshes bzhi la rgya ma gnas su gshegs/ rtogs ldan bzang mo ba ni/ yul dwags po brad lha sa ba/ gdung rus spyil/ yab rnal 'byor
jo stag la sras gsum yod pa'i 'bring po/ mtshan gzhon nu seng ge zer/ byis pa'i dus dwags po sgam po ba la phyag rgya ba'i khrid 'ga' dang / bya yul ba'i slob

ma bo thang ba la bka' gdams kyi chos skor dang / pu gu dor sa chen gyi slob ma gshen rdo rje seng ge la sa skya pa'i chos skor gsan/ bcu dgu la gem chung du zhang ban la bsnyen
rdzogs mdzad/ de nas sangs rgyas dbon blo mda' grong mo che na slob ma mang po la bka' gdams kyi chos skor gsung ba dang mjal bas dad de nyi shu rtsa brgyad nas rin
chen sgang pa'i grwa pa mdzad yul ring du bsten/ bka' gdams kyi chos rdzogs par gsan/ de nas bsam yas phu'i bzang mo dgon pa btab/ bdun cu rtsa bdun pa cho 'phrul zla ba'i
tshes bzhi la bzang mo dgon par gshegs/ khong gi slob ma jo gdan lhas phu bas/ lhas phu dgon gsal dang / lha dge 'dun sgang pas dge 'dun sgang btab/ gzhan yang 'phan yul
zong dgon pa sogs byung / nags mo bas/ byon gyi nags mo dgon pa btab/ zung chu mo pas 'phan yul mda'i zung chur dgon pa btab te/ phyis spos pa grab kyi sas khang yin no/
gong du smos pa sne'u zur pa las 'phel tshul ni/ sne'u zur pa/ gdung rus btsos po/ spras mthong pa sar bya lo la 'khrungs/ byis pa'i dus nas ting nge 'dzin rang 'khrungs
su mnga'/ rab tu byung nas mtshan ye shes 'bar du btags/ dgon pa ba sku mched gsum la sogs pa bla ma mang du bsten/ dgon pa ba dang thog mar mjal ba'i dus/ thugs kha nas
thub pa'i sku 'od 'phro ba cig byon nas sne'u zur pa la thim pas ting nge 'dzin khyad par can skyes/ bla ma la gus pa/ byang

chub kyi sems gnas pa brtan pa/ sgyu ma lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin rnams 'dzom na/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' dpag tu med pa zhal gzigs pa chos nyid yin gsungs/ gzhan
yang sgyu lus kyi rtogs pa brnyes pas/ rang lus mi g.yo ba'i skur ldang nus pa dang / mngon par shes pa rgya chen po mnga' zhing / dgon pa ba dang / sku mched gsum gyi
gsung phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa'i bstan rim mdzad/ dgung lo don drug bzhugs/ gdung bzhus pas ring bsrel dpag tu med pa dang / lha'i spos kyi dris sne'u zur gyi gnas thams
cad khyab pa sogs rnam thar du gsal lo/ /slob ma bdun brgya tsam byung ba'i nang nas grags che ba bzhi ni/ lha bka' gdams pa/ thag ma pa chen po/ byang sems zla ba rgyal
mtshan/ dgun pa lha rje thugs rje rgyal mtshan rnams dang / gzhan yang gtsang nas grang po lung pa zhes 'phags pa don zhags dang / bcu gcig zhal gyi chos bdag tu byed pa
dang / spyi bo lhas pa byang chub 'od ces grags pa rnams so/ /'di rnams bka' gdams gdams ngag pa gtso bor byed pas de'i phyogs su gtogs zhes yar lung jo bo'i chos 'byung
du 'byung ngo / /spyi bo lhas pa la chos kyi rje sa skya paNDi tas rab byung bsnyen rdzogs kyi slob dpon zhus/ bka' gdams gzhung gdams ngag gi chos rnams gsan par/ rnam
thar ngo mtshar snang ba las gsungs te/ thag ma pa'i slob ma/ nam mkha' seng ge yang stod lung thag mar byon/ de nas nam mkha' rgyal po/ seng ge bzang po/ rgyal

sras bzang po/ gsang ba'i bdag pos byin gyis brlabs pa nam mkha' rgyal mtshan dang bzhi ni lho brag thig phyir byon no/ /yang bka' gdams gzhung pa'i brgyud pa/ se spyi phu
ba yan sngar bzhin la/ de nas lha lung gi dbang phyug dang / 'gro mgon gyi slob ma zangs chen pa dar ma bsod nams/ de'i slob ma mtsho sna pa chen po shes rab bzang po/ de'i
slob ma mon grab pa tshul khrims bkra shis/ de'i slob ma mkhan chen chos skyabs bzang po'o/ /yang mkhan chen chos skyabs pa dang / gsang bdag nam mkha' rgyal mtshan gyi
drung du rje blo bzang grags pas bka' gdams gzhung gdams ngag gi chos rnams gsan nas gro lung pa'i bstan rim la gzhi mdzad de/ byang chub lam sgron gyi don 'grel lam rim
che chung brtsams te bka' gdams pa'i brgyud 'dzin du nan gyis 'jug par mdzad do/ /jo bo a ti sha'i sras kyi thu bo gnyis pa/ rngog lo tsA ba'i bshad brgyud 'dzin pa ni
gangs can gyi ljongs 'dir bstan pa spyi la bka' drin che bas/ de'i byon tshul sngon gyi yi ge las 'byung ba bzhin bshad na/ kha ba can gyi ljongs 'brog tsho dang nye ba'i
sar/ sngags rnying ma ba'i dge bshes rdo rje gzhon nu bya ba la/ sras lnga yod pa'i che shos rngog legs pa'i shes rab kyis/ spyir jo bo chen po lo bcu bsten cing phyag phyir
byon pa'i dus su/ gsang phu la phyag mdzub btsugs te/ lung pa ya gi'i nang na dung g.yas su 'khyil ba 'dra ba yod/ der legs she khyod kyis gtsug lag khang thob la/ bshad

nyan gyis/ bstan pa la phan par 'gyur/ zhes lung bstan pas/ gsang phu ne'u thog gi sa cha gzigs te/ bla mas lung bstan pa'i gnas de yin par mkhyen nas/ gsang phu ne'u thog
gi gtsug lag khang bzhengs/ bstan pa'i bya ba mdzad de/ dang por dge 'dun lnga brgya tsam 'dus so/ /de las 'phros pa la gnyis/ lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab las slob ma 'phel
tshul/ mnga' ris pa shes rab rgyal mtshan las bka' gdams glegs bam byung tshul lo/ /dang po ni/ legs she'i gcung po klung khri/ klu byang / chos skyabs/ thub pa bzhi las/
chos skyabs kyi sras lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab yin te/ de'ang lcags mo phag gi lo la sku 'khrungs/ skyes bu dam pa des sku na gzhon nu'i dus nas/ khu bo dang / bka'
chu'i slob chung tshul khrims shes rab la sogs pa bsten nas rab tu byung / rgyud sbyangs/ dgung lo bcu bdun lon pa'i dus/ mnga' ris stod kyi lha bla ma byang chub 'od kyi
dbon po mnga' bdag rtse ldes/ rgya gar du lo tsA slob pa la brdzangs te yul dbus dang kha che la sogs par byon/ paNDi ta pad rdza na dang / 'bum phrag gsum pa/ pa ra he
da ma hA dza na/ su ma ti kirti dang / skal ldan rgyal po la sogs pa mkhas grub mang du bsten/ rgya bal du lo bcu bdun bzhugs nas/ mnga' ris stod du phebs/ mnga' bdag dbang
lde dang / khri bkra shis dbang phyug btsan gyis 'gyur gyi sbyin bdag mdzad nas/ tshad ma rgyan la sogs pa bstan bcos mang du bsgyur/ de nas dbus su phebs/ khu bo'i gdan

sa gsang phu ne'u thog dang / ra sgreng la sogs pa gnas khyad par can mang por chos gsungs/ slob ma khri phrag lhag tsam 'dus par grags shing / dbus gtsang / lho bal/ mdo stod
smad/ shar btsong kha/ rgya mi nyag sogs su grub mtha' 'dzin pa'i slob ma dang / nying slob tu ma gyur pa med cing / dbus gtsang du lo bcu bdun 'gro don mdzad/ rgyas
par gro lung pas mdzad pa'i rnam thar du shes so/ /de'i thugs sras zhang tshe spong chos kyi bla ma/ zhang grong lung pa blo gros 'byung gnas/ khyung rin chen grags/ 'bre
shes rab 'bar bzhi la sras kyi thu bo bzhi zer/ gzhan yang gangs pa she'u/ gung bu rwa can/ sham po mi tig la sogs pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa smin par mdzad pa'i nang nas/
zhang tshe spong chos kyi bla mas ne'u thog gi gdan sa lo sum cu so gnyis mdzad/ de'i rjes gnyal ba ri lus lo gnyis/ rnam par bas lo brgyad mdzad/ de nas gro lung pa gdan
sar gdan drangs pas/ grogs chos kyi spyan ldan de'i gdan sa dron mo la shes 'dod yod kyang / ral ril thams cad kyi rjes su mi byed gsungs pas/ gong gi bla ma de gsum gyi
slob ma dge ba'i bshes gnyen cha pa chos kyi seng ges ne'u thog gi gdan sa lo bco brgyad mdzad cing / slar yang gro lung pa'i spyan sngar byon nas sgro 'dogs bcad de/ slob
ma bsam gyis mi khyab pa byon pa las/ sras kyi thu bo seng chen brgyad ni/ gtsang nag brtson 'grus sengge / dan 'bag smra ba'i sengge / bru nag

bsod nams sengge / rma bya rtsod pa'i sengge / rtsegs dbang phyug sengge / nyang ran pa chos kyi sengge / ldan ma dkon mchog sengge / gnyal pa yon tan sengge ste/ 'ga' zhig
gtsang pa 'jam seng 'dren no/ /jo sras bzhi ni/ 'khon jo sras rtse mo/ rngog jo sras ra mo/ khu jo sras ne tso/ snyos jo sras dpal le rnams so/ /yang 'gar dbang grub/ kong
po 'jag chung / lho pa sgog zan/ yar phu ba blo gros sengge bzhi la shes rab can bzhi zer/ gzhan yang 'jad pa ston skyabs/ rdo rje 'od zer la sogs pa sde snod 'dzin pa
mang po dang / tshur phu ba grub thob dbu se/ zhang tshal pa/ chos rje phag mo grub pa la sogs pa mkhas grub du ma smin par mdzad pa'i nang nas/ rtsegs dbang phyug sengges
gdan sa lo lnga/ de gnyis kyi slob ma gnyal pa dad pa bzang pos lo bdun/ 'jam rtse nas lo bdun byas/ 'di nas gling stod smad gnyis su gyes par 'dod do/ /smad pa la zad
pa dar ma 'od dang / zad pa don grub gnyis kyis lo sum cu mdzad/ de nas slob dpon 'od zer mgon pos lo sum cu so lnga gdan sa mdzad pa la/ slob ma slob dpon shAkya gzhon
nu/ don grub dpal/ kha rag pa la sogs pa byon pa'i shAkya gzhon gyis gdan sa mdzad de/ de nas rim pa ltar byon no/ /gling stod pa ni/ 'jam rtsi ni'i slob ma gtsang pa 'jam
seng / de'i rjes su 'dzin ston zhus ston/ blo gros 'bar rnams rim par byon/ de nas slob dpon gnyal zhig 'on byang rdo nas spyan drangs te gdan sa

lo bco brgyad mdzad cing / slob ma bu dgur grags pa ni/ zad ring / phu dar dkon/ gtsang pa glu gu rnams la snga tshar ba gsum/ 'u yug pa bsod nams sengge/ bo dong rin chen
sengge/ slob dpon 'dzam nam gsum la bar tshar gsum/ rgya 'phreng / 'jam gsar/ skye ba nag gsum la phyi tshar gsum zer ro/ /de ltar slob ma mang yang gdan sa rgyal ba po ston
gyis byas/ de nas rgya 'phreng pa bde ba can nas spyan drangs te gdan sa mdzad/ de nas chu mig pa sengge dpal gyis gdan sa lo bco brgyad mdzad/ de nas da lta'i bar du
gdan sa ma chad par byon pa'o/ /lo tsA ba'i bu chen khyung rin chen grags kyi slob ma/ stod lung rgya dmar/ stag pa kha che sogs las brgyud pa nyang stod gnas gsar la sogs
su dar ro/ /'bre shes rab 'bar gyi nyang stod gnas rnying du phar phyin gyi grwa sa btsugs te/ las stod pa dkon mchog 'bar la sogs pa smin par mdzad do/ /ar byang chub
ye shes kyis gnam rtseng lding dang / gzhu kun dga' ra ba sogs su chos gsungs te/ grwa pa dpe 'grems dus gcig la'ang brgyad brgya tsam 'dus/ grags che ba dkar chung ring
mo sogs mang du byon no/ /gzhan yang gnyal zhig gi slob ma las brgyud pa'i sa skya/ zha lu sogs gtsang gi chos sde grags che ba rnams su mtshan nyid kyi bshad grwa btsugs
te/ mdor na rngog lo tsA ba khu dbon nas brgyud pa rnams a ti sha'i slob brgyud kyi mchog tu gtogs shing / bstan pa spyi la bka' drin che bas zur tsam

smos pa'o/ /gnyis pa mnga' ris pa shes rab rgyal mtshan las/ glegs bam byung tshul ni/ rngog legs pa'i shes rab de nyid gsang phur grwa pa lnga brgya tsam 'dus te/ gzhan phan
skyong ba'i dus su de rnams kyi nang nas rnam g.yeng la mi dga' zhing / 'dod yon la ched du mi byed pa'i byang chub sems dpa' shes rab rgyal mtshan zhes pa mnga' ris stod
pa/ jo bo dang 'brom gnyis ka la chos kyang thos pa cig yod pa de/ 'du tshogs la mi 'ong bar/ gsang phu'i nags khrod cig na sgom 'ba' zhig mdzad kyin bzhugs pa la/ de
dus rngog gsang phu ba/ nags gseb na yar skyo sangs la byon pa na/ byang chub sems dpa' shes rab rgyal mtshan dang mjal nas/ rngog la phyag 'tshal ba dang / rngog na re
khyed bza' btung / longs spyod la mi blta ba ngo mtshar che/ dus deng sang rnam g.yeng spangs nas 'di lta bu'i dge sbyor byed pa la dka' las yod/ khyed thugs dam gyi mthil
ci la mdzad gsungs pas shes rab rgyal mtshan na re/ yongs 'dzin dam pa gsan du gsol/ 'dus byas chos ni 'di 'dra ba/ /skyes pa'i tha ma 'chi ba'i chos/ /bsags pa'i tha ma
'dzad pa la/ /tshe 'di'i snang ba bag re la/ /rgyu mtshan ci yang mi gda' ba/ /de bas mi rtag thun re sgom/ /gsungs pas/ rngog gis dgongs pa la/ 'di chos skad thun mong
ba yin/ 'di la dge sbyor gyi khrigs dang / dad gus ci 'dug lta snyam nas/ dri lan mang du mdzad pas/ bka' gdams glegs bam rngog gi phyag tu

bzhugs pa shes rab rgyal mtshan gyis btsad chod de zhus pa/ thog mar bu chos kyi le'u dang po/ bram ze'i khye'u gsal bar sku skye ba bzhes tshul sogs gsungs/ mdor na tshig
re re la'ang bslab pa gsum/ lha bzhi/ rjes dran lnga tshang ba re mdzad de bslab gsum yang / tshul khrims bsrung ba dang / gzhan don du bsam pa bzang po byed pa de thams
cad bden gnyis su dril nas nyams su len pa dang / lha bzhi ni/ rab tu byung ba'i cha nas shAkya thub pa/ tshad med pa bzhi la dge sbyor byed pa'i cha nas thugs rje chen po/
'gro don byed pa'i cha nas rje btsun ma sgrol ma/ gnyen po bsten pa'i cha nas mi g.yo ba dang / rjes dran lnga ni/ lhag par sgrol ma 'di skad gsungs/ /sras kyi thu bo
spyan ras gzigs/ /khyod kyi rjes 'brang kho mos skyabs/ /kho mo'i gdams pa 'di longs la/ /rjes su 'brangs la bstan par gyis/ /skyabs gnas bla ma dran par mdzod/ /lus ni lha
yi rang bzhin te/ ngag ni bzlas brjod rgyun par mdzod/ /'gro ba ma lus pha mar soms/ /sems kyi gnas lugs stong par spyod/ /lnga po de yi skya bar nas/ /dge rtsa thams
cad dag par mdzod/ /ces te/ 'di rnams kyi nang du glegs bam gyi nyams len 'du bar bzhed cing / bka' babs che chung gang zag blo mtho dman gyi rim pas 'byed tshul glegs bam
las gsungs pa rnams bstan nas/ de nas rjes su glegs bam gyi po sti tshang ba bka' rgya dang bcas te gnang / shes rab rgyal mtshan

gyis kyang gnas nges med du bzhugs nas nyams len mdzad do/ /de nas spyan ras gzigs kyi sprul pa phu chung pa gzhon nu rgyal mtshan la gnang / des ka ma ba rnal 'byor pa rin
chen rgyal mtshan la/ des stabs kha ba zhang ston dar ma rgyal mtshan la/ des lha bla ma ye shes 'od kyi sku skye byang chub bzang po la/ des nam mkha' rin chen la gnang
/ de dag gi lo rgyus rgyas par don du gnyer na/ glegs bam gyi byung tshul ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i dpal 'byor zhes par blta'o/ /zhar la khu ston brtson 'grus g.yung
drung gi lo rgyus ni/ yar lung thang po che dang lha sdings su byon/ spyir jo bo'i chos mang du mnga'/ khyad par shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la rtsal thon/ gshin rje
gshed kyi zhal gzigs/ slob ma'i mchog mngon pa la mkhas pa brang ti dar ma snying po sogs dang / glegs bam las/ na ga rA dza la sogs pa'i 'khor lnga brgya tsam yod ces
'byung ngo / /gsum pa nag tsho'i rjes slob byon tshul ni/ nag tsho lo tsA ba la/ mnga' ris skor gsum du slob ma mang du byon pa la/ dbus su grags che ba rong pa phyag sor
ba yin te/ khong rang gi skye ba bcu gsum dran cing / mngon par shes pa rgya chen po mnga' ba/ sgom pa'i stobs kyis rig pa'i gnas la mkhas pa dang / dang por jo bo chen
po'i gdams ngag kho na rtsad gcod pa la jo bo'i dngos kyi slob ma zhang btsun yer pa ba/ yer pa gzim khang gi sgom pa dad pa bla ma/ ra sgreng du bshes gnyen ston pa/ rnal
'byor pa chen po/ dpal ldan dgon pa ba/

mkha' ru ba snga ma/ lo tsA ba nag tsho/ jo bo legs dang brgyad/ nying slob mkha' ru ba phyi ma/ dge bshes yung nga ba dang bcu la bsten nas bshad pa dang sgrub pa'i gdams
pa dang / jo bo'i lo rgyus rtsad bcad pas/ jo bo dngos kyi slob ma rnams gsung mthun par byung / nying slob gnyis gsung ma mthun te/ khyad par du bstan rim gyi mtshan 'dogs
lugs la/ mkha' ru ba phyi ma'i zhal nas/ bstan pa'i srol kha bya ba yin gsungs/ yung nga ba'i zhal nas/ khyod kyi slob dpon blo rtul bas ma zin par snang / bla ma rnams
bstan pa'i rim pa zhes gsungs pa yin/ de yang / tshul gnas thos dang bsam ldan pas/ /sgom pa la ni rab tu sbyor/ /bya ba'i don yin gsungs/ de nas rong pa phyag sor ba'i
dgongs pa la/ jo bo dngos la lo bcu dgu bsten pa'i lo tsA ba chen po de/ da dung mnga' ris gung thang na bzhugs yod 'dug pas/ jo bo dngos su bzhugs kyang lo tsA ba bar du
'jug dgos pas/ de rang la cig gtug dgos dgongs nas mang yul du byon pas/ lo tsA ba chen po de gung thang yang thog gi gtsug lag khang na bzhugs pa'i drung du byon nas/
dang por gsang sngags kyi gdams pa che chung mang du zhus nas bag phab/ de nas phyi de lo la pha rol tu phyin pa'i sgrub pa'i gdams pa dang / jo bo chen po'i sku che ba'i
yon tan dang / bod du spyan drangs lugs gsung bar zhu ba phul bas/ lo tsA ba'i zhal nas/ de la nga mkhas pa yin/ lo dgu bsten/ bod du

ngas spyan drangs pas/ jo bo'i lo rgyus la shin tu mkhas pa yin te/ khyod min pa rtsad gcod pa rang yang ma byung gsungs nas/ lo rgyus chen mo lam yig de'i dus su gsungs/ sgrub
pa'i gdams ngag kyang ma lus pa gnang ste/ nyin re la chos thun gsum gsum gsungs/ theg pa chen po sngags kyi sgor yang bcug ste/ dbyar re la sngags kyi glegs bam drug
cu tsam thon par byas te lo gsum bzhugs/ bstan rim gyi mtshan 'dogs lugs kyang / yung nga ba'i gsung bzhin du 'dug gsungs/ de nas mar 'byon khar/ khyod kyis sgrub pa'i
gnas 'di lta bu cig tu sgrubs shig 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs zhal mthong par 'gyur ro zhes/ lag sor dgon pa'i lung bstan yang mdzad/ de nas mar la skyel thung mdzad de/ 'gro
chos shig zhus pas/ gong thang pa'i zhal nas/ dal 'byor rten cig shes rab can/ /tshe 'di ji ltar byas kyang phyi/ /bla med byang chub rnyed dka' bas/ /'bad pa chen po
bya 'tshal lo/ /zhes pa la brten nas chos thun gcig gsungs/ der theg pa chen po mtha' dag gi chos ma lus pa 'dus pa yin gsungs/ de nas mar byon/ phod mdo bas sne len bzang
du byas te/ bstan pa la phan pa'i chos shig zhu zer bas/ mdo rtsa dang bslab pa kun las btus pa gnyis gsungs/ de nas tshe 'di'i bya ba thams cad ling gis bskyur nas bla
mas lung bstan pa'i gnas lag sor dgon

par bzhugs te/ nye gnas dang yang mi mjal bas/ gsol ba bug sgo la blangs te sgrub pa rtse gcig tu mdzad pas/ lo gsum na thugs rje chen po'i zhal mthong / lung bstan te/ khyod
kyis tshe 'di nyid du mthong lam thob nas/ slob ma yang sum cus zhal mthong bar 'gyur gsungs/ de nas lo nyi shu rtsa bzhi song ba'i dus mnal lam du mkha' 'gro ma mang
po byung nas jo bo'i ring bsrel ma sba bar ston zer nas/ ring bsrel sder gang gtad pa lho phyogs su gtor ba zhig rmis/ phyis rong pa'i bu bzhir grags pa lhor 'byung ba la
lta bar 'dug gsungs/ de nas pa tshab 'phrang kha rje'i 'khrug pa'i 'dums mdzad pa la/ phod mdor byon pa dang / rma tsho byang rdor zer ba 'dul ba 'dzin pa chen po de dang
mjal bas/ khong dad de/ skyid shod 'on ljang rdor spyang chos btsugs pa bas de'i dus rma tsho'i zur chos pa che ba bzhis chos zhus pas/ rong pa'i bu bzhir grags pa ni/
bya 'dul ba 'dzin pa/ rog 'ching phu ba/ rnam spar ba/ dge bshes zhu lan pa'o/ /rgya ra ston brjid dge bsnyen pas bur ma bgrang / de lngas jo bo'i gdams pa zhus/ zin bris
mdzad pas bya 'dul ba 'dzin pas gdams pa dang lo rgyus nyung 'dus gcig mdzad/ 'ching phu bas lo rgyus nyung 'dus la gdams pa mang ba zhig byas/ rnam spar bas lo rgyus ma
bris pa gdams ngag rnams bris/ zhu lan pas gdams ngag dang lo rgyus gnyis ka rgyas par byas nas/

khyad par du lo rgyus zhib par mdzad de/ mdo sde rnams las/ sangs rgyas kyis yul 'dir gang zag 'di la chos 'di gsungs bya ba yod pas/ chos khungs btsun par rtogs pa la lo rgyus
'di gal che ba yin gsungs nas rgyas bar bris/ yi ge de thams cad 'dul ba 'dzin pa'i phyag tu byung bas khong gi phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pas/ jo bo'i lam yig tu grags/
rgya ra ston brjid la sngags kyi gdams pa gtso bor gnang / 'dis rgya ra'i dgon pa btab/ gzhan yang / ba spu ba shes rab tshul khrims kyis phyag sor ba yun ring du bsten/
jo bo nas brgyud pa'i chos skor/ khyad par spyan ras gzigs kyi gdams ngag thams cad ma lus par gnang / lung bstan nas thugs rje chen po bsgrubs pas lo lnga na zhal mthong
/ theg pa chen po sbyor lam gyi rtogs pa brnyes pa yin gsungs/ ba spu bas 'phags gces sgom shes rab rdo rje dang / mnga' ris pa shes rab rgyal mtshan gnyis la gsungs/ de
gnyis tshogs lam chen po ba yin gsungs/ gce sgom gyis thog mar brag lha klu phug tu lo brgyad sgrub pa mdzad nas/ 'phags pa'i zhal dngos su mthong ngo / /bla ma mnga' ris
pa la ru mtshams kyi brag phug tu bsgrubs pas zhal mthong bar 'gyur gsungs nas lung bstan te/ bsgrubs pas lo bzhi na zhal mthong / dus rgyun du mi ma yin gyis 'tsho ba
drangs gsungs/ de gnyis ka la grub thob skyer sgang pas zhus pas/ lo phyed dang bzhi bsgrubs bas zhal mthong nas/

snyigs ma'i dus su zhal mthong gi brgyud pa mang du 'byung gsungs lung bstan mdzad de/ slob ma yang lnga bcus zhal mthong ngo / /des sangs rgyas gnyan ston la gsungs te/ skyer
sgang du dbyar thog dgun thog bcu gsum bzhugs/ gdams ngag gcig brgyud thams cad ma lus par gnang nas/ lo gsum bsgrubs pas/ phyag bzhi pa/ kharsa pa Ni/ bcu gcig zhal/
phyag stong spyan stong rnams zhal mthong / slob ma bcu gcig gis zhal mthong ba'i lung bstan mdzad pa bzhin byung gsungs/ de nas de lta yang brgyud pa ma chad par bzhugs
pa dang / gzhan yang nag tsho nas brgyud pa'i chos skor/ gsang ba 'dus ba'i bshad rgyud ye shes rdo rje kun las btus la brten pa'i man ngag la sogs pa 'ga' re gnang ngo
/ /drug pa de rnams kyis bstan bcos ji ltar mdzad pa ni/ rgyal bas gdul bya'i bsam pa dang rjes su mthun par mdo rgyud kyi gsung rab mtha' yas shig bka' bstsal pa dang /
de'i dgongs pa gsal bar mdzad pa'i shing rta chen po rnams kyi bstan bcos rtsod bral du ma zhig mdzad pa de thams cad bka' gdams rin po che'i khungs su byed pa'i gzhung yin
la/ de rnams kyi nang nas bslab spyod gnyis/ sa rgyan gnyis/ skyes tshoms gnyis dang drug la bka' gdams gzhung drug ces gsungs pa'i don yang / zab mo lta ba'i rgyud kyi
gzhung bsam gyis mi khyab kyang / don bslab spyod gnyis su 'du ba dang / rgya chen spyod pa'i rgyud kyi gzhung bsam gyis mi khyab

kyang / don sa rgyan gnyis su 'du ba dang / skyes rabs kyis bcom ldan 'das kyi sngon gyi mdzad pa las brtsams te/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa/ pha rol tu phyin pa drug dbye
ba dang bcas pa'i don nyams su len tshul gsungs pa dang / ched du brjod pa'i tshoms dgra bcom pa chos skyabs kyis mdzad pa/ brjod bya sna tshogs pa tshoms su bsdus nas
gsungs pas/ chos spyi la gal che bar dgongs te gzhung drug tu mdzad do/ /bshes gnyen gong ma rnams 'dul spyod gnyis zhes/ 'dul bas lhag pa tshul khrims kyi bslab pa/ spyod
'jug gis byang chub sems dpa'i bslab pa gsum la slob pa ston pas de rnams zab lam rdo rje theg pa'i rten du yang nges par dgos pa la dgongs so/ /gzhan yang jo bo'i chos
chung brgya rtsar grags pa'am/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa gtso bor ston pas spyod phyogs brgya rtsa zhes pa'i glegs bam la/ thog mar mchod brjod kyi tshul gyis bstod
pa'i skor la/ dkon mchog gsum rjes su dran pa'i mdo/ lha las phul byung bar bstod pa bde byed bdag pos mdzad pa/ bshags pa'i bstod pa tsandra go mis mdzad pa/ yon tan
mtha' yas par bstod pa dkon mchog 'bangs kyis mdzad pa/ de'i 'grel pa dang / don bsdus pa'i tshigs bcad phyogs kyi glang pos mdzad pa dang drug skyabs 'gro'i skor la/ skyabs
gsum bdun cu pa zla grags kyis mdzad pa/ skyabs 'gro drug bcu pa bi ma la mi tras mdzad pa/

skyabs 'gro bstan pa jo bo rjes mdzad pa dang gsum/ byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed pa'i cho ga la/ 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ slob dpon byang bzang gi mdzad pa/ dze
ta ri dgra las rnam par rgyal bas mdzad pa/ sems bskyed pa'i cho ga dang / bla ma'i bya ba'i rim pa gnyis jo bos mdzad pa/ sdom pa nyi shu pa tsandra go mis mdzad pa/ de'i
'grel pa zhi ba 'tshos mdzad pa dang bdun no/ /byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i skor la/ byang chub lam gyi sgron ma/ de'i rang 'grel dang / spyod pa bsdus pa'i sgron
ma/ bsdus don sgron me/ dbu ma'i man ngag snying po bsdu ba/ snying po nges par bsdu ba/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa nor bu'i phreng ba/ 'di bka' gdams glegs bam gyi
rtsa tshig yin no/ /byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mdo tsam gdams ngag tu brjod pa theg pa chen po'i lam gyi sgrub thabs yi ger bsdus pa/ theg pa chen po'i lam gyi sgrub
thabs shin tu bsdus pa/ rang gi bya ba'i rim pa bskul ba dang bcas pa yi ger bris pa/ mdo sde'i don kun las btus pa'i man ngag klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i mdo kun las btus
pa'i don bsdus pa/ mi dge bcu'i las kyi lam bstan pa/ las rnam par 'byed pa/ kha ton dang glegs bam klog pa sngon du bya ba'i cho ga pha rol tu phyin pa'i tsha tsha gdab
pa'i cho ga byang chub sems dpa' las dang po pa'i lam la 'jug pa/ de ltar bcu dgu jo bo chen pos mdzad/ 'phags pa rtog pa chen po yongs su rgyas pa'i mdo sde'i sdig bshags
dang /

sgrub pa mdo de nyid las phyung ba las dang po pa'i sa sbyang ba/ dgra las rgyal ba'i gsang bas mdzad pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i yi ge brgya pa'i sgo nas sdig pa bshags pa zhi
ba lhas mdzad pa dang nyi shu rtsa gnyis sgom rim dang bsam gtan gyi yi ge sna tshogs la/ rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba dang / de'i rnam par bshad pa 'phags pa klu sgrub
kyis mdzad pa/ sgom rim gsum dang / rnal 'byor bsgom pa la 'jug pa ka ma la shi las mdzad pa/ don dam byang chub kyi sems sgom pa rin po che'i sgron me dang / kun rdzob
byang chub kyi sems sgom pa padma spung pa gnyis slob dpon rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa/ ting nge 'dzin gyi tshogs kyi le'u slob dpon byang chub bzang pos mdzad pa/ rnal 'byor
gyi mtshan nyid kyi bden pa/ yang ting nge 'dzin gyi le'u nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ bsam gtan gyi chos drug rnam par bzhag pa a wa dhu ti pas mdzad pa/ de'i 'grel pa
dha na shrI las mdzad pa/ rnal 'byor pa'i rtogs pa'i gegs sel ba sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa/ rnal 'byor kyi mtshan nyid kyi bden pa slob dpon byang chub bzang pos mdzad
pa/ dbu ma'i man ngag rin chen za ma tog kha phye ba dang / bden pa gnyis la 'jug pa dang / dran pa cig pa'i man ngag gnyis mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa/ rnal
'byor sgom pa'i lam ye shes snying pos mdzad pa/ rnal 'byor la 'jug pa phyogs kyi glang pos mdzad pa/ mi sdug pa bsgom pa'i rim pa dge ba'i go chas mdzad pa/ lus yongs su
spyad pa'i sgom rim nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ sems mgu bar bya ba'i tshigs su bcad pa theg chen nyi shu pa klu grub kyis mdzad

pa/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i theg pa'i rim pa'i man ngag dpal ye shes grags pas mdzad pa/ sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa bla na med pa'i mdo sde'i rjes su 'gro ba mahA ma tis mdzad
pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i man ngag rin chen 'byung gnas zhi bas mdzad pa/ rnal 'byor la 'jug pa'i man ngag chos kyi dbang pos mdzad pa/ rnal 'byor spyod pa'i
sgom pa'i don bsdus te bstan pa ye shes zla bas mdzad pa dang nyi shu rtsa bdun/ gsang sngags kyi lam rim la/ yi ge drug pa'i glu/ spyod pa'i glu/ de'i 'grel pa/ 'khor
ba las yid nges par 'byung ba'i glu/ chos kyi glu/ ting nge 'dzin gyi glu/ rdo rje gdan gyi glu/ de'i 'grel pa chos kyi dbyings su lta ba'i glu/ ting nge 'dzin gyi tshogs
kyi le'u/ 'jig rten las 'das pa'i yan lag bdun pa'i cho ga rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga dang / bcu gcig jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ bde ba bcu gsum pa'i glu a ti shas mdzad pa/ man
ngag bdud rtsi'i 'khor lo phyag na rdo rjes bsdus pa/ byang chub sems kyi rnam par bshad pa 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ maNTal gyi cho ga dgra las rnam rgyal gyis
mdzad pa/ maNTal gyi cho ga sangs rgyas gsang bas mdzad pa/ maNTal gyi cho ga rdo rje gdan pas mdzad pa/ maNTal gyi cho ga ka ma la shi las mdzad pa/ maNTal gyi cho ga
rnyog med rdo rjes mdzad pa dang bcu dgu gtam du bya ba sna tshogs la/ rmi lam yid bzhin gyi nor bu'i gtam klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ yon tan bdun rab tu brjod pa'i gtam dbyig
gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ sbyin pa'i gtam slob dpon gu na pra bha bas mdzad pa/ tshul khrims kyi gtam/ tshod zin pa'i

gtam/ tshogs kyi gtam dang gsum dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ mi khom pa brgyad kyi gta rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa/ legs bshad za ma tog lta bu'i gtam slob dpon dpa' bos mdzad
pa/ phyin ci log bzhi spang ba'i gtam dang / rtsod pa'i dus kyi gtam ma ti tsi tras mdzad pa/ dben pa'i gtam sa mtsho sbyin gyis mdzad pa dang bcu gcig go /springs yig gi
skor la/ bshes pa'i springs yig klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ slob ma la springs pa/ tsantra go mis mdzad pa/ rgyal po ka ni ka la springs pa ma ti tsi tas mdzad pa/ rab gsal
gzhon nu la springs pa 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyis mdzad pa/ sems rin po che rnam par sbyang ba'i springs yig dze ta ris mdzad pa/ dri ma med pa rin po che'i springs
yig rgyal po ne ya pa la gdams pa dang / pu hrang jo bo la springs yig sum cu pa jo bos mdzad pa dang bdun/ dran pa nyer bzhag gi tshig le'ur byas pa dang / dge ba bcu'i
las kyi lam bstan pa chos ldan rab 'byor dbyangs kyis mdzad pa/ yang mi dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam bstan pa dang / mya ngan bsal ba rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa/ 'dod pa'i yon
tan lnga'i nyes dmigs bshad pa dbyig gnyen gyis mdzad pa dang lnga ste bcu gnyis su bzhed do/ /rtogs brjod la/ gzhon nu ma bdun gyi rtogs pa brjod pa gsang ba byin gyis
mdzad pa gcig lugs kyi bstan bcos la/ shes rab brgya pa 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ dri med dris lan rin po che phreng ba don yod char gyis mdzad pa dang gnyis/ bsngo
ba dang smon lam la/ yan lag bdun pa'i cho ga tshigs su bcad pa nyi shu pa klu sgrub kyis
