mdzad pa/ smon lam bdun cu pa gzhan la phan pa'i dbyangs dgon pa bas mdzad pa dang gnyis so/ /mdor na glegs bam gcig la brgya dang bcu gnyis bzhugs so/ /gzhan yang jo bo chen
pos mdzad pa la/ byang chub ltung bshags kyi 'grel pa dam tshig gis bsdus pa zhes pa'i rtsa ltung gi bshad pa/ gsang 'dus ye shes zhabs lugs lha bcu dgu'i sgrub thabs/
bstod pa/ 'jam dpal rdo rje dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs/ gsang 'dus 'jig rten dbang phyug lha bcu dgu'i sgrub thabs dang / 'jig rten dbang phyug dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub
thabs/ 'jig rten dbang phyug gi gtor chog rgyas pa/ rgyal ba rigs lnga'i bkra shis kyi tshigs su bcad pa/ grub chen lU hi pas mdzad pa'i dpal mngon par rtogs pa'i 'grel
ba chen mo/ 'khor lo sdom pa lha bcu gsum dang / lha lnga dang / dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs/ shar phyogs bhaM ga la'i tshal du bde mchog dkyil 'khor zhal gzigs dus su
bstod pa/ rdo rje phag mo'i sgrub thabs che ba rin chen rgyan zhes pa dang / chung ba gcig rdo rje rnal 'byor ma zhal gzigs pa'i dus su bstod pa/ yang mkha' spyod ma dkar
mo'i sgrub thabs che chung gnyis/ 'byung po thams cad pa'i gtor ma'i cho ga rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga 'phags pa klu sgrub/ na ro pa/ sgeg pa'i rdo rje dang gsum snyan nas
snyan du brgyud pa'i man ngag phyogs gcig tu mdzad pa/ sgrol ma yid bzhin 'khor lo'i sgrub thabs/ 'phags pa bcu gcig zhal gyi bstod pa/ spyan ras gzigs gtso 'khor gsum gyi
sgrub thabs/ yi ge drug pa'i man ngag spyan ras gzigs kyi ri mo'i

brda pa/ sgrol ma sngon mo'i bstod pa zhal gzigs dus su mdzad pa/ dzambha la dkar po'i bstod pa/ sman bla gtso 'khor gsum gyi sgrub thabs/ tshogs bdag dkar po'i sgrub thabs
che chung gnyis/ mi g.yo ba sngon po'i sgrub thabs/ mgon po gri gug gi sgrub thabs/ rdo rje lcags sgrog gi sgrub thabs/ rta mgrin sho na bzhi bskor lha lnga'i sgrub thabs
dang / dkyil chog jo bo bod du 'byon khar slob ma rnams la phyi chos su gdams pa/ rnam dag gtsug gi nor bu/ gzhan yang lha btsun pa byang chub 'od/ lo chen rin chen bzang
po/ 'ol rgol pa ye shes 'bar/ zhang sna chung ston pa rnams la gdams pa dang / jo bos mdzad pa'i mdo bsdus chen mo/ dang po rgya dper lus pa/ zhang shar pa ba'i phyag
tu byung bas/ pa tshab lo tsA ba/ gnas gzhi ya gad du spyan drangs nas bsgyur bar bshad de/ 'di rnams ni jo bos mdzad pa rtsod bral yin la/ gzhan yang bstan 'gyur gyi tho
rnams su jo bo'i mdzad byang 'byar ba gtsug tor dri med dang / gdugs dkar sogs rgya gzhung mang du 'dug kyang 'dir ma bkod do/ /snye thang du mdzad par grags pa rigs kyi
smon lam/ lta sgom spyod gsum gyi glu/ bsam gtan la bskul ba'i glu/ bde ba drug gi glu/ lta spyod zung du 'brel ba'i glu/ dus mchod bzhi'i ngos 'dzin dang phan yon/ bde
mchog rgyud la bsten pa'i rlung gi man ngag gzhan yang stong thun brgyad bcu rtsa gnyis sogs mdzad byang 'byar ba mang du snang zhing / phal cher mdzad par mngon te/ 'dir
dpyad pa zhib tu ma byas so/ /rtsa ltung gi 'grel pa sogs kha cig la yang / jo bos mdzad pa yin min/ bod snga ma

dag dpyad pa mdzad mod/ 'dir zhib tu ma bris so/ /bka' gdams glegs bam du gtogs pa la/ spyir dpe tshan lnga bcu nga bzhi las/ sbyor ba'i chos la dpe tshan bzhi ste/ 'brom chos
kyi rgyal po nyid kyis logs su nan gyis gtad pa'i bka' rgya dang / rang rgyud bskul ma 'debs pa dad pa'i ljon shing gnyis/ sbyor dngos gnyis kar gal che la/ lo rgyus
ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i dpal 'byor zhes pa glegs bam gyi chos 'byung dang / snying gi thig le'i gsal byed zung 'jug nyi ma'i thig le gnyis te dpe tshan bzhi po 'di
glegs bam dngos gzhi la mi the'o/ /byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa nor bu'i phreng ba ni/ dngos gzhi pha chos/ bu chos gnyis ka'i rtsa tshig yin la/ pha chos ni/ bla ma rnams
la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhes pa nas mang po'i nang du ngag la brtag gcig pur 'dug na sems la brtag ces pa'i bar le'u nyi shu rtsa gsum du bsdus nas gsungs pa'i steng du/
bka' rgya ma/ ma 'ongs lung bstan/ 'chi med rdo rje'i glu'i le'u dang gsum bsnan pas nyi shu rtsa drug dang / bu chos la/ the tshom thams cad spang bya zhing / /zhes pa
las 'phros te/ bram ze'i khye'u gsal pa'i skyes rabs dang / de nas rim pa bzhin rtsa tshig las brtsams te/ rngog gi zhus pa'i skyes rabs nyi shu la/ rngog chos nyi shu dang
/ khu ston phebs nas zhus pa gnyis la/ khu chos gnyis te nyi shu rtsa gnyis bu chos yin la/ kha skong gi le'u ste bzhi bcu zhe dgu ni glegs bam dngos gzhi'o/ /rgyal ba
yab sras kyi bkod pa phun sum tshogs pa'i gter zhes pa phyis snar thang pas byas par snang bas/ don bsdu

lta bur snang la 'di dngos gzhi la mi the'o/ /gzhan yang lam rim dang / gsung bgros thor bu ba dang / 'phrin yig dang / man ngag sna tshogs pa'i skor ro/ /dang po lam rim la/
po to ba nas brgyud pa/ spyan snga nas brgyud pa/ gsang phu ba nas brgyud pa'o/ /dang po ni/ dol pa dmar zhur gyi be'u bum gyi rtsa tshig dang / de'i 'grel pa lha don
stengs pas mdzad pa la/ na bza' las mtshan du gsol ba/ be'u bum sngon po dang / be'u bum dmar po zhes pa lo rgyus/ rtsa ba/ 'grel ba/ sa bcad dang bzhi 'dug pa/ yer pa'i
zhang btsun gyis mdzad pa zer yang / zhang yer pa ba dang gnyis gang gis mdzad brtag par bya'o/ /be'u bum khra bo zhes pa bka' gdams kyi gsung bgros sna tshogs pa phyogs
gcig tu bsgrigs pa zhig snang ba las/ gcer sgom gyi bka' gdams thor bu ba btus par mngon no/ /dge bshes grab pas mdzad pa'i dpe chos dang / brag dkar bas de nyid rgyas su
btang ba gnyis la brten nas gcer sgom gyi dpe chos rin chen spungs pa rtsa 'grel mdzad par grags che la/ 'di'i zhabs su spros bsdus byas zhes pa/ grab pas mdzad pa las cung
zad spros/ brag dkar bas mdzad pa'i rgyas pa la bsdus zhes pa'i don no/ /gzhan yang sha ra bas mdzad pa'i lam rim che chung gnyis/ bya 'chad kyi gsung bgros thor bu ba
rnams dang / de las brgyud pa blo sbyong gi yig cha che chung dang / se spyil ba'i lam sgron sa bcad/ Tikka/ sbas pa ston gzhon gyi lam rim dang / lam sgron Tikka sogs
thor bu ba 'ga' dang / rnal 'byor

byang seng gi bstan rim legs pa zhig kyang snang ngo / /snar thang pas kyang yig cha 'ga' re mdzad la/ kha rag skor gsum du dpal ldan dgon pa ba'i gsung bgros bsgrigs pa'i
lam rim dang / gzhan yang gzhung pa brgyud pa'i gsung bgros mdzad byang med pa mang du snang ngo / /gnyis pa bshes gnyen spyan snga nas brgyud pa la/ dge bshes ston pa'i
gsung / spyan snga/ bya yul ba/ gtsang pa rin po che rnams snyan nas snyan du brgyud pa/ rin po che glang lung pas bsgrigs pa'i lam rim dang / yang rnal 'byor pa nas stod
lung pa chen po/ dge bshes lha bzo/ nya ga mo pa/ glang lung pa nas bla ma na rim gyis bstan rim chen mo la zin bris/ mdzad byang yod med mang du snang ba'i 'be sangs rgyas
sgom pas mdzad pa'i zin bris dang / rin po che gser khang pa'i zin bris dang / rin po che tshul khrims dar gyi zhal snga nas mdzad pa'i bstan rim chen po nyid mchog yin
no/ /de lta bu'i bstan rim de ni tshogs su 'chad na bstan pa'i rim pa/ nyams len du dril ba lam gyi rim pa/ gzhung du bkod pa byang chub lam gyi sgron ma ste/ don gcig
la ming gsum btags pa dang 'dra gsungs pa dang / thar pa don gnyer gyi gang zag sangs rgyas kyi sar 'gro ba la bstan pa'i chos thams cad lam gyi rim par dril nas nyams su
len pas lam bstan pa'i rim pa zhes gsungs pa ltar na/ khyad par cher med kyang / cung zad 'byed na/ chos khungs btsun par rtogs pa'i phyir/ thog mar lo rgyus dang / de
nas brgyud pa rjod byed sde snod

gsum dang / brjod bya bslab pa gsum/ gang zag gcig gi lam du lung rnam dag dang sbyar te 'gal med du ston pa bstan pa'i rim pa dang / de'i don theg pa chen po'i lam gyi rim
par dril nas ston pa lam rim zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /yang stod lung pa nas brgyud pa'i bden gnyis/ bden bzhi'i chos skor dang / chos thun rer nyams len don tshan bzhi bzhir
bsdus pa/ bzhi tshan chos thun bcu dgu ja chos chos thun lnga bcu dang / jo bos mang yul lcog ka ri la/ ljongs rgyu ba'i dus gsungs pa/ ri chos su grags pa dang / lam
sgron la gong du smos pa'i Tikka dang / 'chim nam mkha' grags/ chu mig pa gnyis kyi Tikka/ gzhan yang gsung bgros bkod pa'i Tikka mdzad byang med pa mang du snang ba ni/
bka' gdams kyi bshes gnyen gong ma rnams bla ma'i gsung la zin bris tsam las/ mdzad byang mi sbyor ba dang / slob ma rnams kyis kyang bka' 'bum bsgrigs pa sogs cher ma mdzad
cing / gsung bgros thor bu 'dug pa yang yun ring bas kha thor ba sogs ma spros so/ /gsum pa gsang phu ba nas brgyud pa la/ rngog legs shes mdzad pa'i lam rim shlau ka
drug dang / de'i gsal byed blo ldan shes rab kyis mdzad pa shog bu nyi shu tsam dang / de nyid rgyas par 'chad pa gro lung pas mdzad pa'i bstan rim chen mo nyid yin no/
/gnyis pa gsung bgros thor bu ba'i skor la/ blo sbyong mtshon cha 'khor lo/ rma bya dug 'joms/ dgyes sgom rdo rje'i glu/ blo sbyong sems pa'i rim pa/ gser gling pas jo bo
la gnang

ba'i rtog pa 'bur 'joms rtsa 'grel/ blo sbyong thabs bzhi pa/ de'i sgo nas sdig pa bshags pa dang / 'khon sbyang ba'i cho ga ku su lu'i tshogs bsag blo sbyong kun tu bzang
po/ blo sbyong stan thog gcig ma/ blo sbyong thun brgyad ma/ glang thang pa'i tshig rkang brgyad ma/ de'i 'grel pa byed ston gyis mdzad pa/ blo sbyong rten 'brel snying po
dang / bka' gdams thor bu ba sogs dang / gzhan yang rgyal po sa'i sa ghas bod kyi rnam gzhag lo chen dang / nag tsho la zhus kyang gsal bar ma byung pa/ tho mthing gser
gyi lha khang du jo bo dang ston pa zhal 'dzom par zhus pas/ ston pas mngon par shes pas gzigs te/ bod kyi sa bcad dang gnas lugs rnams zhib par gsungs pa sogs mang du snang
ngo / /gsum pa 'phrin yig gi skor dang / jo bos mdzad pa gong du bshad la/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos sku mtshams nas grogs po rnams la springs pa/ dge bshes ston
pas jo bo spyan 'dren pa'i dus mnga' ris nas bod ston rnams la springs pa tshigs su bcad pa bcu dgu pa/ zhang 'phrang kha ber chung la springs pa snga phyi gnyis/ sgom chen
byang chub la springs pa/ bshes gnyen blo gros 'byung gnas la springs pa/ a li sman rgan sogs la gdams pa'o/ /po to bas rang gi slob ma rnams la spyir springs pa/ rang
gi grogs po dol pa'i bla ma la springs pa/ g.ya' ngos dgon par springs pa/ yung nga'i chang 'thung rnams la springs pa/ bya yul gyi mchod gnas lo chung la springs pa/ zhogs
ya gad du springs pa'i yi ge rnams so/ /spyan

sngas sne'u zur pa la dang po springs pa/ rjes su springs pa gdams ngag tshig drug ma dang / dge bshes dbang seng la springs pa/ bya yul ba nyer gnas mdzad dus gdams pa zer
ba sogs dang / stabs ka bas mnga' ris rgyal po la springs pa/ sha ra bas rngog blo ldan la springs pa/ mchod gnas dbang nge la springs pa/ sha'o sgang pa la springs pa/
sgom chen sengge sku la springs pa sogs/ sha ra ba'i 'phrin yig sum cu rtsa bzhi/ gzhan yang dpal ldan dgon pa ba'i bca' yig po to ba'i bca' yig zhang ston shar ba pas snga
phyir byas pa gnyis te dge 'dun spyi'i bca' yig bzhi'o/ /de rnams ni thos tshod tsam min par mthong ba rnams bkod do/ /bzhi pa man ngag gi skor la bka' gdams lha bzhir
grags pa/ dam tshig gsum bkod kyi rgyud la rten pa/ thub pa gtso 'khor gsum bsgoms te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i yig brgya bzlas nas/ sdig pa sbyangs pa dang / byang chub sems
dpa'i ltung ba bshags pa/ gtsug lag khang bzhengs tshul sogs snang ngo / /spyan ras gzigs kyi skor la/ jo bos mdzad pa gong du smos la/ de'i gsal byed kyi sgrub thabs/
rdzogs rim/ las tshogs ma/ rnal 'byor lnga dang / dug gsum shad kyis sbyong ba'i man ngag zhi drag gi sbyin sreg sogs nyi shu tsam dang / sgrol ma'i skor la/ jo bo rgya gar
nas bod du 'byon khar/ rdo rje gdan la skor ba mdzad pa'i dus/ sgrol ma nyid kyis gsungs pa'i bstod pa shlauka nyer gcig dang sbyar ba'i sgrub thabs/ las tshogs rnams
dang / sgrol ma dkar

mo la/ jo bo'i gzhung dang rjes su 'brel ba/ ngag dbang grags pa dang / gser gling pa nas brgyud pa'i tshe khrid las tshogs mang ba dang bcas pa/ mi g.yo ba sngon po la jo
bo'i gzhung dang / dpal ldan dgon pa ba/ gur gyi nya ga mor sgom mdzad kyin bzhugs pa la bar chad kyi mtshan ma byung ba/ jo bo la zhus pas/ nga la rnal 'byor srung ba'i
man ngag yod gsungs nas/ mi g.yo ba'i dmigs pa skor gsum dang / sgrub yig che chung rgyud man ngag dang bcas pa rdzogs par gnang / kha cig sgrub yig che ba bya rgyud kyi
nang gi mi g.yo ba'i rgyud la le'u dang las tshogs mang du yod pa 'di yin zhes zer/ sgrub yig bar pa sogs man ngag rnams/ dgon pa ba nas sne'u zur pa la brgyud pa dang /
bya yul ba nas brgyud pa gnyis sgyer sgom la bzhugs pa sangs rgyas dbon la gnang / de'i gsung la rtogs ldan bzang mo bas zin bris su btab pa da lta yod pa 'di'o/ /mi g.yo
ba bla med kyi rgyud/ phyis shud sgye lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing / dbang rgyud dang bcas pa byung ngo / /gzhan yang tshogs bdag dkar po la/ gser gling
pa/ na ro pa/ kha che rin chen rdo rje rnams kyi rgya gzhung re/ jo bos mdzad pa gnyis dang lnga/ tshogs bdag gi skyes rabs/ gzungs ring / phyi sgrub/ nang sgrub/ gsang
sgrub kyi skor/ gser gling pas jo bo la gnang ba dang / gzhan yang las tshogs le'u bco lnga pa dang / le'u sum cu so gcig pa rnams jo bos rnal 'byor pa/ des spyan snga
pa/ des bya yul pa la brgyud pa'o/ /tshogs bdag dkar po 'di 'jig rten pa'i tshul bstan kyang / kha cig spyan ras gzigs kyi sprul par bzhed/

bka' brgyud 'di'i lugs kyis bdud rtsi 'khyil pa'i sprul par bzhed de mi 'gal lo/ /yang dzambha la dkar po 'brug bzhon lha mo bzhis bskor ba ni jo bo ri bo po ta la'i 'gram
na byon pa'i dus/ spyan ras gzigs kyis zhal dngos su bstan nas gnang ste/ phyi nang gsang gsum gyi las tshogs dang / chu sbyin bya thabs sogs dang / sme brtsegs ljang khu'i
sgrub thabs las tshogs dang bcas pa dang / gtsug tor dri med/ gtsug tor gdugs dkar gyi rjes gnang la sogs pa jo bo nas brgyud pa da lta ma chad pa mang du bzhugs so/ /jo
bo nas brgyud pa'i dbang brgyud yod pa la/ bde mchog lU hi pa/ bde mchog bcu gsum ma/ gsang 'dus 'phags lugs/ ye shes zhabs lugs/ jo bo nyid kyi gsang 'dus 'jig rten dbang
phyug mahA ma ya/ yo ga gtsug dgu kun rig jo lugs/ snur pa rnams de las brgyud cing phyag len mdzad pas snur lugs su grags pa dang / rdo rje phag mo rin chen rgyan dang
/ spyan ras gzigs lha mang du grags pa/ klu sgrub dang / jo bo nyid kyis mdzad pa'i gzhung dang rjes su 'brel ba'i dbang bka' la sogs pa da lta bzhugs pa mang du yod
par sems so/ /chos skyong skor la/ bka' gdams pa spyi la grags pa/ mgon po gri gug la gtso rkyang lha gsum/ lha bzhi/ lha lnga/ lha mang sogs lugs mang du 'dug pa rnams la
mgon po'i rgyud 'ga' re dang / rgya gzhung che chung bco lnga tsam snang ba'i gtso rkyang la jo bo chen po dang / a wa dhU ti pa gnyis kyi gzhung re dang / de la paNDi
ta 'jam dpal dbyangs kyi 'grel pa dang / gtso 'khor gsum du byed pa paNDi ta grags pa rdo rje'i rgya gzhung dang / de'i gsal byed bya yul bas

mdzad pa la brten pa byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa yang mnga' bas/ bla ma gong ma rnams 'di mdzad pa mang la/ lha bzhi byed na/ mgon po'i mdun du gnod sbyin lag na rdo rje/ rdo
rje gsor thabs su 'dzin pa/ gnod sbyin grangs med pa'i tshogs kyis bskor ba/ na ro pa'i gzhung dang / bskul nas 'byung ba bzhin bskyed pa dang / yang lag na rdo rje'i dod
du mgon po trag shad yod pa/ bod kyis byas pa'i lha bzhi zhig kyang 'dug go /legs sred dmar po 'di lho nub pa yin par bzhed cing / mdun du bskyed nas/ las la skul ba'i sgrub
yig kyang yod do/ /yang jo bo'i rgya gzhung du/ gtso bo la mkha' 'gro ma bzhis bskor ba'i lha lnga zhig gsungs pa dang / yang gri gug rigs lnga dang / gtso bo la gshin
rje pho brgyad mo brgyad kyis bskor ba/ lha bcu bdun zangs gri can du grags pa gnyis la/ bram ze mchog sred kyi gzhung che chung / dbang rgyud dang bcas pa yod pa dang
/ yang gtso bo la ye shes zhabs lugs kyi phyogs skyong bco lngas bskor ba dang / mgon po rta mang du grags pa mgon pos bskul nas 'byung ba sogs yod pas/ de dag gi mngon
rtogs dang / rgya gzhung gang nas gang bshad sogs don du gnyer na gzhan du blta'o/ /yang mgon po lho nub pa/ zhal dmar ba/ mi thung gsod byed/ mthar skyes ma zhes mtshan
gyi rnam grangs bzhi dang ldan pa 'di la/ jo bo'i rgya gzhung dang / de'i gsung bshes gnyen ston pas bkod pa'i gab pa sngon byung du grags pa/ phyi sgrub/ nang sgrub/ gsang
sgrub sogs la phyis kyis byas pa'i yig cha mang du 'dug la/ 'di dbang gi gri gug yin par rin po che chos kyi rjes bzhed do/ /gri gug

gi 'khor du yod pa'i mgon po ce spyang gdong can la glang ri thang pa nas/ rgya lcags ri gang kha ba la brgyud pa'i rjes gnang / las tshogs sogs 'dug la/ mgon po beng la/ jo
bo nas brgyud pa gtso 'khor lnga'i rjes gnang dgos sgrub sogs dang / mgon po trag shad la mi 'dra ba mang yang / bka' gdams pa nas brgyud pa/ rkang thang dang / seng zhon
du nges pas/ 'di la sgrub thabs/ zhi drag gi las tshogs mang ngo / /nam mkha'i gos can la/ bka' gdams glegs bam nas mched bcu gnyis su gsungs pa ni/ gser mtsho ma dang
'o mtsho ma/ /bstan skyong ma dang yid 'dzin ma/ /stobs mo che dang drag shul can/ /khrag mdog ma dang dud kha ma/ /thogs med ma dang stobs mo che/ /dbang bsdud ma dang
las 'joms ma/ /bcu gnyis stobs chen bstan srung kun/ /kho bo'i bstan pa mi skyong na/ /ci ste kho bo'i slad bzhin 'brangs/ /zhes gsungs shing / lam yig las/ mched bzhir gsungs
pa ni/ rdo rje shugs chen ma/ 'od ldan ma/ dung skyong ma/ nam mkha'i gos can rnams so/ /mgon po lho nub pa dang / nam mkha'i gos can ni rgya gar nas jo bo'i phyag
phyir lugs sku dang / rgya dpe'i dgos kyi bka' srung la byon zhes 'byung la/ nam mkha'i gos can zhes pa sku gcer bu'i don yin yang / rgyan can sogs ni zhal gzigs yin no/
/bya yul gyi lha mo dmar mo ni/ re ma ti mched bzhi'i dbang gi re ma ti yin te/ 'di la tsaNTi dmar mo zhes pa gtum mo dmar mo zhes pa'o/ /gzhan yang sngon gyi skyes chen
rnams kyi gsan yig

che chung dang / bla ma rnams kyi gsung las mang du thob kyang 'dir rgyas par ma spros shing / deng sang dus kyi dbang gis lugs 'di dag don du gnyer ba dka' bar snang yang
/ 'di dag la brten nas kyang rags pa tsam rtogs shing / zhib tu 'tshol ba'i sgor 'gyur ba srid dam snyam nas bkod la/ blo gros dang ldan zhing / bka' gdams brgyud pa 'di
la dad pa dang ldan pa rnams kyis ji ltar rigs pa bsnan cing spel bar bya'o/ /'dir smras pa/ thog mtha' bar gsum dge ba rgyal ba'i bka'/ /de don bslab pa gsum gyis rgyud
gtams pa'i/ /bshes gnyen dam pa rim par byon rnams kyi/ /rnam thar dran pas slar yang phyag bgyi 'o/ /de lta'i skyes chen rnams kyis gangs ljongs 'dir/ /zab rgyas chos kyi
sgron me cher sbar nas/ /bod yul rmongs pa'i mun pa bsal tshul gyi/ /gtam 'di dpyod ldan yid rab 'phrog byed yin/ /sngon tshe chos rgyal byang chub sems dpa' yis/ /bstan
'gro'i ched du rang gi srog kyang btang / /'di 'dra thos kyang ji snyam mi sems pa'i/ /snyigs ma'i skye bo 'di kun ches rab blun/ /kho bo sngon bsags las kyi 'phro bzang
bas/ /phan bde'i 'byung gnas bstan pa rin chen rgyun/ /phyogs gcig ma yin kun kyang rgyas 'dod pa/ /'di la dkon mchog thugs rjes cis mi gzigs/ /chos sgor zhugs nas mkhas
btsun bzang gsum gyi/ /yon tan thob kyang tshe 'di'i che thabs la/ /gcig tu gzhol bas mi tshe stong zad mkhan/ /deng sang chos pa phal gyi rnam thar lags/ /dkon mchog dad

dang dal 'byor rnyed dka' dang / /mi rtag rgyu 'bras chos la yid ches nas/ /theg chen lta spyod zung 'brel nyams len gyis/ /mi tshe skyel rnams bka' gdams bshes gnyen yin/
/mdor na tshul gnas thos bsam sgom pa sogs/ /sgo gsum dge ba che phra ci bgyid kyang / /phyi ma'i don du dmigs nas bsgrub pa la/ /bka' gdams gsung rab 'di rnams ches ngo
mtshar/ /don gyi snying po dril na 'di lta ste/ /phyi ma mi bsam 'dir snang a 'thas kyi/ /mkhas btsun bzang por rlom pa mang na yang / /rang gzhan gnyis phung chos pa'i gzugs
brnyan yin/ /des na sngon byon bka' gdams bshes gnyen gyi/ /rnam thar bzhin du sgo gsum dge ba'i las/ /ci byed 'jig rten phyi ma'i don chen du/ /dmigs nas sgrub 'di
chos kyi srog rtsa lags/ /de ltar rgyal ba gnyis pa a ti sha'i/ /chos brgyud byung tshul ngo mtshar rgya mtsho 'di/ /phyogs 'dir rang nyid mos pa gtsor byas shing / /gzhan
yang bstan dang 'gro la phan phyir sbyar/ /'di brtsams dge bas bdag cag dpon slob rnams/ /jo bo yab sras slob mar bcas pa bzhin/ /nam yang 'bral med bsam don mthar phyin
nas/ /phyi ma lhan cig bde ba can bgrod shog ces dge ba'i bshes gnyen bka' gdams pa rnams kyi dam pa'i chos byung tshul legs par bshad pa ngo mtshar rgya mtsho zhes bya
'di yang / 'jam mgon grub pa'i 'khor lo bsgyur ba bsod nams dbang po'i zhal snga nas dang / yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa'i mtshan can dus gsum sgrib
med du gzigs pa'i

rgyal ba mus pa chen po rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ sprul pa'i sku lo nas spyan snga rin po che kun dga' don grub/ mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos
kyi grags pa la sogs te yongs 'dzin dge ba'i bshes gnyen bslu med kyi bla ma du ma'i zhabs sen rin po che dbang gi rgyal po spyi bo'i cod pan du 'dzin pa'i skal ba bzang
po can dpal sa skya pa shAkya'i dge bsnyen paNDi ta mkhas pa/ sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos bsam pa dag cing sbyor ba
gus pa'i sgo nas chos kyi rje bsod nams lha'i dbang pos mdzad pa'i bka' gdams chos 'byung nyin mor byed pa'i 'od stong zhes bya ba'i gsung rab la gzhi byas/ tshig sbyor
cung zad ma nges pa rnams btang snyoms su byas te/ 'phags pa'i yul na bha wa ra/ zhes pa/ gangs can gyi yul du dngos po zhes grags shing / rgya nag lugs la shing pho khyi'i
lo nag pa zla ba'i dkar phyogs dga' ba gsum pa'i tshes la bod kyi rdo rje gdan dpal ldan sa skya'i chos grwa chen po bzhi thog bla brang gi yang rtse dpe khang gsar pa
chos mdzod chen mor sbyar ba'i yi ge pa ni lugs 'di'i 'du byed la mkhas pa'i phul du phyin pa bsam 'grub kyis legs par bgyis so/ /'di bgyis dge bas bdag cag dpon slob kyi
'di phyi'i don thams cad yid bzhin du grub ste spyi dang bye brag gi bstan pa nam langs pa la nyi ma shar ba lta bu bya nus pa'i mthu dang ldan par gyur cig de de bzhin
du gyur cig de las gzhan du nam yang ma gyur cig /

swa sti dza yantu bkra shis rgyal bar gyur cig sarba mangga laM/thams cad bkra shis//
